id like to better understand my job, please guide me in what documentation i should provide to better inform you on what it is i do, for the most part it seems my job is to monitor a console and follow a tsg (troubleshooting guide) to manage and clear alerts that pop up on that console, when there is an outage that i am alerted to i follow another tsg/sop for spinning up a bridge and facilitating communication channels for that outage, forgive me for i have trouble finding the words so i hope i can explain what im looking for well enough for you to understand. i know how to do my job and i know what i am doing to perform my job my question is more about what is 'what im doing' doing? i mean to say that i understand that as i follow a TSG and input this or that command that it clears the alert and thats me performance my requested action for my position but what is it that that alert actually means? what is it that im SSHing into or what does it do? what is it supposed to do that it wasnt doing that caused the alert? what was it that i did to resolve that alert by clicking what i clicked or executing the command that i executed? im honestly not 100% sure really what Marchex as a company does, i get that we take phone calls that people make to car dealerships and run them thru AI to try to make them into customers from calls but if i want to rise in this company and make myself essential, which i do, i feel like i need to know more of the in the weeds indepth details of what Marchex does and what i do hi do what i do, i hope im making sense in my request.

Megan Gruberman
Feb 18
General
Severity Definitions: Click here for definitions
Escalation Rotation: PagerDutyOnCall 
Description of monitor
This is a high level summary monitor for CXCP hosts running the dropcamel call stack(s).

Warning Alert
Severity: 4
Investigation/Resolution Steps
One-way escalation.
On-Call Notes
If the status is PAUSED, MAINT, or WINDING DOWN: As the on-call, find out who paused it and whether you or they still need the machine paused.
Critical or Unknown Alert
Severity: 3
Investigation/Resolution Steps
If there are many hosts all reporting an issue, Two-way escalation via PagerDuty.
If the alert text is something like NRPE: Unable to read output, run check_health manually and re-start this TSG using the new information:
Connect to the machine:


ssh HOST
Verify status:


sudo /site/dropcamel/version/latest/bin/check_health
echo exit code: $?
It will likely print something like:


OK - 203 channels; 2023_08_11_04_36_23: 46 calls
exit code: 0
Act according to the output text

If in doubt, Two-way escalation
On-Call Notes
In all cases, diagnose why the issue is occurring and then decide how to fix it. In most cases you'll be reporting an issue to an upstream team like Adtrack for CDR Shepherd or CMR and then just waiting for the issue to resolve.

2 visits in last 30 days

README.md
SOCBOT
Contains scripts, utilities, and cron jobs used or managed by the SOC. Nothing in this repo should run persistently as a service - such things should get their own repository in git.

Dependencies
Oracle Client (whack oracle-client) sqlplus
Perl (whack perl)
Python
LDAP Utils (apt-get ldap-utils) ldapsearch
Postgres Client and dev libraries (apt-get postgresql-client) psql libpq-dev
History
This is the succcessor to the '/site/nocbot/' directory which lived on soc[1-4].sea (noc[1-4].sea).

Contributing
Small scripts unworthy of their own directory can be put in 'scripts/'. If a large number of

Larger utilities such as the Shift Report can have their own directory made under the root of the repo, ex: 'ShiftReport/'.

NEVER should any scripts or similar files be placed directly under the root of this repository, ex: '/badScript.pl'.

Accessing Password file (secret.conf)
Bash:

source $SECRET_FILE 2> /dev/null || \
	(echo "Cannot get password file, SOC ENV not loaded. EXITING." && exit 1)
Perl:

eval "use Secret; 1"
	or die "Cannot find Secret.pm module, SOC ENV not loaded. EXITING.";
About
No description, website, or topics provided.

SOC SOP employeeSeparations
SOC SOP employeeSeparations
Jump to navigationJump to search
If person being separated (or transitioned) is a SOC operator, make sure to change the master Bitwarden password. This application is external facing. Send the new password to all existing SOC operators from your personal Marchex account.




Contents
1	Description
1.1	Separation Steps
1.1.1	Check for Tickets to find previous access
1.1.2	Other Manual Checks:
Description


This SOP outlines steps necessary to remove access from a separated employee.
The separation script is designed to check/remove internal users (LDAP/*@marchex.com) permissions.
If a separation ticket includes a non-Marchex email address you will have to check Adtrack manually.
Assign the ticket to the Swing shift operator to run.
Last3 isn't handled by the SOC. When the employee is removed from LDAP by Corp IT they will lose Last3 access
LDAP NISMaps - CORP IT will be handling this as part of their sep SOP as of 3/18/21.


Note about some vendors:
'Microsourcing' and 'Wildnet Technologies' vendors have no AD (active directory) account and therefore no LDAP account either. They are only given an SMTP pointer in the GAL for their external mail address. They may have one-off, non-AD/LDAP-related accesses to things like Adtrack, so those should still be checked during your separation processes.

Separation Steps
1. What type of separation is this?

 First check to see if this ticket says (UPDATE) OR (REVISION) OR (something else that makes you think there may already be a ticket).  
If there is then merge them, or resolve the first one, or take an appropriate action so they aren't both out in the wild.
 Get the User's alias and manager name and put it into the ticket. -- Check [Directory Manager] to check for LDAP alias.  
 If this is NOT an immediate separation, pass the ticket to Kamran with BPO and he will divvy them up to night shift.  
 If this IS an immediate separation, complete the ticket ASAP. 


2. Go to the soc tools UI

3. Click SOC Separation Tool


Check for Tickets to find previous access
Check new hire ticket for user
You may also be able to find tickets with their username/alias in the subject requesting access
Example Ticket Subject... Access Request: Jira for rkumar
If you find any tickets with access that needs to remove by the SOC:
UIs that need to be removed steps can be found here: uiAccess
Database hosts that need to be removed can be found here (just do a "find" to figure out what kind): databaseAccess
Hosts that might need to be removed Hosts Access


Other Manual Checks:
RT Tickets
Go here to Query RT
On the left hand side, you'll see "owner is"
Check the pulldown, if the user isn't there then they don't own any RTs & you are down with the RT checks
If they are in the pulldown
Select their name in the pulldown
On the line above their name select "Status is" and OPEN
click "add these terms and search" below the box

TACACS (tac-plus)
Cut a sev5 ticket to Neteng for the removal

Manually check and remove access from Grafana Grafana
Manually check and remove access from Chef: Chef
Manually check and remove access from Wallace Wallace
Manually check and remove access from XMS Hammer XMS Hammer
Manually check and remove Auth0 access: Auth0
Manually check and remove access to AWS AWS
Manually check and remove access to PagerDuty PagerDuty
Manually check and remove Slack Access: Slack
Manually check and remove Jira: Jira

lets move on to taking a look at some of the python scripts in the socbot-dev/Separations directory starting with adtrack.py




import logging
import pprint
import psycopg2
import sys
import secret

DB_NAME = 'adtrack_ro'
DB_HOST = 'vspool.som1.marchex.com'
DB_PORT = 5432

DB_USER = secret.get_secret('_ADTRACK_DB_USER')
DB_PASS = secret.get_secret('_ADTRACK_DB_PASS')

def main(user, creds):
    marchex = ("SELECT email FROM at_user "
            "WHERE email ILIKE '{username}@marchex%' AND status != 'disabled'").format(username=user)
    vendor = ("SELECT email FROM at_user "
            "WHERE email ILIKE '{email}' AND status != 'disabled'").format(email=creds['vendorEmail'])

    try:
        conn = psycopg2.connect(host=DB_HOST, database=DB_NAME,
                port=DB_PORT, user=DB_USER, password=DB_PASS)
    except Exception as e:
        raise Exception("Could not connect to DB '{}': {}".format(DB_HOST, e))

    cur = conn.cursor()
    if creds['vendorEmail'] == None:
        try:
            cur.execute(marchex)
        except Exception as e:
            raise Exception("DB Query failed in the adtrack.py module: "+str(e))
    else:
        try:
            cur.execute(vendor)
        except Exception as e:
            raise Exception("DB Query failed in the adtrack.py module: "+str(e))

    rows = cur.fetchall()

    # Close DB communication
    cur.close()
    conn.close()

    if rows:
        output = [row[0] for row in rows]
        return(output,user,creds)
    else:
        output = None
        return(output,user,creds)

def foundAccess(result):
    if result[0] is not None:
        accessChoice = result[2]['accessChoice']
        if accessChoice == "check":
            print "{} has Adtrack UI access".format(result[1])
        if accessChoice == "remove":
            print "{} has Adtrack UI access, but automatic removal is not yet available. Please remove manually:".format(result[1])

if __name__ == '__main__':
    vendorEmail=None
    sepList = raw_input("Enter LDAP user to be separated. If multiple, separate by commas: ").split(',')
    accessChoice = raw_input("Would you like to check or remove access? Check/Remove: ").lower()
    isVendor = raw_input("Is this user a vendor? Yes/No: ").lower()

    while isVendor not in ('yes', 'no'):
        isVendor = raw_input("Sorry, looks like you misspelled 'yes' or 'no' somehow. Is this user a vendor? Yes/No: ").lower()

    if isVendor == "yes":
        vendorEmail = raw_input("Enter vendor email address: ")

    while True:
        if accessChoice not in ('remove','check'):
            accessChoice = raw_input("Sorry, looks like you misspelled 'remove' or 'check'. Please re-indicate if you'd like to remove all access or just check access. Remove/Check: ").lower()
            continue
        else:
            accessChoice = accessChoice
            break

    inputDict = {}
    inputDict.update({'creds' : {'accessChoice' : accessChoice,'vendorEmail':vendorEmail}})
    creds = inputDict['creds']

    for user in sepList:
        result = main(user, creds)
        foundAccess(result)




and avenger.py

import logging
import pprint
import MySQLdb
import sys
import secret

## Config
DB_HOST = 'elpagedb-master.marchex.com'
DB_USER = secret.get_secret('_PROD_MYSQL_USER')
DB_PASS = secret.get_secret('_PROD_MYSQL_PASS')

## SQL queries
SQL_COMMANDS = {
    # checks if user exists and is active
    "check_for_user": "SELECT username, firstname, lastname FROM avenger.user WHERE username = '{username}' AND is_active = 1",

    # removes user role
    "remove": "delete from avenger.user_role where user_id = (select user_id from avenger.user where username = '{username}');",

    # sets user to inactive
    "deactivate": "UPDATE avenger.user set is_active = 0 WHERE username = '{username}';",
}

def command_from_username(command, username):
    return SQL_COMMANDS[command].format(username=username)

def execute_mysql_command(db, query):
    """Helper function to execute queries in try block."""
    try:
        cur = db.cursor()
        cur.execute(query)
        return cur.fetchall()
    except Exception as e:
        raise Exception("Error executing query in avenger.py module: {}\n{}".format(query, str(e)))
    finally:
        cur.close()

def main(user, creds):
    output = None
    username = user
    # Attempt to connect to DB
    try:
        db = MySQLdb.connect(host=DB_HOST, user=DB_USER, passwd=DB_PASS)
    except Exception as e:
        db.close()
        raise Exception("Could not connect to DB in avenger.py module '{}': {}".format(DB_HOST, str(e)))

    # Check for user
    try:
        query_output = execute_mysql_command(db, command_from_username('check_for_user', username))
        if query_output:
            output = ['{} ({} {})'.format(row[0], row[1], row[2]) for row in query_output]
            return(output, username, creds)
        else:
            output = None
            return(output, username, creds)
    except Exception as e:
        raise Exception("DB Query failed in avenger.py module: " + str(e))
    finally:
        db.close()

# Access/no access logic
def foundAccess(result):
    if result[0] is not None:
        accessChoice = result[2]['accessChoice']
        if accessChoice == 'remove':
            deactivation(result)
        if accessChoice == 'check':
            print "{} has Avenger UI access".format(result[1])

# deactivation
def deactivation(result):

    username = result[1]

    # connect to the DB
    try:
        db = MySQLdb.connect(host=DB_HOST, user=DB_USER, passwd=DB_PASS)
    except Exception as e:
        db.close()
        raise Exception("Could not connect to DB in avenger.py module '{}': {}".format(DB_HOST, str(e)))

    # deactivate user
    try:
        # remove user role
        execute_mysql_command(db, command_from_username('remove', username))
        # deactivate user
        execute_mysql_command(db, command_from_username('deactivate', username))
        # if we made it this far, success!
    except Exception as e:
        raise Exception("DB command failed in avenger.py module: "+str(e))
        db.rollback()
    else:
        db.commit()

    # recheck for user
    try:
        query_output = execute_mysql_command(db, command_from_username('check_for_user', username))
        if query_output:
            print "Something went wrong and {}'s account was not deactivated. Please remove AvengerUI access manually".format(result[1])
        else:
            print "Avenger UI Access Removed for {}".format(result[1])
    finally:
        db.close()

if __name__ == '__main__':
    print "Checking Avenger UI access"
    user = raw_input("Input username to check. If multiple, separate by commas: ").split(',')
    accessChoice = raw_input("Would you like to check or remove access? Check/Remove: ").lower()

    while True:
      if accessChoice not in ('remove','check'):
         accessChoice = raw_input("Sorry, looks like you misspelled 'remove' or 'check'. Please re-indicate if you'd like to remove all access or just check access. Remove/Check: ").lower()
         continue
      else:
         accessChoice = accessChoice
         break

    inputDict = {}
    inputDict.update({'creds' : {'accessChoice' : accessChoice}})
    creds = inputDict['creds']

    for u in user:
        result = main(u, creds)
        foundAccess(result)




aws.py

import logging
import subprocess
import json

# DOCUMENTATION:
# http://docs.aws.amazon.com/cli/latest/userguide/cli-chap-getting-set-up.html#cli-signup
# http://docs.aws.amazon.com/AWSEC2/latest/CommandLineReference/ec2-cli-managing-certs.html

# Script requires aws command (Python awscli module)
# sudo pip install awscli

# Command is: aws iam list-users

# Setup:
# cd ~/.ssh
# openssl genrsa 2048 > aws_iam.pem
# openssl req -new -x509 -nodes -sha256 -key aws_iam.pem aws_iam.pem > aws_iam_user_signing.pem
# Go to:
#   https://console.aws.amazon.com/iam/home
# Select your user, click the "Security Credentials" tab, and upload the "Signing Certificate" you generated
# Back to the URL above, go to the same place and click "Create Acess Key"
# Copy the info provided ("Access Key ID", "Security Access Key"), store it somewhere
# You will need it in the next steps

# THEN:
# aws configure
# Provide the Access Key and Security Access Key you got just before.
# Run the command aws iam list-users to test

def main(user, creds):
    check_user = user
    auth_user = creds['operatorUN']

    return_code = subprocess.call(['aws'], stdout=subprocess.PIPE, stderr=subprocess.PIPE)
    if not return_code == 2:
	raise Exception('aws cli tools do not seem to be installed. Check the marchex_aws.py script for instructions on setup.')
    try:
	output = subprocess.check_output(['aws','iam','list-users','--profile',auth_user], stderr=subprocess.STDOUT)
    except subprocess.CalledProcessError as e:
	if 'The config profile' in e.output:
	    raise Exception(('AWS CLI profile not set up. First run aws configure --profile {}'
		'\n\tSee marchex_aws.py for detailed instructions.').format(auth_user))
	else:
	    raise Exception('Command aws iam list-users failed: {}'.format(e.output.strip()))


    if user in output:
        account=user
    else:
        account=None

    return(account,user,creds)

def foundAccess(result):
    if result[0] is not None:
        accessChoice = result[2]['accessChoice']
        if accessChoice == 'check':
	    print "{} has AWS access".format(result[1])
        if accessChoice == "remove":
            deleteAccess(result)

def deleteAccess(result):
    user = result[1]
    auth_user = result[2]['operatorUN']
    try:
        deleted = subprocess.check_output(['aws','iam','delete-user','--profile',auth_user,'--user-name',user],stderr=subprocess.STDOUT)
    except subprocess.CalledProcessError as e:
        raise Exception('Command aws iam delete-user has failed: {}\nPlease remove {} access manually'.format(e,user))

    try:
        output= subprocess.check_output(['aws','iam','list-users','--profile',auth_user], stderr=subprocess.STDOUT)
    except Exception as e:
        print("User {} AWS access was not deleted successfully. Please manually remove it\nError:{}".format(user,e))

    if user not in output:
        print("AWS access for {} was successfully removed".format(user))

if __name__ == '__main__':
    import getpass

    operatorUN = raw_input("Input your LDAP username: ")
    user = raw_input('Input user to check. If multiple, separate by commas: ').split(',')
    accessChoice = raw_input("Would you like to check or remove access? Check/Remove: ").lower()

    while True:
        if accessChoice not in ('remove','check'):
            accessChoice = raw_input("Sorry, looks like you misspelled 'remove' or 'check'. Please re-indicate if you'd like to remove all access or just check access.           Remove/Check: ").lower()
            continue
        else:
            accessChoice = accessChoice
            break

    inputDict = {}
    inputDict.update({'creds': {'operatorUN' : operatorUN, 'accessChoice' : accessChoice}})
    creds = inputDict['creds']

    for u in user:
        result = main(u, creds)
        foundAccess(result)




grafana.py

import requests
import getpass

def main(user, creds):

    operatorUN = creds['operatorUN']
    operatorPass = creds['operatorPass']

    with requests.Session() as s:
        url = 'http://grafana.marchex.com/login'
        values = {'user': operatorUN, 'password': operatorPass}

        # login
        p = s.post(url, data=values)

        # get list of users with Grafana access
        try:
            r = s.get('http://grafana.marchex.com/org/users')
        except Exception as e:
            print("Failed to get grafana user access for {}\nError: {}".format(user,e))

        # check Grafana output
        output = r.content
        my_string = user

        if my_string in output:
            Grafana_status = my_string
        else:
            Grafana_status = None

        return(Grafana_status, user, creds)

# report back if user found or not
def foundAccess(result):
    if result[0] is not None:
        accessChoice = result[2]['accessChoice']
        if accessChoice == 'check':
            print "{} has Grafana access".format(result[1])
        if accessChoice == 'remove':
            print "{} has Grafana access, but automatic removal is not yet available. Please remove manually.".format(result[1])
    else:
        return

if __name__ == '__main__':

    operatorUN = raw_input('Input your username, to authenticate to Grafana: ')
    operatorPass = getpass.getpass('Input your password: ')
    sepList = raw_input("Enter LDAP user to be separated. If multiple, separate by commas: ").split(',')
    accessChoice = raw_input("Would you like to check or remove access? Check/Remove: ").lower()

    # Make sure the user spells the choice right
    while True:
        if accessChoice not in ('remove', 'check'):
            accessChoice = raw_input("Sorry, looks like you misspelled 'remove' or 'check'. Please re-indicate if you'd"
                                     "like to remove all access or just check access. Check/Remove ").lower()
        else:
            accessChoice = accessChoice
            break

    inputDict = {}
    inputDict.update({'creds': {'operatorUN': operatorUN, 'operatorPass': operatorPass, 'accessChoice': accessChoice}})
    creds = inputDict['creds']

    for user in sepList:
        result = main(user, creds)
        foundAccess(result)

        # login to IP Plan & check for user

        output = r.content

#jingleaccess.py

import requests
import urllib2
import mechanize
import getpass
import cookielib
import utils
import re
import secret
from bs4 import BeautifulSoup

# CONFIG
URL = "https://intranet.free411.com/users/index.php"
LOGIN_URL = "https://intranet.free411.com/login.php"
AUTH_USER = secret.get_secret('_JINGLE_UI_USER')
AUTH_PASS = secret.get_secret('_JINGLE_UI_PASS')

def main(user, creds):
    check_user = user
    """Check for user and get deactivation link."""
    # initialize mechanize
    br = mechanize.Browser()
    cj = cookielib.LWPCookieJar()
    br.set_cookiejar(cj)

    # open URL and submit
    br.open(LOGIN_URL)
    br.select_form(nr=0)
    br.form['email_address'] = AUTH_USER
    br.form['password'] = AUTH_PASS
    br.submit()

    # scrape
    response = br.open(URL)
    soup = BeautifulSoup(response, "html.parser")
    div = soup.find("div", {"id": "content"})
    trs = div.findAll('tr')
    link = None
    for tr in trs:
        tds = tr.findAll('td')
        if tds:
            username = tds[0].contents[0].strip().split('@')[0]
            if username == check_user:
                link = tds[3].contents[3]['href']
                return(link, br, user, creds)
    return(link, br, user, creds)


def foundAccess(result):
    """States if user has access. Asks if you want to remove access."""
    if result[0] is not None:
        accessChoice = result[3]['accessChoice']
        if accessChoice == "remove":
            # print "Automatic removal is broke due to a DNS issue. Please remove access manually"
            deactivation(result)
        if accessChoice == "check":
            print "User has JingleCSI Access"


def deactivation(result):
    link = result[0]
    br = result[1]
    check_user = result[2]
    """Removes user access."""
    # deactivate
    response2 = br.open(link)
    soup2 = BeautifulSoup(response2, "html.parser")
    br.select_form(nr=0)
    br.submit()

    # check that user is deactivated
    response = br.open(URL)
    soup = BeautifulSoup(response, "html.parser")
    div = soup.find("div", {"id": "content"})
    trs = div.findAll('tr')
    for tr in trs:
        tds = tr.findAll('td')
        if tds:
            username = tds[0].contents[0].strip().split('@')[0]
    if username == check_user:
        print "Something went wrong and user was not deactivated. Please remove JingleCSI access manually"
    else:
        print "Deactivated JingleCSI Account"


if __name__ == '__main__':
    print "Checking JingleCSI Access"
    sepList = raw_input("Enter LDAP user to be separated. If multiple, separate by commas: ").split(',')
    accessChoice = raw_input("Would you like to check or remove access? Check/remove: ").lower()

    while True:
        if accessChoice not in ('remove', 'check'):
            accessChoice = raw_input("Sorry, looks like you misspelled 'remove' or 'check'. Please re-indicate if "
                                     "you'd like to remove all access or just check access. Remove/Check: ").lower()
            continue
        else:
            accessChoice = accessChoice
            break
    inputDict = {}
    inputDict.update({'creds': {'accessChoice': accessChoice}})
    creds = inputDict['creds']

    for user in sepList:
        result = main(user, creds)
        foundAccess(result)




#jira

import logging
import sys
import urllib2, base64
import json

# Jira API Documentation:
# https://docs.atlassian.com/jira/REST/latest/#api/2/user

URL = "https://jira.marchex.com/rest/api/latest/user?username="

def main(user, creds):
    user = user
    username = creds['operatorUN']
    password = creds['operatorPass']

    request = urllib2.Request(URL + user)

    base64_authstring = base64.encodestring('{}:{}'.format(
        username, password)).replace('\n','')

    request.add_header("Authorization", "Basic " + base64_authstring)
    try:
        response = urllib2.urlopen(request)
    except urllib2.HTTPError as error:
        response = error

    raw_data = response.read()

    try:
        data = json.loads(raw_data)
    except:
        raise Exception("Could not parse response from Jira API")

    if 'errorMessages' in data:
        for error in data['errorMessages']:
            if error.find('does not exist'):
                output=None
    if 'name' in data:
        if data['active'] == True:
            output = "{} ({})".format(data['name'], data['displayName'])
        elif data['active'] == False:
            output = None
        else:
            logging.error("Cannot determine Jira user state. Check UI manually")

    return(output, user, creds)

def foundAccess(result):
    if result[0] is not None:
        accessChoice = result[2]['accessChoice']
        if accessChoice == 'check':
            print "{} has Jira access".format(result[1])
        if accessChoice == 'remove':
            print "{} has Jira access but automatic removal is not yet available. Please remove manually".format(result[1])

if __name__ == '__main__':
    import getpass

    operatorUN = raw_input('Input your username, to authenticate to Jira: ')
    operatorPass = getpass.getpass('Input your password: ')
    sepList = raw_input("Enter LDAP user to be separated. If multiple, separate by commas: ").split(',')
    accessChoice = raw_input("Would you like to check or remove access? Check/Remove: ").lower()

    while True:
        if accessChoice not in ('remove','check'):
            accessChoice = raw_input("Sorry, looks like you misspelled 'remove' or 'check'. Please re-indicate if you'd like to remove all access or just check access. Remove/Check: ").lower()
            continue
        else:
            accessChoice = accessChoice
            break

    inputDict = {}
    inputDict.update({'creds' : {'operatorUN': operatorUN, 'operatorPass': operatorPass, 'accessChoice' : accessChoice}})
    creds = inputDict['creds']

    for user in sepList:
        result = main(user, creds)
        foundAccess(result)




#last3.py

import requests
import getpass
import subprocess
import os

def main(user, creds):

    uid = {'user_id':user}

    with requests.Session() as s:
        url = 'https://last3.marchex.com:443/last3/login/check'
        values = {'username': creds['operatorUN'], 'password': creds['operatorPass']}

        # login
        p = s.post(url, data=values)

        # send user name to site to check
        r = s.get('https://last3.marchex.com/last3/user/search', data=uid)

        # check last3 output
        output = r.content
        my_string = ("https://last3.marchex.com:443/last3/user/view?user_id={}".format(user))

        if my_string in output:
            last3_status = "Y"
        else:
            last3_status = None

        return(last3_status, user, creds)

# report back if user found
def foundAccess(result):
    if result[0] is not None:
        accessChoice = result[2]['accessChoice']
        if accessChoice == 'check':
            print "{} has last3 access".format(result[1])
            getLast3Access(result[1])
        if accessChoice == 'remove':
            print "{} has last3 access, but Corp takes care of removal. There's no need to remove anything".format(result[1])

def getLast3Access(user):
    bashCommand = "ldapsearch -x -LLL -H ldaps://directory.sea.marchex.com -b 'ou=security,dc=marchex,dc=com' '(member=cn='{}',ou=users,dc=marchex,dc=com)' dn".format(user)
    output = os.system(bashCommand)

if __name__ == '__main__':

    operatorUN = raw_input('Input your username, to authenticate to last3: ')
    operatorPass = getpass.getpass('Input your password: ')
    sepList = raw_input("Enter LDAP user to be separated. If multiple, separate by commas: ").split(',')
    accessChoice = raw_input("Would you like to check or remove access? Check/Remove: ").lower()

    # Make sure the user spells the choice right
    while True:
        if accessChoice not in ('remove', 'check'):
            accessChoice = raw_input("Sorry, looks like you misspelled 'remove' or 'check'. Please re-indicate if you'd"
                                     "like to remove all access or just check access. Check/Remove: ").lower()
        else:
            accessChoice = accessChoice
            break

    inputDict = {}
    inputDict.update({'creds': {'operatorUN': operatorUN, 'operatorPass': operatorPass, 'accessChoice': accessChoice}})
    creds = inputDict['creds']

    for user in sepList:
        result = main(user, creds)
        foundAccess(result)





#mi5.py

import requests

    operatorPass = creds['operatorPass']

    with requests.Session() as s:
        url = 'https://mchxauth.marchex.com/users/sign_in'
        values = {'login_user[email]': (operatorUN + '@marchex.com'), 'login_user[password]': operatorPass}

        # login
        p = s.post(url, data=values)

        # get list of users with MI5 access
        r = s.get('https://mchxism.marchex.com/users')

        # check MI5 output
        output = r.content
        my_string = (user)

        if my_string in output:
            mi5_status = my_string
        else:
            mi5_status = None

        return(mi5_status, user, creds)

# report back if user found or not
def foundAccess(result):
    if result[0] is not None:
        accessChoice = result[2]['accessChoice']
        if accessChoice == 'check':
            print "User has MI5 access"
        if accessChoice == 'remove':
            print "User has MI5 access, but automatic removal is not yet available. Please remove manually."
    else:
        return

if __name__ == '__main__':

    operatorUN = raw_input('Input your username, to authenticate to MI5: ')
    operatorPass = getpass.getpass('Input your password: ')
    sepList = raw_input("Enter LDAP user to be separated. If multiple, separate by commas: ").split(',')
    accessChoice = raw_input("Would you like to check or remove access? Check/Remove: ").lower()

    # Make sure the user spells the choice right
    while True:
        if accessChoice not in ('remove', 'check'):
            accessChoice = raw_input("Sorry, looks like you misspelled 'remove' or 'check'. Please re-indicate if you'd"
                                     "like to remove all access or just check access. Check/Remove ").lower()
        else:
            accessChoice = accessChoice
            break

    inputDict = {}
    inputDict.update({'creds': {'operatorUN': operatorUN, 'operatorPass': operatorPass, 'accessChoice': accessChoice}})
    creds = inputDict['creds']

    for user in sepList:
        result = main(user, creds)
        foundAccess(result)




#microsite.py

import logging
import pprint
import MySQLdb
import sys
import secret
DB_HOST = 'bppdb-master.marchex.com'
DB_USER = secret.get_secret('_PROD_MYSQL_USER')
DB_PASS = secret.get_secret('_PROD_MYSQL_PASS')
SQL_COMMANDS = {
    "check_for_user" : "SELECT name, email, status FROM microsite.users WHERE status NOT LIKE 'inactive' AND (email LIKE '%{username}%' OR name LIKE '%{username}%')",
    "deactivate" : "UPDATE microsite.users set status = 'inactive' where email = '{username}@marchex.com';",
    "deactivate_vendor" : "UPDATE microsite.users set status = 'inactive' where email = '{username}';"
}
def command_from_username(command, username):
    return SQL_COMMANDS[command].format(username=username)
def execute_mysql_command(db, query):
    try:
        cur = db.cursor()
        cur.execute(query)
        return cur.fetchall()
    except Exception as e:
        raise Exception("Error executing query in the microsites.py module: {}\n{}".format(query, str(e)))
    finally:
        cur.close()
def main(user, creds):
    output = None
    # Checks for vendor email. Proceeds as normal if value is None
    if creds['vendorEmail'] == None:
        username = user
    else:
        username = creds['vendorEmail']
    #connect to db
    try:
        db = MySQLdb.connect(host=DB_HOST, user=DB_USER, passwd=DB_PASS)
    except Exception as e:
        raise Exception("Could not connect to DB '{}' in the microsites.py module: {}".format(DB_HOST, str(e)))
    #check for user
    try:
        query_output = execute_mysql_command(db, command_from_username('check_for_user', username))
        if query_output:
            output = ['{} ({} status:{})'.format(row[0], row[1], row[2]) for row in query_output]
            return(output, username, creds)
        else:
            output=None
            return(output, username, creds)
    except Exception as e:
        raise Exception("DB Query failed: "+str(e))
#Printing logic for access/no access; continues to deactivate if desired
def foundAccess(result):
    if result[0] is not None:
        accessCheck = result[2]['accessChoice']
        if accessCheck == "check":
            print "{} has Microsite UI access".format(result[1])
        if accessCheck == "remove":
            deactivation(result)
#deactivation
def deactivation(result):
    username = result[1]
    #connect to db
    try:
        db = MySQLdb.connect(host=DB_HOST, user=DB_USER, passwd=DB_PASS)
    except Exception as e:
        raise Exception("Could not connect to DB '{}' for microsites removal for user {}: {}".format(DB_HOST,username, str(e)))
    #deactivate
    if result[2['vendorEmail']] == None:
        try:
            query_output = execute_mysql_command(db, command_from_username('deactivate',username))
        except Exception as e:
            raise Exception("DB command failed deactivating microsites access for {}\nError: : ".format(username,str(e)))
            db.rollback()
        else:
            db. commit()
    else:
        try:
            query_output = execute_mysql_command(db, command_from_username('deactivate_vendor',username))
        except Exception as e:
            raise Exception("DB command failed in microsites.py module: {} ".format(str(e)))
            db.rollback()
        else:
            db. commit()
    #recheck for user
    try:
        query_output = execute_mysql_command(db, command_from_username('check_for_user', username))
        if query_output:
            print "Something went wrong and {} was not deactivated. Please remove MicrositeUI access manually".format(username)
        else:
            print "Microsite Account Deactivated for {}".format(username)
    finally:
        db.close()
if __name__ == '__main__':
    print "Checking Microsite UI access"
    vendorEmail=None
    user = raw_input("Input username to check. If multiple, separate by commas: ").split(',')
    accessChoice = raw_input("Would you like to check or remove access? Check/Remove: ").lower()
    isVendor = raw_input("Is this user a vendor? Yes/No: ").lower()

    while isVendor not in ('yes', 'no'):
        isVendor = raw_input("Sorry, looks like you misspelled 'yes' or 'no' somehow. Is this user a vendor? Yes/No: ").lower()

    if isVendor == "yes":
        vendorEmail = raw_input("Enter vendor email address: ")

    while True:
        if accessChoice not in ('remove','check'):
            accessChoice = raw_input("Sorry, looks like you misspelled 'remove' or 'check'. Please re-indicate if you'd like to remove all access or just check access. Remove/Check: ").lower()
            continue
        else:
            accessChoice = accessChoice
            break
    inputDict = {}
    inputDict.update({'creds' : {'accessChoice' : accessChoice,'vendorEmail':vendorEmail}})
    creds = inputDict['creds']
    for u in user:
        result = main(u, creds)
        foundAccess(result)




#mysql_db.py

import logging
import pprint
import MySQLdb
import sys
import secret
sys.path.insert(1,'/site/socbot/scripts')
import dbaHostHelper

DB_HOSTS = dbaHostHelper.get_mysql_hosts() 

DB_USER = secret.get_secret('_PROD_MYSQL_USER')
DB_PASS = secret.get_secret('_PROD_MYSQL_PASS')

SQL_COMMANDS = {
    "findUser": "SELECT user FROM mysql.user WHERE user LIKE '%{username}';",
    "dropUser": "drop user {username};",
    "flush": "flush privileges;",
}

def command_from_username(command,user):
    return SQL_COMMANDS[command].format(username=user)

def execute_mysql_command(db, query):
    try:
        cur = db.cursor()
        cur.execute(query)
        output = cur.fetchall()
        return output
    except Exception as e:
        raise Exception("Error executing query in the mysql module: {}\n{}".format(query, str(e)))
    finally:
        cur.close()

def main(username,creds):
    output = None
    hostlist=[]
    del hostlist[:]
    for host in DB_HOSTS:
        try:
            db = MySQLdb.connect(host=host, user=DB_USER, passwd=DB_PASS)
        except Exception as e:
            logging.error("Could not connect to DB '{}' in the mysql module: {}".format(host, str(e)))
            continue
        try:
            query_output = execute_mysql_command(db, command_from_username('findUser', username))
        except Exception as e:
            logging.error("DB Query failed while checking for mysql_db access: "+str(e))
        finally:
            db.close()
        if query_output:
            hostlist.append(host)

    if len(hostlist) == 0:
        return(None, username, creds)
    else:
        return(hostlist,username,creds)
def foundAccess(result):
    accessChoice = result[2]['accessChoice']
    if result[0] is not None:
        if accessChoice == 'check':
            for host in result[0]:
                print "{} has account on {}".format(result[1],host)
        if accessChoice == 'remove':
            deactivation(result[0],result[1])

def deactivation(hostlist,username):

    for host in hostlist:
        try:
            db = MySQLdb.connect(host=host, user=DB_USER, passwd=DB_PASS)
        except Exception as e:
            logging.error("The following happened when connecting to {} in the mysql module: {}".format(host,str(e)))
            continue
        try:
            cont = raw_input("{} will be removed from  {}\nContinue (y/n)? (If no, changes will be rolled back): ".format(username,host))
            if cont == 'n':
                print("{} will NOT be removed from {}".format(username,host))
                continue
            else:
                if not execute_mysql_command(db, command_from_username('findUser', username)):
                    print("{} was already removed from {}".format(username,host))
                    continue
                execute_mysql_command(db, command_from_username('dropUser', username))
                execute_mysql_command(db, command_from_username('flush',username))
        except Exception as e:
            raise Exception("DB command failed while attempting to remove {} in the mysql module\nError: {}".format(username,str(e)))
            db.rollback()
        try:
            if not execute_mysql_command(db, command_from_username('findUser', username)):
                print "{} deactivated from {}".format(username,host)
            else:
                print("Something went wrong and {} was not deactivated. Please remove {} access manually".format(username,host))
        except Exception as e:
            logging.error("The following error occurred while attempting to deactivate {} on {}\nError: {}".format(username, host,e))

if __name__ == '__main__':
    user = raw_input("Input username to check: ")
    accessChoice = raw_input("Would you like to check or remove access? Check/Remove: ").lower()

    while True:
        if accessChoice not in ('remove','check'):
            accessChoice = raw_input("Sorry, looks like you misspelled 'remove' or 'check'. Please re-indicate if you'd like to remove all access or just check access. Remove/Check: ").lower()
            continue
        else:
            accessChoice = accessChoice
            break

    inputDict = {}
    inputDict.update({'creds' : {'accessChoice' : accessChoice}})
    creds = inputDict['creds']

    result = main(user,creds)
    foundAccess(result)




#nimui.py

import logging
import os
import subprocess
import secret

DB_INSTANCES = ["OPNEXT",]

DB_USER = secret.get_secret('_ORACLE_USER')
DB_PASS = secret.get_secret('_ORACLE_PASS')

ENV = {
    'TNS_ADMIN': os.environ.get('TNS_ADMIN', '/site/socbot/.oracle'),
    'CLASSPATH': os.environ.get('CLASSPATH', '/site/oracle_client/client-10.2.0.3/jdbc/llib/classes12.jar'),
    'ORACLE_HOME': os.environ.get('ORACLE_HOME', '/site/oracle_client/client-10.2.0.3/'),
    'SQLPATH': os.environ.get('SQLPATH', '/site/socbot/.oracle'),
    'PATH': os.environ['PATH'] + ':/site/oracle_client/client-10.2.0.3/bin',
}

# Verifies that tnsnames.ora file exists
TNSNAMES = ENV['TNS_ADMIN']+'/tnsnames.ora'
if not os.path.isfile(TNSNAMES):
    raise Exception("No tnsnames found (Missing '{}')".format(TNSNAMES))

def main(username,creds):

    for instance in DB_INSTANCES:
        proc = subprocess.Popen(['sqlplus','-s'],
            stdin=subprocess.PIPE,
            stdout=subprocess.PIPE,
            stderr=subprocess.PIPE,
            env=ENV)
        try:
            (stdout, stderr) = proc.communicate(input=("{user}/{passw}@{instance}\n"
                "set pages 200\n"
                "set lines 200\n"
                "set serveroutput on\n"
                "set feedback off\n"
                "SELECT ID, USERNAME, EMAIL, STATUS FROM COMMON.USERS WHERE USERNAME ='{username}';\n"
                ).format(
                    user=DB_USER,
                    passw=DB_PASS,
                    instance=instance,
                    username=username))
        except Exception as e:
            print("Failed to check and connect to opnext in nimui.py module for user {}\nError: {}".format(username,e))

        return(instance, stdout, username, creds)

def foundAccess(result):
    r = result
    if len(r[1]) > 1:
        accessChoice = r[3]['accessChoice']
        if accessChoice == "check":
            print "{} has nimUI access".format(result[2])
        if accessChoice == "remove":
            print "{} has nimUI access, but automatic removal not yet available for this check, please remove manually".format(result[2])

if __name__ == '__main__':
    sepList = raw_input("Enter LDAP user to be separated. If multiple, separate by commas: ").split(',')
    accessChoice = raw_input("Would you like to check or remove access? Check/Remove: ").lower()

    while True:
        if accessChoice not in ('remove','check'):
            accessChoice = raw_input("Sorry, looks like you misspelled 'remove' or 'check'. Please re-indicate if you'd like to remove all access or just check access. Remove/Check: ").lower()
            continue
        else:
            accessChoice = accessChoice
            break

    inputDict = {}
    inputDict.update({'creds' : {'accessChoice' : accessChoice}})
    creds = inputDict['creds']

    for user in sepList:
        result = main(user,creds)
        foundAccess(result)




#nismaps.py

import logging
import pprint
import sys
import smtplib
import ldap

# Local modules
import utils

LDAP_ADDR = 'ldap.sea.marchex.com'
LDAP_BASEDN = 'ou=auto.home,ou=nismaps,dc=marchex,dc=com'
LDAP_SEARCH_FILTER = '(cn={username})'

SMTP_SERVER = 'smtp.marchex.com'
EMAIL_FROM = 'soc@marchex.com'
EMAIL_TO = 'helpdesk@marchex.com'
EMAIL_SUBJECT = 'NISMap Removal - {username}'

def main(user, creds):
    username = user

    try:
        ldp = ldap.open(LDAP_ADDR)
    except ldap.LDAPError as e:
        raise Exception("Couldn't connect to '{}': {}".format(LDAP_ADDR, str(e)))

    result_id = ldp.search(LDAP_BASEDN, ldap.SCOPE_SUBTREE,
        LDAP_SEARCH_FILTER.format(username=username))

    result_set=[]
    while True:
        result_type, result_data = ldp.result(result_id, 0)
        if (result_data == []):
            break
        else:
            result_set.append(result_data)

    if not len(result_set):
        output = None
        return(output,user,creds)
    else:
        output=result_set[0][0]
        return(output, user, creds)

def foundAccess(result):
    accessChoice = result[2]['accessChoice']

    if result[0] is not None:
        if accessChoice == 'check':
            print "LDAP nismaps found for {}".format(result[1])
        if accessChoice == 'remove':
            mail(result)

def mail(result):
    username = result[1]
    details = result[0]
    mailer = smtplib.SMTP(SMTP_SERVER)
    message = ("From: {efrom}\n"
                "To: {to}\n"
                "Subject: {subject}\n"
                "\n"
                "Please remove the following NISMap entry for user '{user}':\n\n"
                "{nismap_info}").format(
                        efrom=EMAIL_FROM,
                        to=EMAIL_TO,
                        subject=EMAIL_SUBJECT.format(username=username),
                        user=username,
                        nismap_info=details)
    mailer.sendmail(EMAIL_FROM, [EMAIL_TO], message)
    print "NISMap information has been sent successfully via email and an unowned ticket has been created."

if __name__ == '__main__':
    print "Checking LDAP nismaps"
    sepList = raw_input("Enter LDAP user to be separated. If multiple, separate by commas: ").split(',')
    accessChoice = raw_input("Would you like to check or remove access? Check/Remove: ").lower()

    while True:
        if accessChoice not in ('remove','check'):
            accessChoice = raw_input("Sorry, looks like you misspelled 'remove' or 'check'. Please re-indicate if you'd like to remove all access or just check access.           Remove/Check: ").lower()
            continue
        else:
            accessChoice = accessChoice
            break

    inputDict = {}
    inputDict.update({'creds' : {'accessChoice' : accessChoice}})
    creds = inputDict['creds']

    for user in sepList:
        result = main(user, creds)
        foundAccess(result)




#oracle_db.py

import logging
import os
import subprocess
import sys
import secret
sys.path.insert(1,'/site/socbot/scripts')
import dbaHostHelper

DB_INSTANCES = dbaHostHelper.get_oracl_hosts()

DB_USER = secret.get_secret('_ORACLE_USER')
DB_PASS = secret.get_secret('_ORACLE_PASS')

ENV = {
	'TNS_ADMIN': os.environ.get('TNS_ADMIN', '/site/socbot/.oracle'),
	'CLASSPATH': os.environ.get('CLASSPATH', '/site/oracle_client/client-10.2.0.3/jdbc/llib/classes12.jar'),
	'ORACLE_HOME': os.environ.get('ORACLE_HOME', '/site/oracle_client/client-10.2.0.3/'),
	'SQLPATH': os.environ.get('SQLPATH', '/site/socbot/.oracle'),
	'PATH': os.environ['PATH'] + ':/site/oracle_client/client-10.2.0.3/bin',
}

# Verifies that tnsnames.ora file exists
TNSNAMES = ENV['TNS_ADMIN']+'/tnsnames.ora'
if not os.path.isfile(TNSNAMES):
    raise Exception("No tnsnames found (Missing '{}')".format(TNSNAMES))

def main(username,creds):
    for instance in DB_INSTANCES:
        proc = subprocess.Popen(['sqlplus','-s'],
            stdin=subprocess.PIPE,
            stdout=subprocess.PIPE,
            stderr=subprocess.PIPE,
            env=ENV)
        (stdout, stderr) = proc.communicate(input=("{user}/{passw}@{instance}\n"
            "set pages 200\n"
            "set lines 200\n"
            "set serveroutput on\n"
            "set feedback off\n"
            "exec USRADM.QUERY_USER('{username}');\n"
            ).format(
                user=DB_USER,
                passw=DB_PASS,
                instance=instance,
                username=username))

        if stderr:
            logging.error("Error in command on database {}: {}".format(instance, stderr))
            if stdout:
                logging.warn("Stdout was: " + str(stdout))
        if not stdout:
            logging.error("Error in command on database {}: no output to STDOUT".format(instance))
        if 'not found' in stdout:
            yield [instance, None, username, creds]
        else:
            yield [instance, stdout, username, creds]

def foundAccess(result):
    for r in result:
        if r[1] is not None:
            accessChoice = r[3]['accessChoice']
            if accessChoice == "check":
                print "User has '{}' access".format(r[0])
            if accessChoice == "remove":
                print " User has '{}' access, but automatic removal not yet available for this check, please remove manually".format(r[0])

if __name__ == '__main__':
    sepList = raw_input("Enter LDAP user to be separated. If multiple, separate by commas: ").split(',')
    accessChoice = raw_input("Would you like to check or remove access? Check/Remove: ").lower()

    while True:
        if accessChoice not in ('remove','check'):
            accessChoice = raw_input("Sorry, looks like you misspelled 'remove' or 'check'. Please re-indicate if you'd like to remove all access or just check access. Remove/Check: ").lower()
            continue
        else:
            accessChoice = accessChoice
            break



    inputDict = {}
    inputDict.update({'creds' : {'accessChoice' : accessChoice}})
    creds = inputDict['creds']

    for user in sepList:
        result = main(user,creds)
        foundAccess(result)




#pagerduty.py

import logging
import sys
import urllib2
import urllib
import json
import pprint
import secret

# PagerDuty Documentation:
# https://developer.pagerduty.com/documentation/rest/users/list

# v2 api key & URL
API_KEY = secret.get_secret("_PAGERDUTY_API_KEY")
URL = "https://api.pagerduty.com/users"

def main(user, creds):
    if creds['vendorEmail'] is not None:
        r = creds['vendorEmail'].split('@')
        username=r[0]
    else:
        username = user

    params = urllib.urlencode({'query': username})
    request = urllib2.Request(URL + '?' + params)
    request.add_header("Authorization", "Token token=" + API_KEY)
    request.add_header("Accept", "application/vnd.pagerduty+json;version=2")

    try:
        response = urllib2.urlopen(request)
    except urllib2.HTTPError as error:
        response = error

    raw_data = response.read()
    try:
        data = json.loads(raw_data)
    except:
        raise Exception("Could not parse response from Pagerduty API")

    try:
        variable = data['users']
        if variable:
            return(variable, username, creds)
        else:
            variable = None
            return (variable, username, creds)
    except KeyError:
        raise Exception("Unexpected result from PagerDuty API:" + str(data))

def foundAccess(result):
    if result[0] is not None:
        accessChoice = result[2]['accessChoice']

        if accessChoice == "check":
            print "{} found in PagerDuty".format(result[1])
        if accessChoice == "remove":
            print "{} was found in PagerDuty, but automatic removal is not yet available. Please remove manually".format(result[1])

if __name__ == '__main__':
    print "Checking Pagerduty access"
    vendorEmail=None
    sepList = raw_input("Enter LDAP user to be separated. If multiple, separate by commas: ").split(',')
    isVendor = raw_input("Is this user a vendor? Yes/No: ").lower()

    while isVendor not in ('yes', 'no'):
        isVendor = raw_input("Sorry, looks like you misspelled 'yes' or 'no' somehow. Is this user a vendor? Yes/No: ").lower()

    if isVendor == "yes":
        vendorEmail = raw_input("Enter vendor email address: ")

    accessChoice = raw_input("Would you like to check or remove access? Check/Remove: ").lower()

    while True:
        if accessChoice not in ('remove', 'check'):
            accessChoice = raw_input("Sorry, looks like you misspelled 'remove' or 'check'. Please re-indicate if "
                                     "you'd like to remove all access or just check access. Remove/Check: ").lower()
            continue
        else:
            accessChoice = accessChoice
            break

    inputDict = {}
    inputDict.update({'creds': {'accessChoice': accessChoice,'vendorEmail':vendorEmail}})
    creds = inputDict['creds']

    for user in sepList:
        result = main(user, creds)
        foundAccess(result)

    ('qa-omniworkflowdb.sea1.marchex.com'):{'host':'qa-omniworkflowdb.sea1.marchex.com','dbname':'workflow_metrics'},
    ('qa-samamfdwdb.sea1.marchex.com'):{'host':'qa-samamfdwdb.sea1.marchex.com','dbname':'mamfdw'},
    ('qa-vspcsdb.som1.marchex.com'):{'host':'qa-vspcsdb.som1.marchex.com','dbname':'partnercredential_db'},
    ('qa-taxdb.som1.marchex.com'):{'host':'qa-taxdb.som1.marchex.com','dbname':'taxonomy_db'},
    ('qa-zuuldb.sea1.marchex.com'):{'host':'qa-zuuldb.sea1.marchex.com','dbname':'zuul'},
}

DB_USER = secret.get_secret('_PROD_POSTGRES_USER')
DB_PASS = secret.get_secret('_PROD_POSTGRES_PASS')

DB_QUERY = "select usename from pg_catalog.pg_user where usename LIKE '%{user}%'"

def connect_to_db(host,port,dbname):
    conn = psycopg2.connect(host=host,
                port=port,
                dbname=dbname,
                user=DB_USER,
                password=DB_PASS)

    cur=conn.cursor()
    
    return(cur,conn)

def main(user, creds):
    sql = DB_QUERY.format(user=user)

    dbs=[]
    del dbs[:]
    for host in HOST_LIST:
        try:
            connections = connect_to_db(
					DB_HOSTS[host].get('host',''),
                    DB_HOSTS[host].get('port',5432),
                    DB_HOSTS[host].get('dbname','')
                    )

            cur = connections[0]
            conn = connections[1]
            cur.execute(sql)
        except KeyError:
            print "{} not in host list, please investigate".format(host)
            continue
        except Exception as e:
            print("DB Query failed: "+str(e))

        rows = cur.fetchall()
        # Close DB communication
        cur.close()
        conn.close()

        if rows:
                dbs.append(DB_HOSTS[host]['host'])
    return(dbs, user, creds)

def foundAccess(result):
    accessChoice = result[2]['accessChoice']
    if len(result[0]) > 0:
        if accessChoice == "check":
            for db in result[0]:
                print "User has account on '{}'".format(db)
        if accessChoice == "remove":
            revokeAccess(result)

def revokeAccess(result):
    databases=result[0]
    user=result[1]
    sql = DB_QUERY.format(user=user)

    for db in databases:
        for v in DB_HOSTS[db]:
            connections = connect_to_db(
                    DB_HOSTS[db].get('host',''),
                    DB_HOSTS[db].get('port',5432),
                    DB_HOSTS[db].get('dbname',''),
                    v)
            cur = connections[0]
            conn = connections[1]


            cont = raw_input("{} will be removed from {}, continue (y/n)? If you select 'n', the user will NOT be removed ".format(user,db)).lower()
            if cont == "n":
                print "{} was not removed from {}".format(user,db)
                continue
            else:
                try:
                    cur.execute("DROP USER {};".format(user))
                    cur.execute("commit;")
                    cur.execute(sql)
                    rows = cur.fetchall()
                    cur.close()
                    conn.close()

                    if not rows:
                        print "{} has been successfully removed from {}".format(user,db)
                    else:
                        print "Something went wrong and {} was not removed from {}. Please remove manually".format(user,db)

                except Exception as e:
                    print(e)
                    cur.close()
                    conn.close()

if __name__ == '__main__':
    print "Checking PostgreSQL DB access"
    sepList = raw_input("Enter LDAP user to be separated. If multiple, separate by commas: ").split(',')
    accessChoice = raw_input("Would you like to check or remove access? Check/Remove: ").lower()

    while True:
        if accessChoice not in ('remove','check'):
            accessChoice = raw_input("Sorry, looks like you misspelled 'remove' or 'check'. Please re-indicate if you'd like to remove all access or just check access. Remove/Check: ").lower()
            continue
        else:
            accessChoice = accessChoice
            break

    inputDict = {}
    inputDict.update({'creds' : {'accessChoice' : accessChoice}})
    creds = inputDict['creds']

    for user in sepList:
        result = main(user,creds)
        foundAccess(result)




#rt_tickets.py

import secret
import rt
from rt_marchex import rtbroker

RT_USER = secret.get_secret('_SOC_UI_USER')
RT_PASS = secret.get_secret('_SOC_UI_PASS')

RT_HOST = 'https://rt.marchex.com'
RT_URL = 'https://rt.marchex.com/REST/1.0'

RT_QUERY = ("Owner = '{user}' "
            "AND ( Status = 'new' OR Status = 'open')")

def main(user, creds):
    rtb = rtbroker(RT_HOST)
    rtb.loginUser(RT_USER, RT_PASS)

    tickets = rtb.ticket_search(RT_USER, RT_QUERY.format(user=user))

    if tickets:
        return(tickets, user, creds)
    else:
        tickets = None
        return(tickets, user, creds)

def foundAccess(result):
    if result[0] is not None:
        accessChoice = result[2]['accessChoice']
        if accessChoice == "check":
            print "RT Tickets found for {}:".format(result[1])
            for key, val in result[0].iteritems():
                print '{}: {}\n'.format(key, val)
        if accessChoice == "remove":
            stealTicket(result)

def loginToRT():
    tracker=rt.Rt(RT_URL, RT_USER, RT_PASS)
    if not tracker.login():
        print "Failed to log in to RT"
        return False
    else:
        return tracker

def stealTicket(results):
    tracker = loginToRT()
    for key in results[0].keys():
        try:
            tracker.edit_ticket(key, Queue='SOC')
            tracker.steal(key)
            tracker.edit_ticket(key, Owner=RT_USER, Queue='Production')
            print "The following RT tickets have been taken:"
        except:
            print "Sorry, something went wrong. The following RT tickets could not be taken from {}:".format(results[1])
    for key, val in tickets[0].iteritems():
        print '{}: {}\n'.format(key, val)

if __name__ == '__main__':
    print "Checking RT Tickets"
    sepList = raw_input("Enter LDAP user to be separated. If multiple, separate by commas: ").split(',')
    accessChoice = raw_input("Would you like to check or remove access? Check/Remove: ").lower()

    while True:
        if accessChoice not in ('remove','check'):
            accessChoice = raw_input("Sorry, looks like you misspelled 'remove' or 'check'. Please re-indicate if you'd like to remove all access or just check access. Remove/Check: ").lower()
            continue
        else:
            accessChoice = accessChoice
            break

    inputDict = {}
    inputDict.update({'creds' : {'accessChoice' : accessChoice }})
    creds = inputDict['creds']

    for user in sepList:
        result = main(user, creds)
        foundAccess(result)




#separation.py

import logging
import pprint
import getpass
import ldap
import utils
# Any changes to sep script can be made starting here ----------------------------------------------------------------
# Any additional access checks to be added to this list
ACCESS_LIST = [
    'adtrack',
    'avenger',
    'aws',
    'grafana',
    'ipplan',
    # 'jingleaccess',
    'jira',
    'last3',
    'mi5',
    'microsite',
    'mysql_db',
    'nimui',
    'nismaps',
    'oracle_db',
    'pagerduty',
    'postgres_db',
    'rt_tickets',
    'slack',
    'tableau',
    'tacacs',
    'zenoss',
    'zenossSom1',
]
# LDAP specifications
LDAP_ADDR = 'ldaps://ldap.sea.marchex.com:636/'
LDAP_BASEDN = 'ou=users,dc=marchex,dc=com'
LDAP_BINDDN = 'uid={user},ou=users,dc=marchex,dc=com'
LDAP_SF = '(cn={user})'
# changes should not need to be made past this point unless something is broken in the script--------------------------
# Don't require signed cert:
ldap.set_option(ldap.OPT_X_TLS_REQUIRE_CERT, ldap.OPT_X_TLS_NEVER)
def main():
    # Gathering credential information
    print "\n########### SEPARATION SCRIPT #############"
    operatorUN = raw_input("Enter your LDAP username: ")
    operatorPass = getpass.getpass("Enter your LDAP password: ")
    # Gather username to be separated. Now able to take multiple.
    sepList = raw_input("Enter LDAP user to be separated. If multiple, separate by commas: ").split(',')
    # Asks if the separated user is a vendor
    isVendor = raw_input("Is this user a vendor? Yes/No: ").lower()
    while isVendor not in ('yes', 'no'):
        isVendor = raw_input("Sorry, looks like you misspelled 'yes' or 'no' somehow. Is this user a vendor? Yes/No: ").lower()
    if isVendor == "yes":
        vendorEmail = raw_input("Enter vendor email address: ")
    else:
        vendorEmail = None
    # Asks if you want to just check or remove access
    accessChoice = raw_input("Would you like to remove all found access or only print found access? "
                             "Remove/Check: ").lower()
    # Logic to make sure operator spells correctly or else everything breaks
    while accessChoice not in ('remove', 'check'):
            accessChoice = raw_input("Sorry, looks like you misspelled 'remove' or 'check'. Please re-indicate if "
                                     "you'd like to remove all access or just check access. Remove/Check: ").lower()
    # creates dictionary of credentials for use in various script modules
    inputDict = {
        'creds': {
            'operatorUN': operatorUN,
            'operatorPass': operatorPass,
            'sepList': sepList,
            'accessChoice': accessChoice,
            'vendorEmail': vendorEmail
        }
    }
    ldp = ldap.initialize(LDAP_ADDR)
    creds = inputDict['creds']
    auth_username = creds['operatorUN']
    auth_password = creds['operatorPass']
    try:
        ldp.simple_bind_s(LDAP_BINDDN.format(user=auth_username), auth_password)
    except ldap.INVALID_CREDENTIALS:
        print ("LDAP authentication failed")
    for user in creds['sepList']:
        verifyLDAP = ldapQuery(user)
        verifyAccess = checkAccess(user, creds)
        print "####### No further access found for {} #######".format(user)
# Make sure user is in LDAP
def ldapQuery(user,result_set=None):
    print "\n####### Checking access for {}: #######".format(user)
    ldp = ldap.initialize(LDAP_ADDR)
    result_id = ldp.search(LDAP_BASEDN, ldap.SCOPE_SUBTREE, LDAP_SF.format(user=user))
    result_type, result_data = ldp.result(result_id, 0)
    if result_set is None:
        result_set = []
    while result_data:
        result_set.append(result_data)
        result_type, result_data = ldp.result(result_id, 0)
    if result_set:
        print """
        User information pulled from LDAP:
        First name: {fn}
        Last name:  {ln}
        Manager:    {manager}""".format(
            fn=result_set[0][0][1].setdefault('givenName', ['Undefined'])[0],
            ln=result_set[0][0][1].setdefault('sn', ['Undefined'])[0],
            manager=result_set[0][0][1].setdefault('manager', ['Undefined'])[0])
    else:
        print "User not found in LDAP."
        return False
def check_chosen_access(chosenAccess):
    return chosenAccess in ACCESS_LIST
def get_valid_access_choice(invalidAccess):
    validAccess = invalidAccess
    while not check_chosen_access(validAccess):
        validAccess = raw_input("Sorry, you've given an invalid option. Give a valid system: ").lower()
    return validAccess
def checkAccess(user, creds, checkThisAccess=[], exclude=False):
    finalAccessList = []
    # Logic checking for any spelling errors in desired access if not default. Logic for excluding if desired.
    if checkThisAccess:
        correctedAccessList = []
        for chosenAccess in checkThisAccess:
            if not check_chosen_access(chosenAccess):
                chosenAccess = get_valid_Access_choice(chosenAccess)
            correctedAccessList.append(chosenAccess)
        if exclude:
            finalAccessList = set(ACCESS_LIST).difference(correctedAccessList)
        else:
            finalAccessList = correctedAccessList
    else:
        finalAccessList = ACCESS_LIST
    # Looping through to check/remove access
    for system in finalAccessList:
        try:
            sep_module = __import__(system)
            sep_result = sep_module.main(user,creds)
            sep_module.foundAccess(sep_result)
        except Exception as e:
            print (e)
if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()




#slack.py

import pprint
import secret
from slackclient import SlackClient
import logging

slackToken = secret.get_secret('_SLACK_API_KEY')

# import logging above and these two statements squelch INFO and DEBUG printout during execution from separation.py
# this makes it so it will not print out anything below warning level (info and debug are below warning level)
logging.getLogger("requests").setLevel(logging.WARNING)
logging.getLogger("urllib3").setLevel(logging.WARNING)

def main(user,creds):
    sc = SlackClient(slackToken)
    users = sc.api_call("users.list")

    for i in users:
        for t in users['members']:
            if user in t['name']:
                if t['deleted'] == False:
                    member = user
                    break
            else:
                member = None

    return(member,user,creds)

def foundAccess(result):
    if result[0] is not None:
        accessChoice = result[2]['accessChoice']
        if accessChoice == 'check':
            print "{} has Slack access".format(result[1])
        if accessChoice == "remove":
            print "{} has Slack access, but automatic removal has not been implemented. Please remove manually".format(result[1])

if __name__ == '__main__':
    operatorUN = raw_input("Input your LDAP username: ")
    user = raw_input('Input user to check. If multiple, separate by commas: ').split(',')
    accessChoice = raw_input("Would you like to check or remove access? Check/Remove: ").lower()

    while True:
        if accessChoice not in ('remove','check'):
            accessChoice = raw_input("Sorry, looks like you misspelled 'remove' or 'check'. Please re-indicate if you'd like to remove all access or just check access.           Remove/Check: ").lower()
            continue
        else:
            accessChoice = accessChoice
            break

    inputDict = {}
    inputDict.update({'creds': {'accessChoice' : accessChoice}})
    creds = inputDict['creds']

    for u in user:
        result = main(u, creds)
        foundAccess(result)




#tableau.py

import urllib2
import xml.etree.ElementTree as ET
import secret

# http://onlinehelp.tableau.com/current/api/rest_api/en-us/REST/rest_api_concepts_auth.htm#python_example_sign_in_sign_out

SERVER_NAME = 'tableau.marchex.com'
SITE_URL_ID = ''

AUTH_USER = secret.get_secret('_TABLEAU_UI_USER')
AUTH_PASS = secret.get_secret('_TABLEAU_UI_PASS')

def main(user, creds):
    check_user = user
    signin_url = "http://{server}/api/2.0/auth/signin".format(server=SERVER_NAME)
    request_xml = ET.Element('tsRequest')
    credentials = ET.SubElement(request_xml, 'credentials', name=AUTH_USER, password=AUTH_PASS)
    site_element = ET.SubElement(credentials, 'site', contentUrl=SITE_URL_ID)
    request_data = ET.tostring(request_xml)

    req = urllib2.Request(signin_url, data=request_data)
    response = urllib2.urlopen(req)
    server_response = response.read()
    response_xml = ET.fromstring(server_response)

    token = response_xml.find('.//t:credentials', namespaces={'t': "http://tableausoftware.com/api"}).attrib['token']
    site_id = response_xml.find('.//t:site', namespaces={'t': "http://tableausoftware.com/api"}).attrib['id']
    headers = {'X-tableau-auth': token}

    # Make the actual check:
    users_url = "http://{server}/api/2.0/sites/{siteid}/users?pageSize=999".format(server=SERVER_NAME, siteid=site_id)
    req2 = urllib2.Request(users_url, headers=headers)
    response2 = urllib2.urlopen(req2)

    response_data2 = response2.read()
    response_xml2 = ET.fromstring(response_data2)
    users_xml = response_xml2.findall('.//t:user', namespaces={'t': "http://tableausoftware.com/api"})

    users_array = []
    for user_xml in users_xml:
        if user_xml.attrib['siteRole'] != 'Unlicensed':
            users_array.append(user_xml.attrib['name'])

    result_array = []
    for user in users_array:
        if user.lower().startswith(check_user):
            result_array.append(user)

    if len(result_array):
        return(result_array, check_user, creds)
    else:
        result_array = None
        return(result_array, check_user, creds)

def foundAccess(result):
    if result[0] is not None:
        accessChoice = result[2]['accessChoice']
	if accessChoice == "check":
	    print "{} has Tableau UI access".format(result[1])
        if accessChoice == "remove":
	    print "{} has Tableau UI access, but automatic removal is not yet available. Please remove manually.".format(result[1])

if __name__ == '__main__':
    print "Checking Tableau UI Access"
    sepList = raw_input("Enter LDAP user to be separated. If multiple, separate by commas: ").split(',')
    accessChoice = raw_input("Would you like to check or remove access? Check/Remove: ").lower()

    while True:
        if accessChoice not in ('remove','check'):
            accessChoice = raw_input("Sorry, looks like you misspelled 'remove' or 'check'. Please re-indicate if you'd like to remove all access or just check access. Remove/Check: ").lower()
            continue
        else:
            accessChoice = accessChoice
            break

    inputDict = {}
    inputDict.update({'creds' : {'accessChoice' : accessChoice}})
    creds = inputDict['creds']

    for user in sepList:
        result = main(user, creds)
        foundAccess(result)




#tacacs.py

import logging
import smtplib
import requests
from email.mime.multipart import MIMEMultipart
from email.mime.text import MIMEText

CONF_URL = "https://github.marchex.com/raw/marchex/chef/master/cookbooks/tacplusapp/templates/default/tac_plus_conf.erb"
SOC = "soc@marchex.com"
EMAIL_TO = "production-issues@marchex.com"
EMAIL_SUBJECT = "TACACS Removal - {username}"

def main(user, creds):
    r=requests.get(CONF_URL)

    if user in r.content:
        return(r.content, user, creds)
    else:
        return(None,user,creds)

def foundAccess(result):
    accessChoice=result[2]['accessChoice']

    if result[0] is not None:
        if accessChoice == "check":
            print "User has TACACS access"
        if accessChoice == "remove":
            mail(result)

def mail(result):
    username = result[1]
    body = "Please remove {} from the TACACS Config".format(username)

    try:
        #send email
        msg = MIMEMultipart()
        msg['Subject'] = "TACACS Removal - {}".format(username)
        msg['From'] = SOC
        msg['To'] = EMAIL_TO

        msg.attach(MIMEText(body,'plain'))

        s = smtplib.SMTP('smtp.marchex.com')
        s.sendmail(SOC, EMAIL_TO, msg.as_string())
        s.quit()

        print "Email sent successfully. An unowned ticket has been created"

    except:
        raise Exception("Failed to send email and create ticket")

if __name__ == '__main__':
    sepList = raw_input("Enter LDAP user to be separated. If multiple, separate by commas: ").split(',')
    accessChoice = raw_input("Would you like to check or remove access? Check/Remove: ").lower()
    while True:
	if accessChoice not in ('remove','check'):
	    accessChoice = raw_input("Sorry, looks like you misspelled 'remove' or 'check'. Please re-indicate if you'd like to remove all access or just check access. Remove/Check: ").lower()
	    continue
	else:
	    accessChoice = accessChoice
	    break

    inputDict={}
    inputDict.update({'creds': {'accessChoice': accessChoice}})
    creds = inputDict['creds']

    for user in sepList:
        result = main(user,creds)
        foundAccess(result)




#zenoss.py

import requests
import getpass
import secret
import logging

# import logging above and these two statements squelch INFO and DEBUG printout during execution from separation.py
# this makes it so it will not print out anything below warning level (info and debug are below warning level)
logging.getLogger("requests").setLevel(logging.WARNING)
logging.getLogger("urllib3").setLevel(logging.WARNING)

operatorUN = secret.get_secret('_ZENOSS_UI_USER')
operatorPass = secret.get_secret('_ZENOSS_UI_PASS')

def main(user, creds):

    uid = {'user_id':user}

    with requests.Session() as s:
        url = 'http://zenoss.marchex.com:8080/zport/acl_users/cookieAuthHelper/login'
        values = {'__ac_name': operatorUN, '__ac_password': operatorPass}

        # login
        p = s.post(url, data=values)

        # send user name to site to check
        r = s.get('http://zenoss.marchex.com:8080/zport/dmd/ZenUsers/manageUserFolder', data=uid)

        # check zenoss output
        output = r.content
        my_string = user
        vendor = "-v"
        if my_string in output:
            zenoss_status = "User has zenoss access"
        elif my_string.find(vendor):
            if my_string[:-2] in output:
                zenoss_status = "User has zenoss access"
            else:
                zenoss_status = None
        else:
            zenoss_status = None

        return(zenoss_status, user, creds)

# report back if user found
def foundAccess(result):
    if result[0] is not None:
        accessChoice = result[2]['accessChoice']
        if accessChoice == 'check':
            print "{} has Zenoss access".format(result[1])
        if accessChoice == 'remove':
            print "{} has Zenoss access, but automatic removal is not yet available. Please remove manually.".format(result[1])

if __name__ == '__main__':

    sepList = raw_input("Enter LDAP user to be separated. If multiple, separate by commas: ").split(',')
    accessChoice = raw_input("Would you like to check or remove access? Check/Remove: ").lower()

    # Make sure the user spells the choice right
    while True:
        if accessChoice not in ('remove', 'check'):
            accessChoice = raw_input("Sorry, looks like you misspelled 'remove' or 'check'. Please re-indicate if you'd"
                                     "like to remove all access or just check access. Check/Remove: ").lower()
        else:
            accessChoice = accessChoice
            break

    inputDict = {}
    inputDict.update({'creds': { 'accessChoice': accessChoice}})
    creds = inputDict['creds']

    for user in sepList:
        result = main(user, creds)
        foundAccess(result)

        result = main(user, creds)
        foundAccess(result)
