import logging
import pprint
import getpass
import ldap
import utils
# Any changes to sep script can be made starting here ----------------------------------------------------------------
# Any additional access checks to be added to this list
ACCESS_LIST = [
    'adtrack',
    'avenger',
    'aws',
    'grafana',
    'ipplan',
    # 'jingleaccess',
    'jira',
    'last3',
    'mi5',
    'microsite',
    'mysql_db',
    'nimui',
    'nismaps',
    'oracle_db',
    'pagerduty',
    'postgres_db',
    'rt_tickets',
    'slack',
    'tableau',
    'tacacs',
    'zenoss',
    'zenossSom1',
]
# LDAP specifications
LDAP_ADDR = 'ldaps://ldap.sea.marchex.com:636/'
LDAP_BASEDN = 'ou=users,dc=marchex,dc=com'
LDAP_BINDDN = 'uid={user},ou=users,dc=marchex,dc=com'
LDAP_SF = '(cn={user})'
# changes should not need to be made past this point unless something is broken in the script--------------------------
# Don't require signed cert:
ldap.set_option(ldap.OPT_X_TLS_REQUIRE_CERT, ldap.OPT_X_TLS_NEVER)
def main():
    # Gathering credential information
    print "\n########### SEPARATION SCRIPT #############"
    operatorUN = raw_input("Enter your LDAP username: ")
    operatorPass = getpass.getpass("Enter your LDAP password: ")
    # Gather username to be separated. Now able to take multiple.
    sepList = raw_input("Enter LDAP user to be separated. If multiple, separate by commas: ").split(',')
    # Asks if the separated user is a vendor
    isVendor = raw_input("Is this user a vendor? Yes/No: ").lower()
    while isVendor not in ('yes', 'no'):
        isVendor = raw_input("Sorry, looks like you misspelled 'yes' or 'no' somehow. Is this user a vendor? Yes/No: ").lower()
    if isVendor == "yes":
        vendorEmail = raw_input("Enter vendor email address: ")
    else:
        vendorEmail = None
    # Asks if you want to just check or remove access
    accessChoice = raw_input("Would you like to remove all found access or only print found access? "
                             "Remove/Check: ").lower()
    # Logic to make sure operator spells correctly or else everything breaks
    while accessChoice not in ('remove', 'check'):
            accessChoice = raw_input("Sorry, looks like you misspelled 'remove' or 'check'. Please re-indicate if "
                                     "you'd like to remove all access or just check access. Remove/Check: ").lower()
    # creates dictionary of credentials for use in various script modules
    inputDict = {
        'creds': {
            'operatorUN': operatorUN,
            'operatorPass': operatorPass,
            'sepList': sepList,
            'accessChoice': accessChoice,
            'vendorEmail': vendorEmail
        }
    }
    ldp = ldap.initialize(LDAP_ADDR)
    creds = inputDict['creds']
    auth_username = creds['operatorUN']
    auth_password = creds['operatorPass']
    try:
        ldp.simple_bind_s(LDAP_BINDDN.format(user=auth_username), auth_password)
    except ldap.INVALID_CREDENTIALS:
        print ("LDAP authentication failed")
    for user in creds['sepList']:
        verifyLDAP = ldapQuery(user)
        verifyAccess = checkAccess(user, creds)
        print "####### No further access found for {} #######".format(user)
# Make sure user is in LDAP
def ldapQuery(user,result_set=None):
    print "\n####### Checking access for {}: #######".format(user)
    ldp = ldap.initialize(LDAP_ADDR)
    result_id = ldp.search(LDAP_BASEDN, ldap.SCOPE_SUBTREE, LDAP_SF.format(user=user))
    result_type, result_data = ldp.result(result_id, 0)
    if result_set is None:
        result_set = []
    while result_data:
        result_set.append(result_data)
        result_type, result_data = ldp.result(result_id, 0)
    if result_set:
        print """
        User information pulled from LDAP:
        First name: {fn}
        Last name:  {ln}
        Manager:    {manager}""".format(
            fn=result_set[0][0][1].setdefault('givenName', ['Undefined'])[0],
            ln=result_set[0][0][1].setdefault('sn', ['Undefined'])[0],
            manager=result_set[0][0][1].setdefault('manager', ['Undefined'])[0])
    else:
        print "User not found in LDAP."
        return False
def check_chosen_access(chosenAccess):
    return chosenAccess in ACCESS_LIST
def get_valid_access_choice(invalidAccess):
    validAccess = invalidAccess
    while not check_chosen_access(validAccess):
        validAccess = raw_input("Sorry, you've given an invalid option. Give a valid system: ").lower()
    return validAccess
def checkAccess(user, creds, checkThisAccess=[], exclude=False):
    finalAccessList = []
    # Logic checking for any spelling errors in desired access if not default. Logic for excluding if desired.
    if checkThisAccess:
        correctedAccessList = []
        for chosenAccess in checkThisAccess:
            if not check_chosen_access(chosenAccess):
                chosenAccess = get_valid_Access_choice(chosenAccess)
            correctedAccessList.append(chosenAccess)
        if exclude:
            finalAccessList = set(ACCESS_LIST).difference(correctedAccessList)
        else:
            finalAccessList = correctedAccessList
    else:
        finalAccessList = ACCESS_LIST
    # Looping through to check/remove access
    for system in finalAccessList:
        try:
            sep_module = __import__(system)
            sep_result = sep_module.main(user,creds)
            sep_module.foundAccess(sep_result)
        except Exception as e:
            print (e)
if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

i found a readme

## SOCBOT

Contains scripts, utilities, and cron jobs used or managed by the SOC.
Nothing in this repo should run persistently as a service - such things
should get their own repository in git.


### Dependencies

* Oracle Client (whack oracle-client) sqlplus
* Perl (whack perl)
* Python
* LDAP Utils (apt-get ldap-utils) ldapsearch
* Postgres Client and dev libraries (apt-get postgresql-client) psql libpq-dev


### History

This is the succcessor to the '/site/nocbot/' directory which lived on
soc[1-4].sea (noc[1-4].sea).


### Contributing

Small scripts unworthy of their own directory can be put in 'scripts/'. If
a large number of 

Larger utilities such as the Shift Report can have their own directory made
under the root of the repo, ex: 'ShiftReport/'.

NEVER should any scripts or similar files be placed directly under the root
of this repository, ex: '/badScript.pl'.


#### Accessing Password file (secret.conf)

*Bash:*

source $SECRET_FILE 2> /dev/null || \
	(echo "Cannot get password file, SOC ENV not loaded. EXITING." && exit 1)


*Perl:*

eval "use Secret; 1"
	or die "Cannot find Secret.pm module, SOC ENV not loaded. EXITING.";

#powershellScripts/jinglejangle.ps1

#This script grabs the table data from the http://intranet.free411.com/users.index.php?show_all_users=1 and exports it to an excel sheet. 
#This script must be run as admin on a windows system that has access to the jingle network. 
#For more detail on what is going on here, see my github. https://github.com/sethstuart/SethsPowershellTidbits . This script is broken into 3 seperate functions. 1. HTTPAuthenticate.ps1, 2. ParseHTMLTabletoCVS.ps1, and 3. CSVtoXLSX.ps1 in order. 

$global:delimiter = ";"

$global:writelocation = "C:\"

$global:csvname = "outfile.csv"

Function Authenticate($global:jingle2){
$passwd = read-host -Prompt "Please enter the SOC@Marchex.com password for the free411/Jingle account. (It's in Bitwarden.)" -AsSecureString
$PwdPointer = [Runtime.InteropServices.Marshal]::SecureStringToBSTR($passwd)
$passwd = [Runtime.InteropServices.Marshal]::PtrToStringAuto($PwdPointer)

$jingle = invoke-webrequest -uri https://intranet.free411.com/login.php -SessionVariable tingle #This line inits the variable jingle, and invokes a request to the user page. We expect it to return a form containing an ID, an empty username field, and an empty passwd field. We also expect it to return a set of cookies associated with the user session. This session variable is called tingle, (as in the weird guy from Legend of Zelda) which rhymes with jingle. 

$fID = $jingle.Forms.Fields.form_id #The variable fID is the ID of the login form_id

$Response = @{"form_id" = $fID;"form_name" = "login";"email_address" = "soc@marchex.com";"password" = $passwd;"login_submit" = "Login"} #This line is the response information we will pass back to the site to authenticate. It is made up of an array with the three previously specified values, and with the name of the form, and  a login action.

$header = @{Accept = '*/*'} #This field is the header field, which allows us to accept any and all content types

$jingle = invoke-webrequest -uri https://intranet.free411.com/login.php -WebSession $tingle -Method POST -Body $Response -Headers $header #This line sends the authentication data to the page and allows us to log in. 

$global:jingle2 = invoke-webrequest -uri https://intranet.free411.com/users/index.php?show_all_users=1 -WebSession $tingle -Method GET -Headers $header #this line will direct us to, and gather the information from the users/index page so we can parse it and send it to excel
}

Authenticate

Function ParseHTMLTableToCSV {
$TableNumber = 0

$tables = @($global:jingle2.ParsedHtml.getElementsByTagName("TABLE"))

$table = $tables[$TableNumber]

$titles = @()

$rows = @($table.Rows)

$TableArray = @()

## Go through all of the rows in the table

foreach($row in $rows)

{

    $cells = @($row.Cells)

   

    ## If we've found a table header, remember its titles

    if($cells[0].tagName -eq "TH")

    {

        $titles = @($cells | % { ("" + $_.InnerText).Trim() })

        continue

    }

    ## If we haven't found any table headers, make up names "P1", "P2", etc.

    if(-not $titles)

    {

        $titles = @(1..($cells.Count + 2) | % { "P$_" })

    }

    ## Now go through the cells in the the row. For each, try to find the

    ## title that represents that column and create a hashtable mapping those

    ## titles to content

    $resultObject = [Ordered] @{}

    for($counter = 0; $counter -lt $cells.Count; $counter++)

    {

        $title = $titles[$counter]

        if(-not $title) { continue }

       

        $resultObject[$title] = ("" + $cells[$counter].InnerText).Trim()

    }

    ## And finally cast that hashtable to a PSCustomObject

    $TableArray += [PSCustomObject] $resultObject 
}

$TableArray | Export-Csv -Path ($global:writelocation + $global:csvname) -Delimiter $global:delimiter -NoTypeInformation
}

ParseHTMLTableToCSV

function CSVtoXLSX {
# Create a new Excel workbook with one empty sheet
$excel = New-Object -ComObject excel.application 
$workbook = $excel.Workbooks.Add(1)
$worksheet = $workbook.worksheets.Item(1)

# Build the QueryTables.Add command and reformat the data
$TxtConnector = ("TEXT;" + ($global:writelocation + $global:csvname))
$Connector = $worksheet.QueryTables.add($TxtConnector,$worksheet.Range("A1"))
$query = $worksheet.QueryTables.item($Connector.name)
$query.TextFileOtherDelimiter = $global:delimiter
$query.TextFileParseType  = 1
$query.TextFileColumnDataTypes = ,1 * $worksheet.Cells.Columns.Count
$query.AdjustColumnWidth = 1

# Execute & delete the import query
$query.Refresh()
$query.Delete()

# Save & close the Workbook as XLSX.
$Workbook.SaveAs($global:writelocation+'UsersList.xlsx')
$excel.Quit()

Remove-Item ($global:writelocation + $global:csvname) #clean up the Csv

write-host "Your file is located in $global:writelocation as UsersList.xlsx."

}

CSVtoXLSX

# Don't require signed cert for LDAP connection
ldap.set_option(ldap.OPT_X_TLS_REQUIRE_CERT, ldap.OPT_X_TLS_NEVER)


def get_user_input(prompt):
    """Wrapper for input to handle common input scenarios."""
    try:
        return input(prompt).strip()
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Error getting user input: {e}")
        return None


def main():
    """ Main function for the separation script. """
    logging.info("########### SEPARATION SCRIPT #############")

    operatorUN = get_user_input("Enter your LDAP username: ")
    operatorPass = getpass.getpass("Enter your LDAP password: ")

    # Gather usernames to be separated
    sepList = get_user_input("Enter LDAP user(s) to be separated (comma-separated): ").split(',')

    # Check if user is a vendor
    while True:
        isVendor = get_user_input("Is this user a vendor? (yes/no): ").lower()
        if isVendor in ('yes', 'no'):
            break
        logging.warning("Invalid input. Please enter 'yes' or 'no'.")

    vendorEmail = get_user_input("Enter vendor email address: ") if isVendor == "yes" else None

    # Ask if we are checking or removing access
    while True:
        accessChoice = get_user_input("Would you like to remove all found access or just check access? (Remove/Check): ").lower()
        if accessChoice in ('remove', 'check'):
            break
        logging.warning("Invalid input. Please enter 'Remove' or 'Check'.")

    creds = {
        "operatorUN": operatorUN,
        "operatorPass": operatorPass,
        "sepList": sepList,
        "accessChoice": accessChoice,
        "vendorEmail": vendorEmail
    }

    try:
        ldp = ldap.initialize(LDAP_ADDR)
        ldp.simple_bind_s(LDAP_BINDDN.format(user=operatorUN), operatorPass)
    except ldap.INVALID_CREDENTIALS:
        logging.error("LDAP authentication failed. Exiting.")
        return
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Unexpected LDAP error: {e}")
        return

    for user in sepList:
        logging.info(f"Processing separation for {user}...")
        if ldapQuery(user):
            checkAccess(user, creds)
        logging.info(f"####### No further access found for {user} #######")


def ldapQuery(user):
    """Check if user exists in LDAP and return user information."""
    logging.info(f"Checking LDAP access for {user}...")
    try:
        ldp = ldap.initialize(LDAP_ADDR)
        result_id = ldp.search(LDAP_BASEDN, ldap.SCOPE_SUBTREE, LDAP_SF.format(user=user))
        result_type, result_data = ldp.result(result_id, 0)

        if not result_data:
            logging.warning(f"User {user} not found in LDAP.")
            return False

        user_data = result_data[0][1]
        logging.info(f"""
        User information from LDAP:
        First Name: {user_data.get('givenName', ['Undefined'])[0]}
        Last Name:  {user_data.get('sn', ['Undefined'])[0]}
        Manager:    {user_data.get('manager', ['Undefined'])[0]}
        """)
        return True

    except ldap.LDAPError as e:
        logging.error(f"LDAP query failed for {user}: {e}")
        return False


def checkAccess(user, creds):
    """Iterates through all systems in ACCESS_LIST and runs their respective separation scripts."""
    logging.info(f"Checking access for {user}...")
    for system in ACCESS_LIST:
        try:
            sep_module = __import__(system.lower())  # Import script dynamically
            sep_result = sep_module.main(user, creds)
            sep_module.foundAccess(sep_result)
        except ImportError:
            logging.warning(f"Module {system} not found. Skipping...")
        except Exception as e:
            logging.error(f"Error running {system} separation: {e}")


if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
import logging
import getpass
import ldap
import utils

# Setup logging
logging.basicConfig(
    format='%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s',
    level=logging.INFO
)

from concurrent.futures import ThreadPoolExecutor

def process_user(user, creds):
    if ldapQuery(user):
        checkAccess(user, creds)

with ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=5) as executor:
    executor.map(lambda user: process_user(user, creds), sepList)

LDAP_SF = '(cn={user})'

# Don't require signed cert for LDAP connection
ldap.set_option(ldap.OPT_X_TLS_REQUIRE_CERT, ldap.OPT_X_TLS_NEVER)


def get_user_input(prompt):
    """Wrapper for input to handle common input scenarios."""
    try:
        return input(prompt).strip()
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Error getting user input: {e}")
        return None


def main():
    """ Main function for the separation script. """
    logging.info("########### SEPARATION SCRIPT #############")

    operatorUN = get_user_input("Enter your LDAP username: ")
    operatorPass = getpass.getpass("Enter your LDAP password: ")

    # Gather usernames to be separated
    sepList = get_user_input("Enter LDAP user(s) to be separated (comma-separated): ").split(',')

    # Check if user is a vendor
    while True:
        isVendor = get_user_input("Is this user a vendor? (yes/no): ").lower()
        if isVendor in ('yes', 'no'):
            break
        logging.warning("Invalid input. Please enter 'yes' or 'no'.")

    vendorEmail = get_user_input("Enter vendor email address: ") if isVendor == "yes" else None

    # Ask if we are checking or removing access
    while True:
        accessChoice = get_user_input("Would you like to remove all found access or just check access? (Remove/Check): ").lower()
        if accessChoice in ('remove', 'check'):
            break
        logging.warning("Invalid input. Please enter 'Remove' or 'Check'.")

    creds = {
        "operatorUN": operatorUN,
        "operatorPass": operatorPass,
        "sepList": sepList,
        "accessChoice": accessChoice,
        "vendorEmail": vendorEmail
    }

    try:
        ldp = ldap.initialize(LDAP_ADDR)
        ldp.simple_bind_s(LDAP_BINDDN.format(user=operatorUN), operatorPass)
    except ldap.INVALID_CREDENTIALS:
        logging.error("LDAP authentication failed. Exiting.")
        return
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Unexpected LDAP error: {e}")
        return

    for user in sepList:
        logging.info(f"Processing separation for {user}...")
        if ldapQuery(user):
            checkAccess(user, creds)
        logging.info(f"####### No further access found for {user} #######")


def ldapQuery(user):
    """Check if user exists in LDAP and return user information."""
    logging.info(f"Checking LDAP access for {user}...")
    try:
        ldp = ldap.initialize(LDAP_ADDR)
        result_id = ldp.search(LDAP_BASEDN, ldap.SCOPE_SUBTREE, LDAP_SF.format(user=user))
        result_type, result_data = ldp.result(result_id, 0)

        if not result_data:
            logging.warning(f"User {user} not found in LDAP.")
            return False

        user_data = result_data[0][1]
        logging.info(f"""
        User information from LDAP:
        First Name: {user_data.get('givenName', ['Undefined'])[0]}
        Last Name:  {user_data.get('sn', ['Undefined'])[0]}
        Manager:    {user_data.get('manager', ['Undefined'])[0]}
        """)
        return True

    except ldap.LDAPError as e:
        logging.error(f"LDAP query failed for {user}: {e}")
        return False


def checkAccess(user, creds):
    """Iterates through all systems in ACCESS_LIST and runs their respective separation scripts."""
    logging.info(f"Checking access for {user}...")
    for system in ACCESS_LIST:
        try:
            sep_module = __import__(f"separations.{system.lower()}", fromlist=[""])
            sep_result = sep_module.main(user, creds)
            sep_module.foundAccess(sep_result)
        except ImportError:
            logging.warning(f"Module {system} not found. Skipping...")
        except Exception as e:
            logging.error(f"Error running {system} separation: {e}")


if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

LDAP_BASEDN = 'ou=users,dc=marchex,dc=com'

# Don't require signed cert for LDAP connection
ldap.set_option(ldap.OPT_X_TLS_REQUIRE_CERT, ldap.OPT_X_TLS_NEVER)


def input(prompt):
    """Wrapper for input to handle common input scenarios."""
    try:
        return input(prompt).strip()
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Error getting user input: {e}")
        return None


def main():
    """ Main function for the separation script. """
    logging.info("########### SEPARATION SCRIPT #############")

    operatorUN = input("Enter your LDAP username: ")
    operatorPass = getpass.getpass("Enter your LDAP password: ")

    # Gather usernames to be separated
    sepList = input("Enter LDAP user(s) to be separated (comma-separated): ").split(',')

    # Check if user is a vendor
    while True:
        isVendor = input("Is this user a vendor? (yes/no): ").lower()
        if isVendor in ('yes', 'no'):
            break
        logging.warning("Invalid input. Please enter 'yes' or 'no'.")

    vendorEmail = None
    if isVendor == "yes":
        if any(sys in ACCESS_LIST for sys in ["PagerDuty", "Microsites"]):
            vendorEmail = input("Enter vendor email address: ")
        else:
            logging.info("Vendor email not needed for selected systems.")

    # Ask if we are checking or removing access
    while True:
        accessChoice = input("Would you like to remove all found access or just check access? (Remove/Check): ").lower()
        if accessChoice in ('remove', 'check'):
            break
        logging.warning("Invalid input. Please enter 'Remove' or 'Check'.")

    creds = {
        "operatorUN": operatorUN,
        "operatorPass": operatorPass,
        "sepList": sepList,
        "accessChoice": accessChoice,
        "vendorEmail": vendorEmail
    }

    try:
        ldp = ldap.initialize(LDAP_ADDR)
        ldp.simple_bind_s(LDAP_BINDDN.format(user=operatorUN), operatorPass)
    except ldap.INVALID_CREDENTIALS:
        logging.error("LDAP authentication failed. Exiting.")
        return
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Unexpected LDAP error: {e}")
        return

    for user in sepList:
        logging.info(f"Processing separation for {user}...")
        if ldapQuery(ldp, user):
            checkAccess(user, creds)
        logging.info(f"####### No further access found for {user} #######")

    # Run separations in parallel using multi-threading
    with ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=5) as executor:
        executor.map(lambda user: process_user(user, creds), sepList)
            
def ldapQuery(ldp, user):
    """Check if user exists in LDAP and return user information."""
    logging.info(f"Checking LDAP access for {user}...")
    try:
        result_id = ldp.search(LDAP_BASEDN, ldap.SCOPE_SUBTREE, LDAP_SF.format(user=user))
        result_type, result_data = ldp.result(result_id, 0)

        if not result_data:
            logging.warning(f"User {user} not found in LDAP.")
            return False

        user_data = result_data[0][1]
        logging.info(f"""
        User information from LDAP:
        First Name: {user_data.get('givenName', ['Undefined'])[0]}
        Last Name:  {user_data.get('sn', ['Undefined'])[0]}
        Manager:    {user_data.get('manager', ['Undefined'])[0]}
        """)
        return True

    except ldap.LDAPError as e:
        logging.error(f"LDAP query failed for {user}: {e}")
        return False


def checkAccess(user, creds):
    """Iterates through all systems in ACCESS_LIST and runs their respective separation scripts."""
    logging.info(f"Checking access for {user}...")
    missing_modules = []
    
    for system in ACCESS_LIST:
        try:
            sep_module = __import__(f"separations.{system.lower()}", fromlist=[""])
            sep_result = sep_module.main(user, creds)
            sep_module.foundAccess(sep_result)
        except ImportError:
            missing_modules.append(system)
        except Exception as e:
            logging.error(f"Error running {system} separation: {e}")
    
    if missing_modules:
        logging.warning(f"The following systems have no separation scripts and were skipped: {', '.join(missing_modules)}")

def process_user(ldp, user):
    if ldapQuery(ldp, user):
        checkAccess(user)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

ACCESS_LIST = [system for system, enabled in SYSTEMS_CATALOG.items() if enabled]
MISSING_SCRIPTS = []

# LDAP Configurations
LDAP_ADDR = 'ldaps://ldap.sea.marchex.com:636/'
LDAP_BASEDN = 'ou=users,dc=marchex,dc=com'
LDAP_BINDDN = 'uid={user},ou=users,dc=marchex,dc=com'
LDAP_SF = '(cn={user})'

# Don't require signed cert for LDAP connection
ldap.set_option(ldap.OPT_X_TLS_REQUIRE_CERT, ldap.OPT_X_TLS_NEVER)


def get_user_input(prompt):
    """Wrapper for input to handle common input scenarios."""
    try:
        return input(prompt).strip()
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Error getting user input: {e}")
        return None


def main():
    """ Main function for the separation script. """
    logging.info("########### SEPARATION SCRIPT #############")

    operatorUN = get_user_input("Enter your LDAP username: ")
    operatorPass = getpass.getpass("Enter your LDAP password: ")

    # Gather usernames to be separated
    sepList = get_user_input("Enter LDAP user(s) to be separated (comma-separated): ").split(',')

    # Check if user is a vendor
    while True:
        isVendor = get_user_input("Is this user a vendor? (yes/no): ").lower()
        if isVendor in ('yes', 'no'):
            break
        logging.warning("Invalid input. Please enter 'yes' or 'no'.")

    vendorEmail = None
    if isVendor == "yes":
        if any(sys in ACCESS_LIST for sys in ["PagerDuty", "Microsites"]):
            vendorEmail = get_user_input("Enter vendor email address: ")
        else:
            logging.info("Vendor email not needed for selected systems.")

    # Ask if we are checking or removing access
    while True:
        accessChoice = get_user_input("Would you like to remove all found access or just check access? (Remove/Check): ").lower()
        if accessChoice in ('remove', 'check'):
            break
        logging.warning("Invalid input. Please enter 'Remove' or 'Check'.")

    creds = {
        "operatorUN": operatorUN,
        "operatorPass": operatorPass,
        "sepList": sepList,
        "accessChoice": accessChoice,
        "vendorEmail": vendorEmail
    }

    try:
        ldp = ldap.initialize(LDAP_ADDR)
        ldp.simple_bind_s(LDAP_BINDDN.format(user=operatorUN), operatorPass)
    except ldap.INVALID_CREDENTIALS:
        logging.error("LDAP authentication failed. Exiting.")
        return
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Unexpected LDAP error: {e}")
        return

    # Run separations in parallel using multi-threading
    with ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=5) as executor:
        executor.map(lambda user: process_user(ldp, user, creds), sepList)

    logging.info(f"####### No further access found for {user} #######")

    if MISSING_SCRIPTS:
        logging.warning(f"Missing separation scripts: {', '.join(set(MISSING_SCRIPTS))}")


def ldapQuery(ldp, user):
    """Check if user exists in LDAP and return user information."""
    logging.info(f"Checking LDAP access for {user}...")
    try:
        result_id = ldp.search(LDAP_BASEDN, ldap.SCOPE_SUBTREE, LDAP_SF.format(user=user))
        result_type, result_data = ldp.result(result_id, 0)

        if not result_data:
            logging.warning(f"User {user} not found in LDAP.")
            return False

        user_data = result_data[0][1]
        logging.info(f"""
        User information from LDAP:
        First Name: {user_data.get('givenName', ['Undefined'])[0]}
        Last Name:  {user_data.get('sn', ['Undefined'])[0]}
        Manager:    {user_data.get('manager', ['Undefined'])[0]}
        """)
        return True

    except ldap.LDAPError as e:
        logging.error(f"LDAP query failed for {user}: {e}")
        return False


def checkAccess(user, creds):
    global MISSING_SCRIPTS  # Track missing scripts across all users
    logging.info(f"Checking access for {user}...")

    for system in ACCESS_LIST:
        try:
            sep_module = __import__(f"separations.{system.lower()}", fromlist=[""])
            sep_result = sep_module.main(user, creds)
            sep_module.foundAccess(sep_result)
        except ImportError:
            MISSING_SCRIPTS.append(system)
        except Exception as e:
            logging.error(f"Error running {system} separation: {e}")


def process_user(user, creds):
    try:
        ldp = ldap.initialize(LDAP_ADDR)
        ldp.simple_bind_s(LDAP_BINDDN.format(user=creds["operatorUN"]), creds["operatorPass"])

        if ldapQuery(ldp, user):
            checkAccess(user, creds)
        logging.info(f"####### No further access found for {user} #######")

    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Error processing user {user}: {e}")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

import logging
import pprint
import psycopg2
import sys
import secret

DB_NAME = 'adtrack_ro'
DB_HOST = 'vspool.som1.marchex.com'
DB_PORT = 5432

DB_USER = secret.get_secret('_ADTRACK_DB_USER')
DB_PASS = secret.get_secret('_ADTRACK_DB_PASS')

def main(user, creds):
    marchex = ("SELECT email FROM at_user "
            "WHERE email ILIKE '{username}@marchex%' AND status != 'disabled'").format(username=user)
    vendor = ("SELECT email FROM at_user "
            "WHERE email ILIKE '{email}' AND status != 'disabled'").format(email=creds['vendorEmail'])

    try:
        conn = psycopg2.connect(host=DB_HOST, database=DB_NAME,
                port=DB_PORT, user=DB_USER, password=DB_PASS)
    except Exception as e:
        raise Exception("Could not connect to DB '{}': {}".format(DB_HOST, e))

    cur = conn.cursor()
    if creds['vendorEmail'] == None:
        try:
            cur.execute(marchex)
        except Exception as e:
            raise Exception("DB Query failed in the adtrack.py module: "+str(e))
    else:
        try:
            cur.execute(vendor)
        except Exception as e:
            raise Exception("DB Query failed in the adtrack.py module: "+str(e))

    rows = cur.fetchall()

    # Close DB communication
    cur.close()
    conn.close()

    if rows:
        output = [row[0] for row in rows]
        return(output,user,creds)
    else:
        output = None
        return(output,user,creds)

def foundAccess(result):
    if result[0] is not None:
        accessChoice = result[2]['accessChoice']
        if accessChoice == "check":
            print "{} has Adtrack UI access".format(result[1])
        if accessChoice == "remove":
            print "{} has Adtrack UI access, but automatic removal is not yet available. Please remove manually:".format(result[1])

if __name__ == '__main__':
    vendorEmail=None
    sepList = raw_input("Enter LDAP user to be separated. If multiple, separate by commas: ").split(',')
    accessChoice = raw_input("Would you like to check or remove access? Check/Remove: ").lower()
    isVendor = raw_input("Is this user a vendor? Yes/No: ").lower()

    while isVendor not in ('yes', 'no'):
        isVendor = raw_input("Sorry, looks like you misspelled 'yes' or 'no' somehow. Is this user a vendor? Yes/No: ").lower()

    if isVendor == "yes":
        vendorEmail = raw_input("Enter vendor email address: ")

    while True:
        if accessChoice not in ('remove','check'):
            accessChoice = raw_input("Sorry, looks like you misspelled 'remove' or 'check'. Please re-indicate if you'd like to remove all access or just check access. Remove/Check: ").lower()
            continue
        else:
            accessChoice = accessChoice
            break

    inputDict = {}
    inputDict.update({'creds' : {'accessChoice' : accessChoice,'vendorEmail':vendorEmail}})
    creds = inputDict['creds']

    for user in sepList:
        result = main(user, creds)
        foundAccess(result)

import logging
import pprint
import MySQLdb
import sys
import secret

## Config
DB_HOST = 'elpagedb-master.marchex.com'
DB_USER = secret.get_secret('_PROD_MYSQL_USER')
DB_PASS = secret.get_secret('_PROD_MYSQL_PASS')

## SQL queries
SQL_COMMANDS = {
    # checks if user exists and is active
    "check_for_user": "SELECT username, firstname, lastname FROM avenger.user WHERE username = '{username}' AND is_active = 1",

    # removes user role
    "remove": "delete from avenger.user_role where user_id = (select user_id from avenger.user where username = '{username}');",

    # sets user to inactive
    "deactivate": "UPDATE avenger.user set is_active = 0 WHERE username = '{username}';",
}

def command_from_username(command, username):
    return SQL_COMMANDS[command].format(username=username)

def execute_mysql_command(db, query):
    """Helper function to execute queries in try block."""
    try:
        cur = db.cursor()
        cur.execute(query)
        return cur.fetchall()
    except Exception as e:
        raise Exception("Error executing query in avenger.py module: {}\n{}".format(query, str(e)))
    finally:
        cur.close()

def main(user, creds):
    output = None
    username = user
    # Attempt to connect to DB
    try:
        db = MySQLdb.connect(host=DB_HOST, user=DB_USER, passwd=DB_PASS)
    except Exception as e:
        db.close()
        raise Exception("Could not connect to DB in avenger.py module '{}': {}".format(DB_HOST, str(e)))

    # Check for user
    try:
        query_output = execute_mysql_command(db, command_from_username('check_for_user', username))
        if query_output:
            output = ['{} ({} {})'.format(row[0], row[1], row[2]) for row in query_output]
            return(output, username, creds)
        else:
            output = None
            return(output, username, creds)
    except Exception as e:
        raise Exception("DB Query failed in avenger.py module: " + str(e))
    finally:
        db.close()

# Access/no access logic
def foundAccess(result):
    if result[0] is not None:
        accessChoice = result[2]['accessChoice']
        if accessChoice == 'remove':
            deactivation(result)
        if accessChoice == 'check':
            print "{} has Avenger UI access".format(result[1])

# deactivation
def deactivation(result):

    username = result[1]

    # connect to the DB
    try:
        db = MySQLdb.connect(host=DB_HOST, user=DB_USER, passwd=DB_PASS)
    except Exception as e:
        db.close()
        raise Exception("Could not connect to DB in avenger.py module '{}': {}".format(DB_HOST, str(e)))

    # deactivate user
    try:
        # remove user role
        execute_mysql_command(db, command_from_username('remove', username))
        # deactivate user
        execute_mysql_command(db, command_from_username('deactivate', username))
        # if we made it this far, success!
    except Exception as e:
        raise Exception("DB command failed in avenger.py module: "+str(e))
        db.rollback()
    else:
        db.commit()

    # recheck for user
    try:
        query_output = execute_mysql_command(db, command_from_username('check_for_user', username))
        if query_output:
            print "Something went wrong and {}'s account was not deactivated. Please remove AvengerUI access manually".format(result[1])
        else:
            print "Avenger UI Access Removed for {}".format(result[1])
    finally:
        db.close()

if __name__ == '__main__':
    print "Checking Avenger UI access"
    user = raw_input("Input username to check. If multiple, separate by commas: ").split(',')
    accessChoice = raw_input("Would you like to check or remove access? Check/Remove: ").lower()

    while True:
      if accessChoice not in ('remove','check'):
         accessChoice = raw_input("Sorry, looks like you misspelled 'remove' or 'check'. Please re-indicate if you'd like to remove all access or just check access. Remove/Check: ").lower()
         continue
      else:
         accessChoice = accessChoice
         break

    inputDict = {}
    inputDict.update({'creds' : {'accessChoice' : accessChoice}})
    creds = inputDict['creds']

    for u in user:
        result = main(u, creds)
        foundAccess(result)

import logging
import subprocess
import json

# DOCUMENTATION:
# http://docs.aws.amazon.com/cli/latest/userguide/cli-chap-getting-set-up.html#cli-signup
# http://docs.aws.amazon.com/AWSEC2/latest/CommandLineReference/ec2-cli-managing-certs.html

# Script requires aws command (Python awscli module)
# sudo pip install awscli

# Command is: aws iam list-users

# Setup:
# cd ~/.ssh
# openssl genrsa 2048 > aws_iam.pem
# openssl req -new -x509 -nodes -sha256 -key aws_iam.pem aws_iam.pem > aws_iam_user_signing.pem
# Go to:
#   https://console.aws.amazon.com/iam/home
# Select your user, click the "Security Credentials" tab, and upload the "Signing Certificate" you generated
# Back to the URL above, go to the same place and click "Create Acess Key"
# Copy the info provided ("Access Key ID", "Security Access Key"), store it somewhere
# You will need it in the next steps

# THEN:
# aws configure
# Provide the Access Key and Security Access Key you got just before.
# Run the command aws iam list-users to test

def main(user, creds):
    check_user = user
    auth_user = creds['operatorUN']

    return_code = subprocess.call(['aws'], stdout=subprocess.PIPE, stderr=subprocess.PIPE)
    if not return_code == 2:
	raise Exception('aws cli tools do not seem to be installed. Check the marchex_aws.py script for instructions on setup.')
    try:
	output = subprocess.check_output(['aws','iam','list-users','--profile',auth_user], stderr=subprocess.STDOUT)
    except subprocess.CalledProcessError as e:
	if 'The config profile' in e.output:
	    raise Exception(('AWS CLI profile not set up. First run aws configure --profile {}'
		'\n\tSee marchex_aws.py for detailed instructions.').format(auth_user))
	else:
	    raise Exception('Command aws iam list-users failed: {}'.format(e.output.strip()))


    if user in output:
        account=user
    else:
        account=None

    return(account,user,creds)

def foundAccess(result):
    if result[0] is not None:
        accessChoice = result[2]['accessChoice']
        if accessChoice == 'check':
	    print "{} has AWS access".format(result[1])
        if accessChoice == "remove":
            deleteAccess(result)

def deleteAccess(result):
    user = result[1]
    auth_user = result[2]['operatorUN']
    try:
        deleted = subprocess.check_output(['aws','iam','delete-user','--profile',auth_user,'--user-name',user],stderr=subprocess.STDOUT)
    except subprocess.CalledProcessError as e:
        raise Exception('Command aws iam delete-user has failed: {}\nPlease remove {} access manually'.format(e,user))

    try:
        output= subprocess.check_output(['aws','iam','list-users','--profile',auth_user], stderr=subprocess.STDOUT)
    except Exception as e:
        print("User {} AWS access was not deleted successfully. Please manually remove it\nError:{}".format(user,e))

    if user not in output:
        print("AWS access for {} was successfully removed".format(user))

if __name__ == '__main__':

    operatorUN = raw_input("Input your LDAP username: ")

import requests
import getpass

def main(user, creds):

    operatorUN = creds['operatorUN']
    operatorPass = creds['operatorPass']

    with requests.Session() as s:
        url = 'http://grafana.marchex.com/login'
        values = {'user': operatorUN, 'password': operatorPass}

        # login
        p = s.post(url, data=values)

        # get list of users with Grafana access
        try:
            r = s.get('http://grafana.marchex.com/org/users')
        except Exception as e:
            print("Failed to get grafana user access for {}\nError: {}".format(user,e))

        # check Grafana output
        output = r.content
        my_string = user

        if my_string in output:
            Grafana_status = my_string
        else:
            Grafana_status = None

        return(Grafana_status, user, creds)

# report back if user found or not
def foundAccess(result):
    if result[0] is not None:
        accessChoice = result[2]['accessChoice']
        if accessChoice == 'check':
            print "{} has Grafana access".format(result[1])
        if accessChoice == 'remove':
            print "{} has Grafana access, but automatic removal is not yet available. Please remove manually.".format(result[1])
    else:
        return

if __name__ == '__main__':

    operatorUN = raw_input('Input your username, to authenticate to Grafana: ')
    operatorPass = getpass.getpass('Input your password: ')
    sepList = raw_input("Enter LDAP user to be separated. If multiple, separate by commas: ").split(',')
    accessChoice = raw_input("Would you like to check or remove access? Check/Remove: ").lower()

    # Make sure the user spells the choice right
    while True:
        if accessChoice not in ('remove', 'check'):
            accessChoice = raw_input("Sorry, looks like you misspelled 'remove' or 'check'. Please re-indicate if you'd"
                                     "like to remove all access or just check access. Check/Remove ").lower()
        else:
            accessChoice = accessChoice
            break

    inputDict = {}
    inputDict.update({'creds': {'operatorUN': operatorUN, 'operatorPass': operatorPass, 'accessChoice': accessChoice}})
    creds = inputDict['creds']

    for user in sepList:
        result = main(user, creds)
        foundAccess(result)

def main(user, creds):

    with requests.Session() as s:

        # login to IP Plan & check for user
        try:
            r = s.get('https://ipplan.marchex.com/admin/usermanager.php?action=usereditform', auth=HTTPBasicAuth(IPPLAN_USER, IPPLAN_PASS))
        except Exception as e:
            print("Failed to get ipplan information on {}\nError: {}".format(user,e))

        output = r.content

        if user in output:
            status = "Y"
        else:
            status = None

        return(status, user, creds)

next is JIRA.py




import logging
import sys
import urllib2, base64
import json

# Jira API Documentation:
# https://docs.atlassian.com/jira/REST/latest/#api/2/user

URL = "https://jira.marchex.com/rest/api/latest/user?username="

def main(user, creds):
    user = user
    username = creds['operatorUN']
    password = creds['operatorPass']

    request = urllib2.Request(URL + user)

    base64_authstring = base64.encodestring('{}:{}'.format(
        username, password)).replace('\n','')

    request.add_header("Authorization", "Basic " + base64_authstring)
    try:
        response = urllib2.urlopen(request)
    except urllib2.HTTPError as error:
        response = error

    raw_data = response.read()

    try:
        data = json.loads(raw_data)
    except:
        raise Exception("Could not parse response from Jira API")

    if 'errorMessages' in data:
        for error in data['errorMessages']:
            if error.find('does not exist'):
                output=None
    if 'name' in data:
        if data['active'] == True:
            output = "{} ({})".format(data['name'], data['displayName'])
        elif data['active'] == False:
            output = None
        else:
            logging.error("Cannot determine Jira user state. Check UI manually")

    return(output, user, creds)

def foundAccess(result):
    if result[0] is not None:
        accessChoice = result[2]['accessChoice']
        if accessChoice == 'check':
            print "{} has Jira access".format(result[1])
        if accessChoice == 'remove':
            print "{} has Jira access but automatic removal is not yet available. Please remove manually".format(result[1])

if __name__ == '__main__':
    import getpass

    operatorUN = raw_input('Input your username, to authenticate to Jira: ')
    operatorPass = getpass.getpass('Input your password: ')
    sepList = raw_input("Enter LDAP user to be separated. If multiple, separate by commas: ").split(',')
    accessChoice = raw_input("Would you like to check or remove access? Check/Remove: ").lower()

    while True:
        if accessChoice not in ('remove','check'):
            accessChoice = raw_input("Sorry, looks like you misspelled 'remove' or 'check'. Please re-indicate if you'd like to remove all access or just check access. Remove/Check: ").lower()
            continue
        else:
            accessChoice = accessChoice
            break

    inputDict = {}
    inputDict.update({'creds' : {'operatorUN': operatorUN, 'operatorPass': operatorPass, 'accessChoice' : accessChoice}})
    creds = inputDict['creds']

    for user in sepList:
        result = main(user, creds)
        foundAccess(result)

import logging
import pprint
import MySQLdb
import sys
import secret
DB_HOST = 'bppdb-master.marchex.com'
DB_USER = secret.get_secret('_PROD_MYSQL_USER')
DB_PASS = secret.get_secret('_PROD_MYSQL_PASS')
SQL_COMMANDS = {
    "check_for_user" : "SELECT name, email, status FROM microsite.users WHERE status NOT LIKE 'inactive' AND (email LIKE '%{username}%' OR name LIKE '%{username}%')",
    "deactivate" : "UPDATE microsite.users set status = 'inactive' where email = '{username}@marchex.com';",
    "deactivate_vendor" : "UPDATE microsite.users set status = 'inactive' where email = '{username}';"
}
def command_from_username(command, username):
    return SQL_COMMANDS[command].format(username=username)
def execute_mysql_command(db, query):
    try:
        cur = db.cursor()
        cur.execute(query)
        return cur.fetchall()
    except Exception as e:
        raise Exception("Error executing query in the microsites.py module: {}\n{}".format(query, str(e)))
    finally:
        cur.close()
def main(user, creds):
    output = None
    # Checks for vendor email. Proceeds as normal if value is None
    if creds['vendorEmail'] == None:
        username = user
    else:
        username = creds['vendorEmail']
    #connect to db
    try:
        db = MySQLdb.connect(host=DB_HOST, user=DB_USER, passwd=DB_PASS)
    except Exception as e:
        raise Exception("Could not connect to DB '{}' in the microsites.py module: {}".format(DB_HOST, str(e)))
    #check for user
    try:
        query_output = execute_mysql_command(db, command_from_username('check_for_user', username))
        if query_output:
            output = ['{} ({} status:{})'.format(row[0], row[1], row[2]) for row in query_output]
            return(output, username, creds)
        else:
            output=None
            return(output, username, creds)
    except Exception as e:
        raise Exception("DB Query failed: "+str(e))
#Printing logic for access/no access; continues to deactivate if desired
def foundAccess(result):
    if result[0] is not None:
        accessCheck = result[2]['accessChoice']
        if accessCheck == "check":
            print "{} has Microsite UI access".format(result[1])
        if accessCheck == "remove":
            deactivation(result)
#deactivation
def deactivation(result):
    username = result[1]
    #connect to db
    try:
        db = MySQLdb.connect(host=DB_HOST, user=DB_USER, passwd=DB_PASS)
    except Exception as e:
        raise Exception("Could not connect to DB '{}' for microsites removal for user {}: {}".format(DB_HOST,username, str(e)))
    #deactivate
    if result[2['vendorEmail']] == None:
        try:
            query_output = execute_mysql_command(db, command_from_username('deactivate',username))
        except Exception as e:
            raise Exception("DB command failed deactivating microsites access for {}\nError: : ".format(username,str(e)))
            db.rollback()
        else:
            db. commit()
    else:
        try:
            query_output = execute_mysql_command(db, command_from_username('deactivate_vendor',username))
        except Exception as e:
            raise Exception("DB command failed in microsites.py module: {} ".format(str(e)))
            db.rollback()
        else:
            db. commit()
    #recheck for user
    try:
        query_output = execute_mysql_command(db, command_from_username('check_for_user', username))
        if query_output:
            print "Something went wrong and {} was not deactivated. Please remove MicrositeUI access manually".format(username)
        else:
            print "Microsite Account Deactivated for {}".format(username)
    finally:
        db.close()
if __name__ == '__main__':
    print "Checking Microsite UI access"
    vendorEmail=None
    user = raw_input("Input username to check. If multiple, separate by commas: ").split(',')
    accessChoice = raw_input("Would you like to check or remove access? Check/Remove: ").lower()
    isVendor = raw_input("Is this user a vendor? Yes/No: ").lower()

    while isVendor not in ('yes', 'no'):
        isVendor = raw_input("Sorry, looks like you misspelled 'yes' or 'no' somehow. Is this user a vendor? Yes/No: ").lower()

    if isVendor == "yes":
        vendorEmail = raw_input("Enter vendor email address: ")

    while True:
        if accessChoice not in ('remove','check'):
            accessChoice = raw_input("Sorry, looks like you misspelled 'remove' or 'check'. Please re-indicate if you'd like to remove all access or just check access. Remove/Check: ").lower()
            continue
        else:
            accessChoice = accessChoice
            break
    inputDict = {}
    inputDict.update({'creds' : {'accessChoice' : accessChoice,'vendorEmail':vendorEmail}})

import logging
import pprint
import MySQLdb
import sys
import secret
sys.path.insert(1,'/site/socbot/scripts')
import dbaHostHelper

DB_HOSTS = dbaHostHelper.get_mysql_hosts() 

DB_USER = secret.get_secret('_PROD_MYSQL_USER')
DB_PASS = secret.get_secret('_PROD_MYSQL_PASS')

SQL_COMMANDS = {
    "findUser": "SELECT user FROM mysql.user WHERE user LIKE '%{username}';",
    "dropUser": "drop user {username};",
    "flush": "flush privileges;",
}

def command_from_username(command,user):
    return SQL_COMMANDS[command].format(username=user)

def execute_mysql_command(db, query):
    try:
        cur = db.cursor()
        cur.execute(query)
        output = cur.fetchall()
        return output
    except Exception as e:
        raise Exception("Error executing query in the mysql module: {}\n{}".format(query, str(e)))
    finally:
        cur.close()

def main(username,creds):
    output = None
    hostlist=[]
    del hostlist[:]
    for host in DB_HOSTS:
        try:
            db = MySQLdb.connect(host=host, user=DB_USER, passwd=DB_PASS)
        except Exception as e:
            logging.error("Could not connect to DB '{}' in the mysql module: {}".format(host, str(e)))
            continue
        try:
            query_output = execute_mysql_command(db, command_from_username('findUser', username))
        except Exception as e:
            logging.error("DB Query failed while checking for mysql_db access: "+str(e))
        finally:
            db.close()
        if query_output:
            hostlist.append(host)

    if len(hostlist) == 0:
        return(None, username, creds)
    else:
        return(hostlist,username,creds)
def foundAccess(result):
    accessChoice = result[2]['accessChoice']
    if result[0] is not None:
        if accessChoice == 'check':
            for host in result[0]:
                print "{} has account on {}".format(result[1],host)
        if accessChoice == 'remove':
            deactivation(result[0],result[1])

def deactivation(hostlist,username):

    for host in hostlist:
        try:
            db = MySQLdb.connect(host=host, user=DB_USER, passwd=DB_PASS)
        except Exception as e:
            logging.error("The following happened when connecting to {} in the mysql module: {}".format(host,str(e)))
            continue
        try:
            cont = raw_input("{} will be removed from  {}\nContinue (y/n)? (If no, changes will be rolled back): ".format(username,host))
            if cont == 'n':
                print("{} will NOT be removed from {}".format(username,host))
                continue
            else:
                if not execute_mysql_command(db, command_from_username('findUser', username)):
                    print("{} was already removed from {}".format(username,host))
                    continue
                execute_mysql_command(db, command_from_username('dropUser', username))
                execute_mysql_command(db, command_from_username('flush',username))
        except Exception as e:
            raise Exception("DB command failed while attempting to remove {} in the mysql module\nError: {}".format(username,str(e)))
            db.rollback()
        try:
            if not execute_mysql_command(db, command_from_username('findUser', username)):
                print "{} deactivated from {}".format(username,host)
            else:
                print("Something went wrong and {} was not deactivated. Please remove {} access manually".format(username,host))
        except Exception as e:
            logging.error("The following error occurred while attempting to deactivate {} on {}\nError: {}".format(username, host,e))

if __name__ == '__main__':
    user = raw_input("Input username to check: ")
    accessChoice = raw_input("Would you like to check or remove access? Check/Remove: ").lower()

    while True:
        if accessChoice not in ('remove','check'):
            accessChoice = raw_input("Sorry, looks like you misspelled 'remove' or 'check'. Please re-indicate if you'd like to remove all access or just check access. Remove/Check: ").lower()
            continue
        else:
            accessChoice = accessChoice
            break

    inputDict = {}
    inputDict.update({'creds' : {'accessChoice' : accessChoice}})
    creds = inputDict['creds']

    result = main(user,creds)
    foundAccess(result)

import logging
import os
import subprocess
import secret

DB_INSTANCES = ["OPNEXT",]

DB_USER = secret.get_secret('_ORACLE_USER')
DB_PASS = secret.get_secret('_ORACLE_PASS')

ENV = {
    'TNS_ADMIN': os.environ.get('TNS_ADMIN', '/site/socbot/.oracle'),
    'CLASSPATH': os.environ.get('CLASSPATH', '/site/oracle_client/client-10.2.0.3/jdbc/llib/classes12.jar'),
    'ORACLE_HOME': os.environ.get('ORACLE_HOME', '/site/oracle_client/client-10.2.0.3/'),
    'SQLPATH': os.environ.get('SQLPATH', '/site/socbot/.oracle'),
    'PATH': os.environ['PATH'] + ':/site/oracle_client/client-10.2.0.3/bin',
}

# Verifies that tnsnames.ora file exists
TNSNAMES = ENV['TNS_ADMIN']+'/tnsnames.ora'
if not os.path.isfile(TNSNAMES):
    raise Exception("No tnsnames found (Missing '{}')".format(TNSNAMES))

def main(username,creds):

    for instance in DB_INSTANCES:
        proc = subprocess.Popen(['sqlplus','-s'],
            stdin=subprocess.PIPE,
            stdout=subprocess.PIPE,
            stderr=subprocess.PIPE,
            env=ENV)
        try:
            (stdout, stderr) = proc.communicate(input=("{user}/{passw}@{instance}\n"
                "set pages 200\n"
                "set lines 200\n"
                "set serveroutput on\n"
                "set feedback off\n"
                "SELECT ID, USERNAME, EMAIL, STATUS FROM COMMON.USERS WHERE USERNAME ='{username}';\n"
                ).format(
                    user=DB_USER,
                    passw=DB_PASS,
                    instance=instance,
                    username=username))
        except Exception as e:
            print("Failed to check and connect to opnext in nimui.py module for user {}\nError: {}".format(username,e))

        return(instance, stdout, username, creds)

def foundAccess(result):
    r = result
    if len(r[1]) > 1:
        accessChoice = r[3]['accessChoice']
        if accessChoice == "check":
            print "{} has nimUI access".format(result[2])
        if accessChoice == "remove":
            print "{} has nimUI access, but automatic removal not yet available for this check, please remove manually".format(result[2])

if __name__ == '__main__':
    sepList = raw_input("Enter LDAP user to be separated. If multiple, separate by commas: ").split(',')
    accessChoice = raw_input("Would you like to check or remove access? Check/Remove: ").lower()

    while True:
        if accessChoice not in ('remove','check'):
            accessChoice = raw_input("Sorry, looks like you misspelled 'remove' or 'check'. Please re-indicate if you'd like to remove all access or just check access. Remove/Check: ").lower()
            continue
        else:
            accessChoice = accessChoice
            break

    inputDict = {}
    inputDict.update({'creds' : {'accessChoice' : accessChoice}})
    creds = inputDict['creds']

    for user in sepList:
        result = main(user,creds)
        foundAccess(result)
import logging
import os
import subprocess
import sys
import secret
sys.path.insert(1,'/site/socbot/scripts')
import dbaHostHelper

DB_INSTANCES = dbaHostHelper.get_oracl_hosts()

DB_USER = secret.get_secret('_ORACLE_USER')
DB_PASS = secret.get_secret('_ORACLE_PASS')

ENV = {
	'TNS_ADMIN': os.environ.get('TNS_ADMIN', '/site/socbot/.oracle'),
	'CLASSPATH': os.environ.get('CLASSPATH', '/site/oracle_client/client-10.2.0.3/jdbc/llib/classes12.jar'),
	'ORACLE_HOME': os.environ.get('ORACLE_HOME', '/site/oracle_client/client-10.2.0.3/'),
	'SQLPATH': os.environ.get('SQLPATH', '/site/socbot/.oracle'),
	'PATH': os.environ['PATH'] + ':/site/oracle_client/client-10.2.0.3/bin',
}

# Verifies that tnsnames.ora file exists
TNSNAMES = ENV['TNS_ADMIN']+'/tnsnames.ora'
if not os.path.isfile(TNSNAMES):
    raise Exception("No tnsnames found (Missing '{}')".format(TNSNAMES))

def main(username,creds):
    for instance in DB_INSTANCES:
        proc = subprocess.Popen(['sqlplus','-s'],
            stdin=subprocess.PIPE,
            stdout=subprocess.PIPE,
            stderr=subprocess.PIPE,
            env=ENV)
        (stdout, stderr) = proc.communicate(input=("{user}/{passw}@{instance}\n"
            "set pages 200\n"
            "set lines 200\n"
            "set serveroutput on\n"
            "set feedback off\n"
            "exec USRADM.QUERY_USER('{username}');\n"
            ).format(
                user=DB_USER,
                passw=DB_PASS,
                instance=instance,
                username=username))

        if stderr:
            logging.error("Error in command on database {}: {}".format(instance, stderr))
            if stdout:
                logging.warn("Stdout was: " + str(stdout))
        if not stdout:
            logging.error("Error in command on database {}: no output to STDOUT".format(instance))
        if 'not found' in stdout:
            yield [instance, None, username, creds]
        else:
            yield [instance, stdout, username, creds]

def foundAccess(result):
    for r in result:
        if r[1] is not None:
            accessChoice = r[3]['accessChoice']
            if accessChoice == "check":
                print "User has '{}' access".format(r[0])
            if accessChoice == "remove":
                print " User has '{}' access, but automatic removal not yet available for this check, please remove manually".format(r[0])

if __name__ == '__main__':
    sepList = raw_input("Enter LDAP user to be separated. If multiple, separate by commas: ").split(',')
    accessChoice = raw_input("Would you like to check or remove access? Check/Remove: ").lower()

    while True:
        if accessChoice not in ('remove','check'):
            accessChoice = raw_input("Sorry, looks like you misspelled 'remove' or 'check'. Please re-indicate if you'd like to remove all access or just check access. Remove/Check: ").lower()
            continue
        else:
            accessChoice = accessChoice
            break



    inputDict = {}
    inputDict.update({'creds' : {'accessChoice' : accessChoice}})
    creds = inputDict['creds']

    for user in sepList:
        result = main(user,creds)
        foundAccess(result)

next is pagerduty.py


import logging
import sys
import urllib2
import urllib
import json
import pprint
import secret

# PagerDuty Documentation:
# https://developer.pagerduty.com/documentation/rest/users/list

# v2 api key & URL
API_KEY = secret.get_secret("_PAGERDUTY_API_KEY")
URL = "https://api.pagerduty.com/users"

def main(user, creds):
    if creds['vendorEmail'] is not None:
        r = creds['vendorEmail'].split('@')
        username=r[0]
    else:
        username = user

    params = urllib.urlencode({'query': username})
    request = urllib2.Request(URL + '?' + params)
    request.add_header("Authorization", "Token token=" + API_KEY)
    request.add_header("Accept", "application/vnd.pagerduty+json;version=2")

    try:
        response = urllib2.urlopen(request)
    except urllib2.HTTPError as error:
        response = error

    raw_data = response.read()
    try:
        data = json.loads(raw_data)
    except:
        raise Exception("Could not parse response from Pagerduty API")

    try:
        variable = data['users']
        if variable:
            return(variable, username, creds)
        else:
            variable = None
            return (variable, username, creds)
    except KeyError:
        raise Exception("Unexpected result from PagerDuty API:" + str(data))

def foundAccess(result):
    if result[0] is not None:
        accessChoice = result[2]['accessChoice']

        if accessChoice == "check":
            print "{} found in PagerDuty".format(result[1])
        if accessChoice == "remove":
            print "{} was found in PagerDuty, but automatic removal is not yet available. Please remove manually".format(result[1])

if __name__ == '__main__':
    print "Checking Pagerduty access"
    vendorEmail=None
    sepList = raw_input("Enter LDAP user to be separated. If multiple, separate by commas: ").split(',')
    isVendor = raw_input("Is this user a vendor? Yes/No: ").lower()

    while isVendor not in ('yes', 'no'):
        isVendor = raw_input("Sorry, looks like you misspelled 'yes' or 'no' somehow. Is this user a vendor? Yes/No: ").lower()

    if isVendor == "yes":
        vendorEmail = raw_input("Enter vendor email address: ")

    accessChoice = raw_input("Would you like to check or remove access? Check/Remove: ").lower()

    while True:
        if accessChoice not in ('remove', 'check'):
            accessChoice = raw_input("Sorry, looks like you misspelled 'remove' or 'check'. Please re-indicate if "
                                     "you'd like to remove all access or just check access. Remove/Check: ").lower()
            continue
        else:
            accessChoice = accessChoice
            break

    inputDict = {}
    inputDict.update({'creds': {'accessChoice': accessChoice,'vendorEmail':vendorEmail}})
    creds = inputDict['creds']

    for user in sepList:
        result = main(user, creds)
        foundAccess(result)

DB_USER = secret.get_secret('_PROD_POSTGRES_USER')
DB_PASS = secret.get_secret('_PROD_POSTGRES_PASS')

DB_QUERY = "select usename from pg_catalog.pg_user where usename LIKE '%{user}%'"

def connect_to_db(host,port,dbname):
    conn = psycopg2.connect(host=host,
                port=port,
                dbname=dbname,
                user=DB_USER,
                password=DB_PASS)

    cur=conn.cursor()
    
    return(cur,conn)

def main(user, creds):
    sql = DB_QUERY.format(user=user)

    dbs=[]
    del dbs[:]
    for host in HOST_LIST:
        try:
            connections = connect_to_db(
					DB_HOSTS[host].get('host',''),
                    DB_HOSTS[host].get('port',5432),
                    DB_HOSTS[host].get('dbname','')
                    )

            cur = connections[0]
            conn = connections[1]
            cur.execute(sql)
        except KeyError:
            print "{} not in host list, please investigate".format(host)
            continue
        except Exception as e:
            print("DB Query failed: "+str(e))

        rows = cur.fetchall()
        # Close DB communication
        cur.close()
        conn.close()

        if rows:
                dbs.append(DB_HOSTS[host]['host'])
    return(dbs, user, creds)

def foundAccess(result):
    accessChoice = result[2]['accessChoice']
    if len(result[0]) > 0:
        if accessChoice == "check":
            for db in result[0]:
                print "User has account on '{}'".format(db)
        if accessChoice == "remove":
            revokeAccess(result)

def revokeAccess(result):
    databases=result[0]
    user=result[1]
    sql = DB_QUERY.format(user=user)

    for db in databases:
        for v in DB_HOSTS[db]:
            connections = connect_to_db(
                    DB_HOSTS[db].get('host',''),
                    DB_HOSTS[db].get('port',5432),
                    DB_HOSTS[db].get('dbname',''),
                    v)
            cur = connections[0]
            conn = connections[1]


            cont = raw_input("{} will be removed from {}, continue (y/n)? If you select 'n', the user will NOT be removed ".format(user,db)).lower()
            if cont == "n":
                print "{} was not removed from {}".format(user,db)
                continue
            else:
                try:
                    cur.execute("DROP USER {};".format(user))
                    cur.execute("commit;")
                    cur.execute(sql)
                    rows = cur.fetchall()
                    cur.close()
                    conn.close()

                    if not rows:
                        print "{} has been successfully removed from {}".format(user,db)
                    else:
                        print "Something went wrong and {} was not removed from {}. Please remove manually".format(user,db)

                except Exception as e:
                    print(e)
                    cur.close()
                    conn.close()

if __name__ == '__main__':
    print "Checking PostgreSQL DB access"
    sepList = raw_input("Enter LDAP user to be separated. If multiple, separate by commas: ").split(',')
    accessChoice = raw_input("Would you like to check or remove access? Check/Remove: ").lower()

    while True:
        if accessChoice not in ('remove','check'):
            accessChoice = raw_input("Sorry, looks like you misspelled 'remove' or 'check'. Please re-indicate if you'd like to remove all access or just check access. Remove/Check: ").lower()
            continue
        else:
            accessChoice = accessChoice
            break

    inputDict = {}

next is RT_tickets.py




import secret
import rt
from rt_marchex import rtbroker

RT_USER = secret.get_secret('_SOC_UI_USER')
RT_PASS = secret.get_secret('_SOC_UI_PASS')

RT_HOST = 'https://rt.marchex.com'
RT_URL = 'https://rt.marchex.com/REST/1.0'

RT_QUERY = ("Owner = '{user}' "
            "AND ( Status = 'new' OR Status = 'open')")

def main(user, creds):
    rtb = rtbroker(RT_HOST)
    rtb.loginUser(RT_USER, RT_PASS)

    tickets = rtb.ticket_search(RT_USER, RT_QUERY.format(user=user))

    if tickets:
        return(tickets, user, creds)
    else:
        tickets = None
        return(tickets, user, creds)

def foundAccess(result):
    if result[0] is not None:
        accessChoice = result[2]['accessChoice']
        if accessChoice == "check":
            print "RT Tickets found for {}:".format(result[1])
            for key, val in result[0].iteritems():
                print '{}: {}\n'.format(key, val)
        if accessChoice == "remove":
            stealTicket(result)

def loginToRT():
    tracker=rt.Rt(RT_URL, RT_USER, RT_PASS)
    if not tracker.login():
        print "Failed to log in to RT"
        return False
    else:
        return tracker

def stealTicket(results):
    tracker = loginToRT()
    for key in results[0].keys():
        try:
            tracker.edit_ticket(key, Queue='SOC')
            tracker.steal(key)
            tracker.edit_ticket(key, Owner=RT_USER, Queue='Production')
            print "The following RT tickets have been taken:"
        except:
            print "Sorry, something went wrong. The following RT tickets could not be taken from {}:".format(results[1])
    for key, val in tickets[0].iteritems():
        print '{}: {}\n'.format(key, val)

if __name__ == '__main__':
    print "Checking RT Tickets"
    sepList = raw_input("Enter LDAP user to be separated. If multiple, separate by commas: ").split(',')
    accessChoice = raw_input("Would you like to check or remove access? Check/Remove: ").lower()

    while True:
        if accessChoice not in ('remove','check'):
            accessChoice = raw_input("Sorry, looks like you misspelled 'remove' or 'check'. Please re-indicate if you'd like to remove all access or just check access. Remove/Check: ").lower()
            continue
        else:
            accessChoice = accessChoice
            break

    inputDict = {}
    inputDict.update({'creds' : {'accessChoice' : accessChoice }})
    creds = inputDict['creds']

    for user in sepList:
        result = main(user, creds)
        foundAccess(result)

Edit

Matt Wiesemann
Feb 13

If person being separated (or transitioned) is a SOC operator,
make sure to change the master Bitwarden password. This application is
external facing. Send the new password to all existing SOC operators
from your personal Marchex account.

Description
* This SOP outlines steps necessary to remove access from a separated
employee.

The separation script is designed to check/remove internal users
(LDAP/*@marchex.com) permissions.
If a separation ticket includes a non-Marchex email address you will
have to check Adtrack manually.
Assign the ticket to the Swing shift operator to run.
Last3 isn't handled by the SOC. When the employee is removed from
LDAP by Corp IT they will lose Last3 access
LDAP NISMaps - CORP IT will be handling this as part of their sep
SOP as of 3/18/21.
Note about some vendors:
'Microsourcing' and 'Wildnet Technologies' vendors have no AD (active
directory) account and therefore no LDAP account either. They are only
given an SMTP pointer in the GAL for their external mail address. They
may have one-off, non-AD/LDAP-related accesses to things like Adtrack,
so those should still be checked during your separation processes.

Separation Steps
1. What type of separation is this?

 First check to see if this ticket says (UPDATE) OR (REVISION) OR (something else that makes you think there may already be a ticket).  
If there is then merge them, or resolve the first one, or take an appropriate action so they aren't both out in the wild.

 Get the User's alias and manager name and put it into the ticket. -- Check https://directorymanager.marchex.com/` '''Directory Manager'''  to check for LDAP alias.  

 If this is NOT an immediate` separation, pass the ticket to Kamran with BPO and he will divvy them up to night shift.  
 If this IS an immediate` separation, complete the ticket ASAP. 

2. Go to the soc tools
UI 

3. Click SOC Separation Tool

Check for Tickets to find previous access
Check new hire ticket for user
You may also be able to find tickets with their username/alias in
the subject requesting access
Example Ticket Subject... Access Request: Jira for rkumar
If you find any tickets with access that needs to remove by the SOC:
UIs that need to be removed steps can be found here:
uiAccess 
Database hosts that need to be removed can be found here
(just do a "find" to figure out what kind):
databaseAccess 
Hosts that might need to be removed Hosts
Access 
Other Manual Checks:
RT Tickets

Go here to Query
RT 
On the left hand side, you'll see "owner is"
Check the pulldown, if the user isn't there then they don't
own any RTs & you are down with the RT checks
If they are in the pulldown
Select their name in the pulldown
On the line above their name select "Status is" and OPEN
click "add these terms and search" below the box
TACACS (tac-plus)

Cut a sev5 ticket to Neteng for the removal
Manually check and remove access from Grafana
Grafana 

Manually check and remove access from Chef:
Chef 

Manually check and remove access from Wallace
Wallace 

Manually check and remove access from XMS Hammer
XMSHammer 

Manually check and remove Auth0 access''':
Auth0 

Manually check and remove access to AWS
AWS 

Manually check and remove access to PagerDuty
PagerDuty 

Manually check and remove Slack Access:
Slack 

Manually check and remove Jira:
Jira 

Manually check and remove Snowflake:
Snowflake

import logging
import getpass
import ldap
import utils
from concurrent.futures import ThreadPoolExecutor

# Setup logging
logging.basicConfig(
    format='%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s',
    level=logging.INFO
)

# Systems that require separation processing
SYSTEMS_CATALOG = {
    "AdTrack": True,
    "AFR": True,
    "Auth0": True,
    "Avenger": True,
    "AWS": True,
    "ADO": True,
    "AzurePortal": True,
    "CallScoring": True,
    "Chef": True,
    "Cuttlefish": True,
    "EmailAccess": True,
    "Engage": True,
    "EquityEdge_GreatPlains": True,
    "GitHub": True,
    "Grafana": True,
    "Ipplan": True,
    "JIRA": True,
    "Marchex.io": True,
    "MI5": True,
    "Microsites": True,
    "NewRelic": True,
    "Nexus": True,
    "NimUI": True,
    "NISMaps": True,
    "OpenVPN": True,
    "PagerDuty": True,
    "Pulley": True,
    "Postman": True,
    "RT": True,
    "Slack": True,
    "MarketingEdge": True,
    "Sendgrid": True,
    "Sentry": True,
    "Snowflake": True,
    "Wallace": True,
    "XMSHammer": True
}

ACCESS_LIST = [system for system, enabled in SYSTEMS_CATALOG.items() if enabled]
MISSING_SCRIPTS = []

# LDAP Configurations
LDAP_ADDR = 'ldaps://ldap.sea.marchex.com:636/'
LDAP_BASEDN = 'ou=users,dc=marchex,dc=com'
LDAP_BINDDN = 'uid={user},ou=users,dc=marchex,dc=com'
LDAP_SF = '(cn={user})'

# Don't require signed cert for LDAP connection
ldap.set_option(ldap.OPT_X_TLS_REQUIRE_CERT, ldap.OPT_X_TLS_NEVER)


def get_user_input(prompt):
    """Wrapper for input to handle common input scenarios."""
    try:
        return input(prompt).strip()
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Error getting user input: {e}")
        return None


def main():
    """ Main function for the separation script. """
    logging.info("########### SEPARATION SCRIPT #############")

    operatorUN = get_user_input("Enter your LDAP username: ")
    operatorPass = getpass.getpass("Enter your LDAP password: ")

    # Gather usernames to be separated
    sepList = get_user_input("Enter LDAP user(s) to be separated (comma-separated): ").split(',')

    # Check if user is a vendor
    while True:
        isVendor = get_user_input("Is this user a vendor? (yes/no): ").lower()
        if isVendor in ('yes', 'no'):
            break
        logging.warning("Invalid input. Please enter 'yes' or 'no'.")

    vendorEmail = None
    if isVendor == "yes":
        if any(sys in ACCESS_LIST for sys in ["PagerDuty", "Microsites"]):
            vendorEmail = get_user_input("Enter vendor email address: ")
        else:
            logging.info("Vendor email not needed for selected systems.")

    # Ask if we are checking or removing access
    while True:
        accessChoice = get_user_input("Would you like to remove all found access or just check access? (Remove/Check): ").lower()
        if accessChoice in ('remove', 'check'):
            break
        logging.warning("Invalid input. Please enter 'Remove' or 'Check'.")

    creds = {
        "operatorUN": operatorUN,
        "operatorPass": operatorPass,
        "sepList": sepList,
        "accessChoice": accessChoice,
        "vendorEmail": vendorEmail
    }

    try:
        ldp = ldap.initialize(LDAP_ADDR)
        ldp.simple_bind_s(LDAP_BINDDN.format(user=operatorUN), operatorPass)
    except ldap.INVALID_CREDENTIALS:
        logging.error("LDAP authentication failed. Exiting.")
        return
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Unexpected LDAP error: {e}")
        return

    # Run separations in parallel using multi-threading
    with ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=5) as executor:
        executor.map(lambda user: process_user(ldp, user, creds), sepList)

    logging.info(f"####### No further access found for {user} #######")

    if MISSING_SCRIPTS:
        logging.warning(f"Missing separation scripts: {', '.join(set(MISSING_SCRIPTS))}")


def ldapQuery(ldp, user):
    """Check if user exists in LDAP and return user information."""
    logging.info(f"Checking LDAP access for {user}...")
    try:
        result_id = ldp.search(LDAP_BASEDN, ldap.SCOPE_SUBTREE, LDAP_SF.format(user=user))
        result_type, result_data = ldp.result(result_id, 0)

        if not result_data:
            logging.warning(f"User {user} not found in LDAP.")
            return False

        user_data = result_data[0][1]
        logging.info(f"""
        User information from LDAP:
        First Name: {user_data.get('givenName', ['Undefined'])[0]}
        Last Name:  {user_data.get('sn', ['Undefined'])[0]}
        Manager:    {user_data.get('manager', ['Undefined'])[0]}
        """)
        return True

    except ldap.LDAPError as e:
        logging.error(f"LDAP query failed for {user}: {e}")
        return False


def checkAccess(user, creds):
    global MISSING_SCRIPTS  # Track missing scripts across all users
    logging.info(f"Checking access for {user}...")

    for system in ACCESS_LIST:
        try:
            sep_module = __import__(f"separations.{system.lower()}", fromlist=[""])
            sep_result = sep_module.main(user, creds)
            sep_module.foundAccess(sep_result)
        except ImportError:
            MISSING_SCRIPTS.append(system)
        except Exception as e:
            logging.error(f"Error running {system} separation: {e}")


def process_user(user, creds):
    try:
        ldp = ldap.initialize(LDAP_ADDR)
        ldp.simple_bind_s(LDAP_BINDDN.format(user=creds["operatorUN"]), creds["operatorPass"])

        if ldapQuery(ldp, user):
            checkAccess(user, creds)
        logging.info(f"####### No further access found for {user} #######")

    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Error processing user {user}: {e}")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

LDAP_BASEDN = 'ou=users,dc=marchex,dc=com'
