# High Priority Contact List Location
HIGH_PRI_FILE = r'\\marchex\files\soc\Emergency\High Priority Contact List\NOCHighPriorityContactList1.xlsx'

# Don't require signed cert for LDAP connection
ldap.set_option(ldap.OPT_X_TLS_REQUIRE_CERT, ldap.OPT_X_TLS_NEVER)


def get_user_input(prompt):
    """Wrapper for input to handle common input scenarios."""
    try:
        return input(prompt).strip()
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Error getting user input: {e}")
        return None


def get_directory_info(user):
    """Query Directory Manager for user alias & manager name."""
    directory_url = f"https://directorymanager.marchex.com/api/user/{user}"
    try:
        response = requests.get(directory_url)
        response.raise_for_status()
        user_data = response.json()
        return user_data.get('alias', 'Unknown'), user_data.get('manager', 'Unknown')
    except Exception as e:
        logging.warning(f"Failed to retrieve Directory Manager info for {user}: {e}")
        return 'Unknown', 'Unknown'


def check_high_priority_contact_list(user):
    """Check and remove user from High Priority Contact List."""
    if not os.path.exists(HIGH_PRI_FILE):
        logging.warning("High Priority Contact List file not found.")
        return
    
    try:
        wb = openpyxl.load_workbook(HIGH_PRI_FILE)
        sheet = wb.active
        for row in sheet.iter_rows():
            for cell in row:
                if str(user).lower() in str(cell.value).lower():
                    logging.info(f"Removing {user} from High Priority Contact List.")
                    cell.value = None
                    wb.save(HIGH_PRI_FILE)
                    return
        logging.info(f"{user} not found in High Priority Contact List.")
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Error modifying High Priority Contact List: {e}")


def main():
    """ Main function for the separation script. """
    logging.info("########### SEPARATION SCRIPT #############")

    operatorUN = get_user_input("Enter your LDAP username: ")
    operatorPass = getpass.getpass("Enter your LDAP password: ")

    # Gather usernames to be separated
    sepList = get_user_input("Enter LDAP user(s) to be separated (comma-separated): ").split(',')

    # Check if user is a vendor
    while True:
        isVendor = get_user_input("Is this user a vendor? (yes/no): ").lower()
        if isVendor in ('yes', 'no'):
            break

            vendorEmail = get_user_input("Enter vendor email address: ")
        else:
            logging.info("Vendor email not needed for selected systems.")

    # Ask if we are checking or removing access
    while True:
        accessChoice = get_user_input("Would you like to remove all found access or just check access? (Remove/Check): ").lower()
        if accessChoice in ('remove', 'check'):
            break
        logging.warning("Invalid input. Please enter 'Remove' or 'Check'.")

    creds = {
        "operatorUN": operatorUN,
        "operatorPass": operatorPass,
        "sepList": sepList,
        "accessChoice": accessChoice,
        "vendorEmail": vendorEmail
    }

    try:
        ldp = ldap.initialize(LDAP_ADDR)
        ldp.simple_bind_s(LDAP_BINDDN.format(user=operatorUN), operatorPass)
    except ldap.INVALID_CREDENTIALS:
        logging.error("LDAP authentication failed. Exiting.")
        return
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Unexpected LDAP error: {e}")

    if MISSING_SCRIPTS:
        logging.warning(f"Missing separation scripts: {', '.join(set(MISSING_SCRIPTS))}")


def process_user(ldp, user, creds):
    """Process separation for an individual user."""
    try:
        alias, manager = get_directory_info(user)
        logging.info(f"User {user} Alias: {alias}, Manager: {manager}")

        if ldapQuery(ldp, user):
            checkAccess(user, creds)

        check_high_priority_contact_list(user)

        logging.info(f"####### No further access found for {user} #######")

    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Error processing user {user}: {e}")


def ldapQuery(ldp, user):
    """Check if user exists in LDAP."""
    logging.info(f"Checking LDAP access for {user}...")
    try:
        result_id = ldp.search(LDAP_BASEDN, ldap.SCOPE_SUBTREE, LDAP_SF.format(user=user))
        result_type, result_data = ldp.result(result_id, 0)
        if not result_data:
            logging.warning(f"User {user} not found in LDAP.")
            return False
        return True
    except ldap.LDAPError as e:
        logging.error(f"LDAP query failed for {user}: {e}")
        return False


def checkAccess(user, creds):
    """Run access removal scripts."""
    global MISSING_SCRIPTS 
    logging.info(f"Checking access for {user}...")

    for system in ACCESS_LIST:
        try:
            sep_module = __import__(f"separations.{system.lower()}", fromlist=[""])
            sep_module.main(user, creds)
        except ImportError:
            MISSING_SCRIPTS.append(system)
        except Exception as e:
            logging.error(f"Error running {system} separation: {e}")


if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

# Systems that require separation processing
SYSTEMS_CATALOG = {

# LDAP Configurations
LDAP_ADDR = 'ldaps://ldap.sea.marchex.com:636/'
LDAP_BASEDN = 'ou=users,dc=marchex,dc=com'
LDAP_BINDDN = 'uid={user},ou=users,dc=marchex,dc=com'
LDAP_SF = '(cn={user})'

# RT (Request Tracker) Configuration
RT_HOST = 'https://rt.marchex.com'
RT_URL = 'https://rt.marchex.com/REST/1.0'
RT_USER = "socbot"  # Replace with actual RT user
RT_PASS = "securepass"  # Replace with actual RT password

# High Priority Contact List Location
HIGH_PRI_FILE = r'\\marchex\files\soc\Emergency\High Priority Contact List\NOCHighPriorityContactList1.xlsx'

# Don't require signed cert for LDAP connection
ldap.set_option(ldap.OPT_X_TLS_REQUIRE_CERT, ldap.OPT_X_TLS_NEVER)


def get_user_input(prompt):
    """Wrapper for input to handle common input scenarios."""
    try:
        return input(prompt).strip()
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Error getting user input: {e}")
        return None


def get_directory_info(user):
    """Query Directory Manager for user alias & manager name."""
    directory_url = f"https://directorymanager.marchex.com/api/user/{user}"
    try:
        response = requests.get(directory_url)
        response.raise_for_status()
        user_data = response.json()
        return user_data.get('alias', 'Unknown'), user_data.get('manager', 'Unknown')
    except Exception as e:
        logging.warning(f"Failed to retrieve Directory Manager info for {user}: {e}")
        return 'Unknown', 'Unknown'


def check_rt_for_access_tickets(user):
    """Check RT (Request Tracker) for past access requests related to this user."""
    logging.info(f"Checking RT for past access requests related to {user}...")
    query = f"Owner = '{user}' AND (Status = 'new' OR Status = 'open')"
    tracker = rt.Rt(RT_URL, RT_USER, RT_PASS)
    if not tracker.login():
        logging.error("Failed to authenticate with RT.")
        return
    try:
        tickets = tracker.search(Queue="SOC", raw_query=query)
        if tickets:
            logging.info(f"User {user} has {len(tickets)} past access tickets in RT.")
            for ticket in tickets:
                logging.info(f"RT Ticket Found: {ticket['id']} - {ticket['Subject']}")
        else:
            logging.info(f"No previous access tickets found in RT for {user}.")
    except Exception as e:
        logging.warning(f"Error checking RT for {user}: {e}")


def check_high_priority_contact_list(user):
    """Check and remove user from High Priority Contact List."""
    if not os.path.exists(HIGH_PRI_FILE):
        logging.warning("High Priority Contact List file not found.")
        return
    try:
        wb = openpyxl.load_workbook(HIGH_PRI_FILE)
        sheet = wb.active
        for row in sheet.iter_rows():
            for cell in row:
                if str(user).lower() in str(cell.value).lower():
                    logging.info(f"Removing {user} from High Priority Contact List.")
                    cell.value = None
                    wb.save(HIGH_PRI_FILE)
                    return
        logging.info(f"{user} not found in High Priority Contact List.")
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Error modifying High Priority Contact List: {e}")


def submit_sev5_ticket_for_TACACS(user):
    """Submit a SEV5 ticket to NetEng for TACACS removal."""
    logging.info(f"Submitting SEV5 ticket for TACACS removal for {user}.")
    
    # Simulated API request
    ticket_payload = {
        "summary": f"SEV5 - Remove TACACS access for {user}",
        "description": f"User {user} requires TACACS access removal as part of separation.",
        "priority": "SEV5",
        "assigned_team": "NetEng"
    }
    try:
        response = requests.post("https://ticketing.marchex.com/api/tickets", json=ticket_payload)
        response.raise_for_status()
        logging.info(f"SEV5 ticket successfully created for TACACS removal: {response.json().get('ticket_id')}")
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Failed to create SEV5 ticket for TACACS: {e}")


def main():
    """ Main function for the separation script. """
    logging.info("########### SEPARATION SCRIPT #############")
    operatorUN = get_user_input("Enter your LDAP username: ")
    operatorPass = getpass.getpass("Enter your LDAP password: ")

    # Gather usernames to be separated
    sepList = get_user_input("Enter LDAP user(s) to be separated (comma-separated): ").split(',')

    # Check if user is a vendor
    while True:
        isVendor = get_user_input("Is this user a vendor? (yes/no): ").lower()
        if isVendor in ('yes', 'no'):
            break
        logging.warning("Invalid input. Please enter 'yes' or 'no'.")
    vendorEmail = None
    if isVendor == "yes":
        if any(sys in ACCESS_LIST for sys in ["PagerDuty", "Microsites"]):
            vendorEmail = get_user_input("Enter vendor email address: ")
        else:
            logging.info("Vendor email not needed for selected systems.")

    # Ask if we are checking or removing access
    while True:
        accessChoice = get_user_input("Would you like to remove all found access or just check access? (Remove/Check): ").lower()
        if accessChoice in ('remove', 'check'):
            break
        logging.warning("Invalid input. Please enter 'Remove' or 'Check'.")
    creds = {
        "operatorUN": operatorUN,
        "operatorPass": operatorPass,
        "sepList": sepList,
        "accessChoice": accessChoice,
        "vendorEmail": vendorEmail
    }
    try:
        ldp = ldap.initialize(LDAP_ADDR)
        ldp.simple_bind_s(LDAP_BINDDN.format(user=operatorUN), operatorPass)
    except ldap.INVALID_CREDENTIALS:
        logging.error("LDAP authentication failed. Exiting.")
        return
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Unexpected LDAP error: {e}")
        return
    with ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=5) as executor:
        executor.map(lambda user: process_user(ldp, user, creds), sepList)
    logging.info(f"####### No further access found for {user} #######")
    if MISSING_SCRIPTS:
        logging.warning(f"Missing separation scripts: {', '.join(set(MISSING_SCRIPTS))}")


def process_user(ldp, user, creds):
    """Process separation for an individual user."""
    try:
        alias, manager = get_directory_info(user)
        logging.info(f"User {user} Alias: {alias}, Manager: {manager}")
        check_rt_for_access_tickets(user)
        if ldapQuery(ldp, user):
            checkAccess(user, creds)
        check_high_priority_contact_list(user)
        if "TACACS" in ACCESS_LIST:
            submit_sev5_ticket_for_TACACS(user)
        logging.info(f"####### No further access found for {user} #######")
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Error processing user {user}: {e}")


def ldapQuery(ldp, user):
    """Check if user exists in LDAP."""
    logging.info(f"Checking LDAP access for {user}...")
    try:
        result_id = ldp.search(LDAP_BASEDN, ldap.SCOPE_SUBTREE, LDAP_SF.format(user=user))
        result_type, result_data = ldp.result(result_id, 0)
        if not result_data:
            logging.warning(f"User {user} not found in LDAP.")
            return False
        return True
    except ldap.LDAPError as e:
        logging.error(f"LDAP query failed for {user}: {e}")
        return False


def checkAccess(user, creds):
    """Run access removal scripts."""
    global MISSING_SCRIPTS 
    logging.info(f"Checking access for {user}...")
    for system in ACCESS_LIST:
        try:
            sep_module = __import__(f"separations.{system.lower()}", fromlist=[""])
            sep_module.main(user, creds)
        except ImportError:
            MISSING_SCRIPTS.append(system)
        except Exception as e:
            logging.error(f"Error running {system} separation: {e}")


if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

import logging
import psycopg2
import secret

# Setup logging
logging.basicConfig(
    format="%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s",
    level=logging.INFO
)

# Database configuration
DB_CONFIG = {
    "dbname": "adtrack_ro",
    "host": "vspool.som1.marchex.com",
    "port": 5432,
    "user": secret.get_secret("_ADTRACK_DB_USER"),
    "password": secret.get_secret("_ADTRACK_DB_PASS")
}

def get_db_connection():
    """Establish a connection to the AdTrack database."""
    try:
        conn = psycopg2.connect(**DB_CONFIG)
        return conn
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Database connection failed: {e}")
        return None

def main(user, creds):
    """Check or remove AdTrack access for a given user."""
    if creds["vendorEmail"]:
        query = "SELECT email FROM at_user WHERE email ILIKE %s AND status != 'disabled'"
        search_param = creds["vendorEmail"]
    else:
        query = "SELECT email FROM at_user WHERE email ILIKE %s AND status != 'disabled'"
        search_param = f"{user}@marchex%"

    conn = get_db_connection()
    if not conn:
        return None, user, creds

    try:
        with conn.cursor() as cur:
            cur.execute(query, (search_param,))
            rows = cur.fetchall()

        conn.close()
        return [row[0] for row in rows] if rows else None, user, creds

    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Database query failed: {e}")
        return None, user, creds

def remove_access(user):
    """Attempt to remove user access from AdTrack."""
    conn = get_db_connection()
    if not conn:
        return

    delete_query = "UPDATE at_user SET status = 'disabled' WHERE email ILIKE %s"
    try:
        with conn.cursor() as cur:
            cur.execute(delete_query, (f"{user}@marchex%",))
            conn.commit()
        logging.info(f"Access removed for {user} in AdTrack.")

    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Failed to remove AdTrack access for {user}: {e}")

    finally:
        conn.close()

def foundAccess(result):
    """Handle access check and potential removal."""
    if result[0]:
        user = result[1]
        accessChoice = result[2]["accessChoice"]

        if accessChoice == "check":
            logging.info(f"{user} has AdTrack UI access.")
        elif accessChoice == "remove":
            logging.info(f"{user} has AdTrack UI access. Attempting removal...")
            remove_access(user)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    sepList = input("Enter LDAP user(s) to be separated (comma-separated): ").split(",")
    accessChoice = input("Would you like to check or remove access? (Check/Remove): ").lower()
    isVendor = input("Is this user a vendor? (Yes/No): ").lower()

    vendorEmail = None
    if isVendor == "yes":
        vendorEmail = input("Enter vendor email address: ")

    creds = {"accessChoice": accessChoice, "vendorEmail": vendorEmail}

    for user in sepList:
        result = main(user.strip(), creds)
        foundAccess(result)

import logging
import getpass
import ldap
import utils
import requests
import openpyxl
import os
import json
import rt
from concurrent.futures import ThreadPoolExecutor

# Setup logging
logging.basicConfig(
    format='%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s',
    level=logging.INFO
)

# Systems that require separation processing
SYSTEMS_CATALOG = {
    "AdTrack": True,
    "AFR": True,
    "Auth0": True,
    "Avenger": True,
    "AWS": True,
    "ADO": True,
    "AzurePortal": True,
    "CallScoring": True,
    "Chef": True,
    "Cuttlefish": True,
    "EmailAccess": True,
    "Engage": True,
    "EquityEdge_GreatPlains": True,
    "GitHub": True,
    "Grafana": True,
    "Ipplan": True,
    "JIRA": True,
    "Marchex.io": True,
    "MI5": True,
    "Microsites": True,
    "NewRelic": True,
    "Nexus": True,
    "NimUI": True,
    "NISMaps": True,
    "OpenVPN": True,
    "PagerDuty": True,
    "Pulley": True,
    "Postman": True,
    "RT": True, # Checking RT for past access requests
    "Slack": True,
    "MarketingEdge": True,
    "Sendgrid": True,
    "Sentry": True,
    "Snowflake": True,
    "TACACS": True,  # Needs special handling (SEV5 ticket)
    "Wallace": True,
    "XMSHammer": True
}

ACCESS_LIST = [system for system, enabled in SYSTEMS_CATALOG.items() if enabled]
MISSING_SCRIPTS = []

# LDAP Configurations
LDAP_ADDR = 'ldaps://ldap.sea.marchex.com:636/'
LDAP_BASEDN = 'ou=users,dc=marchex,dc=com'
LDAP_BINDDN = 'uid={user},ou=users,dc=marchex,dc=com'
LDAP_SF = '(cn={user})'

# RT (Request Tracker) Configuration
RT_HOST = 'https://rt.marchex.com'
RT_URL = 'https://rt.marchex.com/REST/1.0'
RT_USER = "socbot"  # Replace with actual RT user
RT_PASS = "securepass"  # Replace with actual RT password

# High Priority Contact List Location
HIGH_PRI_FILE = r'\\marchex\files\soc\Emergency\High Priority Contact List\NOCHighPriorityContactList1.xlsx'

# Don't require signed cert for LDAP connection
ldap.set_option(ldap.OPT_X_TLS_REQUIRE_CERT, ldap.OPT_X_TLS_NEVER)


def get_user_input(prompt):
    """Wrapper for input to handle common input scenarios."""
    try:
        return input(prompt).strip()
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Error getting user input: {e}")
        return None


def get_directory_info(user):
    """Query Directory Manager for user alias & manager name."""
    directory_url = f"https://directorymanager.marchex.com/api/user/{user}"
    try:
        response = requests.get(directory_url)
        response.raise_for_status()
        user_data = response.json()
        return user_data.get('alias', 'Unknown'), user_data.get('manager', 'Unknown')
    except Exception as e:
        logging.warning(f"Failed to retrieve Directory Manager info for {user}: {e}")
        return 'Unknown', 'Unknown'


def check_rt_for_access_tickets(user):
    """Check RT (Request Tracker) for past access requests related to this user."""
    logging.info(f"Checking RT for past access requests related to {user}...")
    query = f"Owner = '{user}' AND (Status = 'new' OR Status = 'open')"
    tracker = rt.Rt(RT_URL, RT_USER, RT_PASS)
    if not tracker.login():
        logging.error("Failed to authenticate with RT.")
        return
    try:
        tickets = tracker.search(Queue="SOC", raw_query=query)
        if tickets:
            logging.info(f"User {user} has {len(tickets)} past access tickets in RT.")
            for ticket in tickets:
                logging.info(f"RT Ticket Found: {ticket['id']} - {ticket['Subject']}")
        else:
            logging.info(f"No previous access tickets found in RT for {user}.")
    except Exception as e:
        logging.warning(f"Error checking RT for {user}: {e}")


def check_high_priority_contact_list(user):
    """Check and remove user from High Priority Contact List."""
    if not os.path.exists(HIGH_PRI_FILE):
        logging.warning("High Priority Contact List file not found.")
        return
    try:
        wb = openpyxl.load_workbook(HIGH_PRI_FILE)
        sheet = wb.active
        for row in sheet.iter_rows():
            for cell in row:
                if str(user).lower() in str(cell.value).lower():
                    logging.info(f"Removing {user} from High Priority Contact List.")
                    cell.value = None
                    wb.save(HIGH_PRI_FILE)
                    return
        logging.info(f"{user} not found in High Priority Contact List.")
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Error modifying High Priority Contact List: {e}")


def submit_sev5_ticket_for_TACACS(user):

    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Failed to create SEV5 ticket for TACACS: {e}")

import logging
import psycopg2
import secret

# Setup logging
logging.basicConfig(
    format="%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s",
    level=logging.INFO
)

# Enable mock mode for safe testing (set to True for testing)
MOCK_MODE = True  

# Database configuration
DB_CONFIG = {
    "dbname": "adtrack_ro",
    "host": "vspool.som1.marchex.com",
    "port": 5432,
    "user": secret.get_secret("_ADTRACK_DB_USER"),
    "password": secret.get_secret("_ADTRACK_DB_PASS")
}

def get_db_connection():
    """Establish a connection to the AdTrack database."""
    if MOCK_MODE:
        logging.info("[MOCK] Skipping real DB connection.")
        return None  # Return None to avoid actual DB connections

    try:
        conn = psycopg2.connect(**DB_CONFIG)
        return conn
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Database connection failed: {e}")
        return None

def main(user, creds):
    """Check or remove AdTrack access for a given user."""
    if creds["vendorEmail"]:
        search_param = creds["vendorEmail"]
    else:
        search_param = f"{user}@marchex%"

    if MOCK_MODE:
        logging.info(f"[MOCK] Simulating DB lookup for {search_param}")
        # Simulate finding the user
        found_users = [f"{user}@marchex.com"]
        return found_users, user, creds if found_users else (None, user, creds)

    conn = get_db_connection()
    if not conn:
        return None, user, creds

    query = "SELECT email FROM at_user WHERE email ILIKE %s AND status != 'disabled'"
    try:
        with conn.cursor() as cur:
            cur.execute(query, (search_param,))
            rows = cur.fetchall()

        conn.close()
        return [row[0] for row in rows] if rows else None, user, creds

    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Database query failed: {e}")
        return None, user, creds

def remove_access(user):
    """Attempt to remove user access from AdTrack."""
    if MOCK_MODE:
        logging.info(f"[MOCK] Would remove access for {user} in AdTrack.")
        return  # Do nothing in mock mode

    conn = get_db_connection()
    if not conn:
        return

    delete_query = "UPDATE at_user SET status = 'disabled' WHERE email ILIKE %s"
    try:
        with conn.cursor() as cur:
            cur.execute(delete_query, (f"{user}@marchex%",))
            conn.commit()
        logging.info(f"Access removed for {user} in AdTrack.")

    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Failed to remove AdTrack access for {user}: {e}")

    finally:
        conn.close()

def foundAccess(result):
    """Handle access check and potential removal."""
    if result[0]:
        user = result[1]
        accessChoice = result[2]["accessChoice"]

        if accessChoice == "check":
            logging.info(f"{user} has AdTrack UI access.")
        elif accessChoice == "remove":
            logging.info(f"{user} has AdTrack UI access. Attempting removal...")
            remove_access(user)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    sepList = input("Enter LDAP user(s) to be separated (comma-separated): ").split(",")

lets go ahead and add mock mode for testing to the avenger.py script




import logging
import MySQLdb
import secret

# Setup logging
logging.basicConfig(
    format="%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s",
    level=logging.INFO
)

# Database Configuration
DB_CONFIG = {
    "host": "elpagedb-master.marchex.com",
    "user": secret.get_secret("_PROD_MYSQL_USER"),
    "passwd": secret.get_secret("_PROD_MYSQL_PASS"),
    "database": "avenger"
}

# SQL Queries
SQL_COMMANDS = {
    "check_for_user": "SELECT username, firstname, lastname FROM user WHERE username = %s AND is_active = 1",
    "remove": "DELETE FROM user_role WHERE user_id = (SELECT user_id FROM user WHERE username = %s)",
    "deactivate": "UPDATE user SET is_active = 0 WHERE username = %s"
}

def get_db_connection():
    """Establish a connection to the Avenger database."""
    try:
        return MySQLdb.connect(**DB_CONFIG)
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Database connection failed: {e}")
        return None

def execute_mysql_command(db, query, params=()):
    """Execute a MySQL query safely using parameterized queries."""
    try:
        with db.cursor() as cur:
            cur.execute(query, params)
            return cur.fetchall()
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Error executing query: {query} | Error: {e}")
        return None

def main(user, creds):
    """Check if a user has Avenger UI access."""
    conn = get_db_connection()
    if not conn:
        return None, user, creds

    try:
        result = execute_mysql_command(conn, SQL_COMMANDS["check_for_user"], (user,))
        return [f"{row[0]} ({row[1]} {row[2]})" for row in result] if result else None, user, creds
    finally:
        conn.close()

def remove_access(user):
    """Remove Avenger UI access for a given user."""
    conn = get_db_connection()
    if not conn:
        return

    try:
        # Remove user role and deactivate user
        execute_mysql_command(conn, SQL_COMMANDS["remove"], (user,))
        execute_mysql_command(conn, SQL_COMMANDS["deactivate"], (user,))
        conn.commit()
        logging.info(f"Avenger UI access removed for {user}.")
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Failed to remove Avenger UI access for {user}: {e}")
        conn.rollback()
    finally:
        conn.close()

def foundAccess(result):
    """Check if the user has access and remove if required."""
    if result[0]:
        user = result[1]
        accessChoice = result[2]["accessChoice"]

        if accessChoice == "check":
            logging.info(f"{user} has Avenger UI access.")
        elif accessChoice == "remove":
            logging.info(f"{user} has Avenger UI access. Attempting removal...")
            remove_access(user)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    logging.info("Checking Avenger UI access...")
    
    # Collect input from user
    sepList = input("Enter username(s) to check (comma-separated): ").split(",")
    accessChoice = input("Would you like to check or remove access? (Check/Remove): ").strip().lower()

    # Validate access choice
    while accessChoice not in ("remove", "check"):
        accessChoice = input("Invalid input. Please enter 'Remove' or 'Check': ").strip().lower()

    creds = {"accessChoice": accessChoice}

    for user in sepList:
        result = main(user.strip(), creds)
        foundAccess(result)

import logging
import subprocess
import shutil
import json

# Setup logging
logging.basicConfig(
    format="%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s",
    level=logging.INFO
)

def check_aws_cli():
    """Check if AWS CLI is installed."""
    if not shutil.which("aws"):
        logging.error("AWS CLI is not installed. Please install it using 'pip install awscli'.")
        return False
    return True

def get_aws_users(auth_user):
    """Retrieve the list of AWS IAM users."""
    try:
        output = subprocess.check_output(['aws', 'iam', 'list-users', '--profile', auth_user], stderr=subprocess.STDOUT)
        users = json.loads(output).get('Users', [])
        return {user['UserName'] for user in users}
    except subprocess.CalledProcessError as e:
        logging.error(f"AWS CLI error: {e.output.decode().strip()}")
        return None

def main(user, creds):
    """Check if a user has AWS IAM access."""
    if not check_aws_cli():
        return None, user, creds

    auth_user = creds['operatorUN']
    aws_users = get_aws_users(auth_user)

    if aws_users is None:
        return None, user, creds

    if user in aws_users:
        return user, user, creds
    else:
        return None, user, creds

def foundAccess(result):
    """Check if the user has AWS IAM access and remove if required."""
    if result[0]:
        user = result[1]
        accessChoice = result[2]['accessChoice']

        if accessChoice == "check":
            logging.info(f"{user} has AWS IAM access.")
        elif accessChoice == "remove":
            logging.info(f"{user} has AWS IAM access. Attempting removal...")
            deleteAccess(user, result[2]['operatorUN'])

def deleteAccess(user, auth_user):
    """Remove AWS IAM access for a given user."""
    try:
        subprocess.check_output(['aws', 'iam', 'delete-user', '--profile', auth_user, '--user-name', user], stderr=subprocess.STDOUT)
        logging.info(f"AWS IAM access removed for {user}.")
    except subprocess.CalledProcessError as e:
        logging.error(f"Failed to remove AWS IAM access for {user}: {e.output.decode().strip()}")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    logging.info("Checking AWS IAM access...")

    operatorUN = input("Enter your LDAP username: ").strip()
    users = input("Enter username(s) to check (comma-separated): ").strip().split(",")
    accessChoice = input("Would you like to check or remove access? (Check/Remove): ").strip().lower()

    while accessChoice not in ("remove", "check"):
        accessChoice = input("Invalid input. Please enter 'Remove' or 'Check': ").strip().lower()

    creds = {"operatorUN": operatorUN, "accessChoice": accessChoice}

    for user in users:
        result = main(user.strip(), creds)
        foundAccess(result)

import logging
import getpass
import ldap
import utils
import requests
import openpyxl
import os
import json
import rt
from concurrent.futures import ThreadPoolExecutor

# Setup logging
logging.basicConfig(
    format='%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s',
    level=logging.INFO
)

# 🟢 Enable Mock Mode for Safe Testing (Change to False for Live Runs)
MOCK_MODE = True  


# Systems that require separation processing
SYSTEMS_CATALOG = {
    "AdTrack": True,
    "AFR": True,
    "Auth0": True,
    "Avenger": True,
    "AWS": True,
    "ADO": True,
    "AzurePortal": True,
    "CallScoring": True,
    "Chef": True,
    "Cuttlefish": True,
    "EmailAccess": True,
    "Engage": True,
    "EquityEdge_GreatPlains": True,
    "GitHub": True,
    "Grafana": True,
    "Ipplan": True,
    "JIRA": True,
    "Marchex.io": True,
    "MI5": True,
    "Microsites": True,
    "NewRelic": True,
    "Nexus": True,
    "NimUI": True,
    "NISMaps": True,
    "OpenVPN": True,
    "PagerDuty": True,
    "Pulley": True,
    "Postman": True,
    "RT": True, # Checking RT for past access requests
    "Slack": True,
    "MarketingEdge": True,
    "Sendgrid": True,
    "Sentry": True,
    "Snowflake": True,
    "TACACS": True,  # Needs special handling (SEV5 ticket)
    "Wallace": True,
    "XMSHammer": True
}

ACCESS_LIST = [system for system, enabled in SYSTEMS_CATALOG.items() if enabled]
MISSING_SCRIPTS = []

# LDAP Configurations
LDAP_ADDR = 'ldaps://ldap.sea.marchex.com:636/'
LDAP_BASEDN = 'ou=users,dc=marchex,dc=com'
LDAP_BINDDN = 'uid={user},ou=users,dc=marchex,dc=com'
LDAP_SF = '(cn={user})'

# RT (Request Tracker) Configuration
RT_HOST = 'https://rt.marchex.com'
RT_URL = 'https://rt.marchex.com/REST/1.0'
RT_USER = "socbot"  # Replace with actual RT user
RT_PASS = "securepass"  # Replace with actual RT password

# High Priority Contact List Location
HIGH_PRI_FILE = r'\\marchex\files\soc\Emergency\High Priority Contact List\NOCHighPriorityContactList1.xlsx'

# Don't require signed cert for LDAP connection
ldap.set_option(ldap.OPT_X_TLS_REQUIRE_CERT, ldap.OPT_X_TLS_NEVER)


def get_user_input(prompt):
    """Wrapper for input to handle common input scenarios."""
    try:
        return input(prompt).strip()
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Error getting user input: {e}")
        return None


def get_directory_info(user):
    """Query Directory Manager for user alias & manager name."""
    directory_url = f"https://directorymanager.marchex.com/api/user/{user}"
    try:
        response = requests.get(directory_url)
        response.raise_for_status()
        user_data = response.json()
        return user_data.get('alias', 'Unknown'), user_data.get('manager', 'Unknown')
    except Exception as e:
        logging.warning(f"Failed to retrieve Directory Manager info for {user}: {e}")
        return 'Unknown', 'Unknown'


def check_rt_for_access_tickets(user):
    """Check RT (Request Tracker) for past access requests related to this user."""
    logging.info(f"Checking RT for past access requests related to {user}...")
    query = f"Owner = '{user}' AND (Status = 'new' OR Status = 'open')"
    tracker = rt.Rt(RT_URL, RT_USER, RT_PASS)
    if not tracker.login():
        logging.error("Failed to authenticate with RT.")
        return
    try:
        tickets = tracker.search(Queue="SOC", raw_query=query)
        if tickets:
            logging.info(f"User {user} has {len(tickets)} past access tickets in RT.")
            for ticket in tickets:
                logging.info(f"RT Ticket Found: {ticket['id']} - {ticket['Subject']}")
        else:
            logging.info(f"No previous access tickets found in RT for {user}.")
    except Exception as e:
        logging.warning(f"Error checking RT for {user}: {e}")


def check_high_priority_contact_list(user):
    """Check and remove user from High Priority Contact List."""
    if not os.path.exists(HIGH_PRI_FILE):
        logging.warning("High Priority Contact List file not found.")
        return
    try:
        wb = openpyxl.load_workbook(HIGH_PRI_FILE)
        sheet = wb.active
        for row in sheet.iter_rows():
            for cell in row:
                if str(user).lower() in str(cell.value).lower():
                    logging.info(f"Removing {user} from High Priority Contact List.")
                    cell.value = None
                    wb.save(HIGH_PRI_FILE)
                    return
        logging.info(f"{user} not found in High Priority Contact List.")
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Error modifying High Priority Contact List: {e}")


def submit_sev5_ticket_for_TACACS(user):
    """Submit a SEV5 ticket to NetEng for TACACS removal."""
    logging.info(f"Submitting SEV5 ticket for TACACS removal for {user}.")
    
    # Simulated API request
    ticket_payload = {
        "summary": f"SEV5 - Remove TACACS access for {user}",
        "description": f"User {user} requires TACACS access removal as part of separation.",
        "priority": "SEV5",
        "assigned_team": "NetEng"
    }
    try:
        response = requests.post("https://ticketing.marchex.com/api/tickets", json=ticket_payload)
        response.raise_for_status()
        logging.info(f"SEV5 ticket successfully created for TACACS removal: {response.json().get('ticket_id')}")
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Failed to create SEV5 ticket for TACACS: {e}")


def main():
    """ Main function for the separation script. """
    logging.info("########### SEPARATION SCRIPT #############")
    operatorUN = get_user_input("Enter your LDAP username: ")
    operatorPass = getpass.getpass("Enter your LDAP password: ")

    # Gather usernames to be separated
    sepList = get_user_input("Enter LDAP user(s) to be separated (comma-separated): ").split(',')

    # Check if user is a vendor
    while True:
        isVendor = get_user_input("Is this user a vendor? (yes/no): ").lower()
        if isVendor in ('yes', 'no'):
            break
        logging.warning("Invalid input. Please enter 'yes' or 'no'.")
    vendorEmail = None
    if isVendor == "yes":
        if any(sys in ACCESS_LIST for sys in ["PagerDuty", "Microsites"]):
            vendorEmail = get_user_input("Enter vendor email address: ")
        else:
            logging.info("Vendor email not needed for selected systems.")

    # Ask if we are checking or removing access
    while True:
        accessChoice = get_user_input("Would you like to remove all found access or just check access? (Remove/Check): ").lower()
        if accessChoice in ('remove', 'check'):
            break
        logging.warning("Invalid input. Please enter 'Remove' or 'Check'.")
    
    creds = {
        "operatorUN": operatorUN,
        "operatorPass": operatorPass,
        "sepList": sepList,
        "accessChoice": accessChoice,
        "vendorEmail": vendorEmail,
        "MOCK_MODE": MOCK_MODE  # 🟢 Global Mock Mode Toggle
    }

    try:
        ldp = ldap.initialize(LDAP_ADDR)
        ldp.simple_bind_s(LDAP_BINDDN.format(user=operatorUN), operatorPass)
    except ldap.INVALID_CREDENTIALS:
        logging.error("LDAP authentication failed. Exiting.")
        return
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Unexpected LDAP error: {e}")
        return
    
    with ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=5) as executor:
        executor.map(lambda user: process_user(ldp, user, creds), sepList)

    logging.info(f"####### No further access found for {user} #######")
    
    if MISSING_SCRIPTS:
        logging.warning(f"Missing separation scripts: {', '.join(set(MISSING_SCRIPTS))}")


def process_user(ldp, user, creds):
    """Process separation for an individual user."""
    try:
        alias, manager = get_directory_info(user)
        logging.info(f"User {user} Alias: {alias}, Manager: {manager}")
        check_rt_for_access_tickets(user)
        if ldapQuery(ldp, user):
            checkAccess(user, creds)
        check_high_priority_contact_list(user)
        if "TACACS" in ACCESS_LIST:
            submit_sev5_ticket_for_TACACS(user)
        logging.info(f"####### No further access found for {user} #######")
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Error processing user {user}: {e}")


def ldapQuery(ldp, user):
    """Check if user exists in LDAP."""
    logging.info(f"Checking LDAP access for {user}...")
    try:
        result_id = ldp.search(LDAP_BASEDN, ldap.SCOPE_SUBTREE, LDAP_SF.format(user=user))
        result_type, result_data = ldp.result(result_id, 0)
        if not result_data:
            logging.warning(f"User {user} not found in LDAP.")
            return False
        return True
    except ldap.LDAPError as e:
        logging.error(f"LDAP query failed for {user}: {e}")
        return False


def checkAccess(user, creds):
    """Run access removal scripts."""
    global MISSING_SCRIPTS 
    logging.info(f"Checking access for {user}...")
    for system in ACCESS_LIST:
        try:
            sep_module = __import__(f"separations.{system.lower()}", fromlist=[""])
            sep_module.main(user, creds)
        except ImportError:
            MISSING_SCRIPTS.append(system)
        except Exception as e:
            logging.error(f"Error running {system} separation: {e}")


if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

import logging
import MySQLdb
import secret

# Setup logging
logging.basicConfig(
    format="%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s",
    level=logging.INFO
)

# Enable mock mode for safe testing (set to True for testing)
MOCK_MODE = True  

# Database Configuration
DB_CONFIG = {
    "host": "elpagedb-master.marchex.com",
    "user": secret.get_secret("_PROD_MYSQL_USER"),
    "passwd": secret.get_secret("_PROD_MYSQL_PASS"),
    "database": "avenger"
}

# SQL Queries
SQL_COMMANDS = {
    "check_for_user": "SELECT username, firstname, lastname FROM user WHERE username = %s AND is_active = 1",
    "remove": "DELETE FROM user_role WHERE user_id = (SELECT user_id FROM user WHERE username = %s)",
    "deactivate": "UPDATE user SET is_active = 0 WHERE username = %s"
}

def get_db_connection():
    """Establish a connection to the Avenger database."""
    if MOCK_MODE:
        logging.info("[MOCK] Skipping real DB connection.")
        return None  # Return None to avoid actual DB interactions
    
    try:
        return MySQLdb.connect(**DB_CONFIG)
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Database connection failed: {e}")
        return None

def execute_mysql_command(db, query, params=()):
    """Execute a MySQL query safely using parameterized queries."""
    if MOCK_MODE:
        logging.info(f"[MOCK] Simulating query execution: {query} | Params: {params}")
        if "check_for_user" in query:
            return [(params[0], "MockFirst", "MockLast")]  # Simulated user found
        return None  # Default mock response

    try:
        with db.cursor() as cur:
            cur.execute(query, params)
            return cur.fetchall()
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Error executing query: {query} | Error: {e}")
        return None

def main(user, creds):
    """Check if a user has Avenger UI access."""
    if MOCK_MODE:
        logging.info(f"[MOCK] Checking access for {user}.")
        # Simulate user found in Avenger
        return [f"{user} (MockFirst MockLast)"], user, creds

    conn = get_db_connection()
    if not conn:
        return None, user, creds

    try:
        result = execute_mysql_command(conn, SQL_COMMANDS["check_for_user"], (user,))
        return [f"{row[0]} ({row[1]} {row[2]})" for row in result] if result else None, user, creds
    finally:
        if conn:
            conn.close()

def remove_access(user):
    """Remove Avenger UI access for a given user."""
    if MOCK_MODE:
        logging.info(f"[MOCK] Would remove access for {user} in Avenger.")
        return  # Do nothing in mock mode

    conn = get_db_connection()
    if not conn:
        return

    try:
        execute_mysql_command(conn, SQL_COMMANDS["remove"], (user,))
        execute_mysql_command(conn, SQL_COMMANDS["deactivate"], (user,))
        conn.commit()
        logging.info(f"Avenger UI access removed for {user}.")
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Failed to remove Avenger UI access for {user}: {e}")
        conn.rollback()
    finally:
        if conn:
            conn.close()

def foundAccess(result):
    """Check if the user has access and remove if required."""
    if result[0]:
        user = result[1]
        accessChoice = result[2]["accessChoice"]

        if accessChoice == "check":
            logging.info(f"{user} has Avenger UI access.")
        elif accessChoice == "remove":
            logging.info(f"{user} has Avenger UI access. Attempting removal...")
            remove_access(user)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    logging.info("Checking Avenger UI access...")

    # Collect input from user
    sepList = input("Enter username(s) to check (comma-separated): ").split(",")
    accessChoice = input("Would you like to check or remove access? (Check/Remove): ").strip().lower()

    # Validate access choice
    while accessChoice not in ("remove", "check"):
        accessChoice = input("Invalid input. Please enter 'Remove' or 'Check': ").strip().lower()

    creds = {"accessChoice": accessChoice}

    for user in sepList:
        result = main(user.strip(), creds)
        foundAccess(result)

import logging
import psycopg2
import secret

# Setup logging
logging.basicConfig(
    format="%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s",
    level=logging.INFO
)

# Enable mock mode for safe testing (set to True for testing)
MOCK_MODE = True  

# Database configuration
DB_CONFIG = {
    "dbname": "adtrack_ro",
    "host": "vspool.som1.marchex.com",
    "port": 5432,
    "user": secret.get_secret("_ADTRACK_DB_USER"),
    "password": secret.get_secret("_ADTRACK_DB_PASS")
}

def get_db_connection():
    """Establish a connection to the AdTrack database."""
    if MOCK_MODE:
        logging.info("[MOCK] Skipping real DB connection.")
        return None  # Return None to avoid actual DB connections

    try:
        conn = psycopg2.connect(**DB_CONFIG)
        return conn
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Database connection failed: {e}")
        return None

def main(user, creds):
    """Check or remove AdTrack access for a given user."""
    if creds["vendorEmail"]:
        search_param = creds["vendorEmail"]
    else:
        search_param = f"{user}@marchex%"

    if MOCK_MODE:
        logging.info(f"[MOCK] Simulating DB lookup for {search_param}")
        # Simulate finding the user
        found_users = [f"{user}@marchex.com"]
        return found_users, user, creds if found_users else (None, user, creds)

    conn = get_db_connection()
    if not conn:
        return None, user, creds

    query = "SELECT email FROM at_user WHERE email ILIKE %s AND status != 'disabled'"
    try:
        with conn.cursor() as cur:
            cur.execute(query, (search_param,))
            rows = cur.fetchall()

        conn.close()
        return [row[0] for row in rows] if rows else None, user, creds

    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Database query failed: {e}")
        return None, user, creds

def remove_access(user):
    """Attempt to remove user access from AdTrack."""
    if MOCK_MODE:
        logging.info(f"[MOCK] Would remove access for {user} in AdTrack.")
        return  # Do nothing in mock mode

    conn = get_db_connection()
    if not conn:
        return

    delete_query = "UPDATE at_user SET status = 'disabled' WHERE email ILIKE %s"
    try:
        with conn.cursor() as cur:
            cur.execute(delete_query, (f"{user}@marchex%",))
            conn.commit()
        logging.info(f"Access removed for {user} in AdTrack.")

    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Failed to remove AdTrack access for {user}: {e}")

    finally:
        conn.close()

def foundAccess(result):
    """Handle access check and potential removal."""
    if result[0]:
        user = result[1]
        accessChoice = result[2]["accessChoice"]

        if accessChoice == "check":
            logging.info(f"{user} has AdTrack UI access.")
        elif accessChoice == "remove":
            logging.info(f"{user} has AdTrack UI access. Attempting removal...")
            remove_access(user)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    sepList = input("Enter LDAP user(s) to be separated (comma-separated): ").split(",")
    accessChoice = input("Would you like to check or remove access? (Check/Remove): ").lower()
    isVendor = input("Is this user a vendor? (Yes/No): ").lower()

    vendorEmail = None
    if isVendor == "yes":
        vendorEmail = input("Enter vendor email address: ")

    creds = {"accessChoice": accessChoice, "vendorEmail": vendorEmail}

    for user in sepList:
        result = main(user.strip(), creds)
        foundAccess(result)
now before we continue to implement further mock modes in the other scripts lets take one last look at aws to make sure its mock mode implementation is also correctly toggled by the separations script rather then being hard coded and toggled programmatically in the aws script.




import logging
import subprocess
import shutil
import json

# Setup logging
logging.basicConfig(
    format="%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s",
    level=logging.INFO
)

def check_aws_cli():
    """Check if AWS CLI is installed."""
    if not shutil.which("aws"):
        logging.error("AWS CLI is not installed. Please install it using 'pip install awscli'.")
        return False
    return True

def get_aws_users(auth_user, mock_mode):
    """Retrieve the list of AWS IAM users."""
    if mock_mode:
        logging.info("[MOCK] Simulating AWS IAM user list retrieval.")
        return {"mockuser1", "mockuser2", "mockadmin"}  # Simulated AWS users

    try:
        output = subprocess.check_output(['aws', 'iam', 'list-users', '--profile', auth_user], stderr=subprocess.STDOUT)
        users = json.loads(output).get('Users', [])
        return {user['UserName'] for user in users}
    except subprocess.CalledProcessError as e:
        logging.error(f"AWS CLI error: {e.output.decode().strip()}")
        return None

def main(user, creds):
    """Check if a user has AWS IAM access."""
    mock_mode = creds["MOCK_MODE"]  # Read Mock Mode from creds

    if mock_mode:
        logging.info(f"[MOCK] Checking AWS IAM access for {user}.")
        return (user, user, creds) if user in {"mockuser1", "mockuser2", "mockadmin"} else (None, user, creds)

    if not check_aws_cli():
        return None, user, creds

    auth_user = creds['operatorUN']
    aws_users = get_aws_users(auth_user, mock_mode)

    if aws_users is None:
        return None, user, creds

    return (user, user, creds) if user in aws_users else (None, user, creds)

def foundAccess(result):
    """Check if the user has AWS IAM access and remove if required."""
    if result[0]:
        user = result[1]
        accessChoice = result[2]['accessChoice']
        mock_mode = result[2]["MOCK_MODE"]

        if accessChoice == "check":
            logging.info(f"{user} has AWS IAM access.")
        elif accessChoice == "remove":
            logging.info(f"{user} has AWS IAM access. Attempting removal...")
            deleteAccess(user, result[2]['operatorUN'], mock_mode)

def deleteAccess(user, auth_user, mock_mode):
    """Remove AWS IAM access for a given user."""
    if mock_mode:
        logging.info(f"[MOCK] Would remove AWS IAM access for {user}.")
        return  # Skip actual deletion in mock mode

    try:
        subprocess.check_output(['aws', 'iam', 'delete-user', '--profile', auth_user, '--user-name', user], stderr=subprocess.STDOUT)
        logging.info(f"AWS IAM access removed for {user}.")
    except subprocess.CalledProcessError as e:
        logging.error(f"Failed to remove AWS IAM access for {user}: {e.output.decode().strip()}")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    logging.info("Checking AWS IAM access...")

    operatorUN = input("Enter your LDAP username: ").strip()
    users = input("Enter username(s) to check (comma-separated): ").strip().split(",")
    accessChoice = input("Would you like to check or remove access? (Check/Remove): ").strip().lower()

    while accessChoice not in ("remove", "check"):
        accessChoice = input("Invalid input. Please enter 'Remove' or 'Check': ").strip().lower()

    creds = {
        "operatorUN": operatorUN,
        "accessChoice": accessChoice,
        "MOCK_MODE": True  # This would be overridden when called from separations.py
    }

    for user in users:
        result = main(user.strip(), creds)
        foundAccess(result)

import requests
import getpass
import logging

# Setup logging
logging.basicConfig(
    format="%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s",
    level=logging.INFO
)

# Grafana API Configuration
GRAFANA_URL = "https://grafana.marchex.com"
GRAFANA_API_KEY = "your-api-key-here"  # Use an API key instead of login credentials

def authenticate_grafana(session, operatorUN, operatorPass):
    """ Authenticate with Grafana API and store session. """
    login_url = f"{GRAFANA_URL}/login"
    credentials = {"user": operatorUN, "password": operatorPass}
    
    try:
        response = session.post(login_url, json=credentials)
        response.raise_for_status()
        logging.info("Successfully authenticated to Grafana.")
    except requests.exceptions.RequestException as e:
        logging.error(f"Failed to authenticate with Grafana: {e}")
        return False
    
    return True

def get_grafana_users(session):
    """ Fetch list of all Grafana users. """
    users_url = f"{GRAFANA_URL}/api/org/users"

    try:
        response = session.get(users_url, headers={"Authorization": f"Bearer {GRAFANA_API_KEY}"})
        response.raise_for_status()
        return response.json()
    except requests.exceptions.RequestException as e:
        logging.error(f"Failed to retrieve Grafana users: {e}")
        return None

def main(user, creds):
    """ Check if a user has Grafana access. """
    operatorUN = creds["operatorUN"]
    operatorPass = creds["operatorPass"]

    with requests.Session() as session:
        if not authenticate_grafana(session, operatorUN, operatorPass):
            return None, user, creds

        grafana_users = get_grafana_users(session)

        if grafana_users is None:
            return None, user, creds

        # Check if the user exists in Grafana
        matching_users = [u for u in grafana_users if u["login"] == user]

        if matching_users:
            return user, user, creds
        else:
            return None, user, creds

def foundAccess(result):
    """ Check if the user has Grafana access and remove if required. """
    if result[0]:
        user = result[1]
        accessChoice = result[2]["accessChoice"]

        if accessChoice == "check":
            logging.info(f"{user} has Grafana access.")
        elif accessChoice == "remove":
            logging.info(f"{user} has Grafana access. Attempting removal...")
            deleteAccess(user)

def deleteAccess(user):
    """ Remove a user from Grafana. """
    delete_url = f"{GRAFANA_URL}/api/admin/users/{user}"

    try:
        response = requests.delete(delete_url, headers={"Authorization": f"Bearer {GRAFANA_API_KEY}"})
        response.raise_for_status()
        logging.info(f"Grafana access removed for {user}.")
    except requests.exceptions.RequestException as e:
        logging.error(f"Failed to remove Grafana access for {user}: {e}")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    logging.info("Checking Grafana access...")

    operatorUN = input("Enter your LDAP username: ").strip()
    operatorPass = getpass.getpass("Enter your LDAP password: ").strip()
    users = input("Enter username(s) to check (comma-separated): ").strip().split(",")
    accessChoice = input("Would you like to check or remove access? (Check/Remove): ").strip().lower()

    while accessChoice not in ("remove", "check"):
        accessChoice = input("Invalid input. Please enter 'Remove' or 'Check': ").strip().lower()

    creds = {"operatorUN": operatorUN, "operatorPass": operatorPass, "accessChoice": accessChoice}

    for user in users:
        result = main(user.strip(), creds)
        foundAccess(result)
next is ipplan.py




import requests
import getpass
import logging
from requests.auth import HTTPBasicAuth

# Setup logging
logging.basicConfig(
    format="%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s",
    level=logging.INFO
)

# IP Plan Configuration
IPPLAN_URL = "https://ipplan.marchex.com/admin/usermanager.php?action=usereditform"
IPPLAN_USER = "your-ipplan-username"  # Replace with actual credentials retrieval method
IPPLAN_PASS = "your-ipplan-password"

def authenticate_ipplan(session):
    """ Authenticate with IP Plan and store session. """
    try:
        response = session.get(IPPLAN_URL, auth=HTTPBasicAuth(IPPLAN_USER, IPPLAN_PASS))
        response.raise_for_status()
        logging.info("Successfully authenticated to IP Plan.")
    except requests.exceptions.RequestException as e:
        logging.error(f"Failed to authenticate with IP Plan: {e}")
        return False
    return True

def get_ipplan_users(session):
    """ Fetch list of users from IP Plan. """
    try:
        response = session.get(IPPLAN_URL, auth=HTTPBasicAuth(IPPLAN_USER, IPPLAN_PASS))
        response.raise_for_status()
        return response.text  # Adjust parsing if IP Plan returns structured data (HTML or JSON)
    except requests.exceptions.RequestException as e:
        logging.error(f"Failed to retrieve IP Plan users: {e}")
        return None

def main(user, creds):
    """ Check if a user has IP Plan access. """
    with requests.Session() as session:
        if not authenticate_ipplan(session):
            return None, user, creds

        ipplan_users = get_ipplan_users(session)

        if ipplan_users is None:
            return None, user, creds

        # Check if the user exists in IP Plan
        if user in ipplan_users:
            return user, user, creds
        else:
            return None, user, creds

def foundAccess(result):
    """ Check if the user has IP Plan access and remove if required. """
    if result[0]:
        user = result[1]
        accessChoice = result[2]["accessChoice"]

        if accessChoice == "check":
            logging.info(f"{user} has IP Plan access.")
        elif accessChoice == "remove":
            logging.info(f"{user} has IP Plan access. Attempting removal...")
            deleteAccess(user)

def deleteAccess(user):
    """ Remove a user from IP Plan (if supported). """
    remove_url = f"https://ipplan.marchex.com/admin/usermanager.php?action=remove&user={user}"

    try:
        response = requests.get(remove_url, auth=HTTPBasicAuth(IPPLAN_USER, IPPLAN_PASS))
        response.raise_for_status()
        logging.info(f"IP Plan access removed for {user}.")
    except requests.exceptions.RequestException as e:
        logging.error(f"Failed to remove IP Plan access for {user}: {e}")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    logging.info("Checking IP Plan access...")

    operatorUN = input("Enter your LDAP username: ").strip()
    operatorPass = getpass.getpass("Enter your LDAP password: ").strip()
    users = input("Enter username(s) to check (comma-separated): ").strip().split(",")
    accessChoice = input("Would you like to check or remove access? (Check/Remove): ").strip().lower()

    while accessChoice not in ("remove", "check"):
        accessChoice = input("Invalid input. Please enter 'Remove' or 'Check': ").strip().lower()

    creds = {"operatorUN": operatorUN, "operatorPass": operatorPass, "accessChoice": accessChoice}

    for user in users:
        result = main(user.strip(), creds)
        foundAccess(result)
next is JIRA.py




import requests
import getpass
import logging
import json

# Setup logging
logging.basicConfig(
    format="%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s",
    level=logging.INFO
)

# JIRA API Configuration
JIRA_URL = "https://jira.marchex.com/rest/api/latest/user"
JIRA_API_TOKEN = "your_api_token_here"  # Use API Token instead of passwords
JIRA_USERNAME = "your_email@marchex.com"

def get_jira_headers():
    """Return the authentication headers for JIRA API."""
    return {
        "Authorization": f"Bearer {JIRA_API_TOKEN}",
        "Content-Type": "application/json"
    }

def check_jira_access(user):
    """Check if a user has access to JIRA."""
    try:
        response = requests.get(
            f"{JIRA_URL}?username={user}",
            headers=get_jira_headers()
        )
        response.raise_for_status()
        data = response.json()

        if data.get("active", False):
            return f"{data['name']} ({data['displayName']})"
        else:
            return None

    except requests.exceptions.HTTPError as e:
        if response.status_code == 404:
            logging.warning(f"User {user} does not exist in JIRA.")
        else:
            logging.error(f"JIRA API request failed: {e}")
        return None
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Unexpected error while checking JIRA access: {e}")
        return None

def remove_jira_access(user):
    """Attempt to deactivate the user in JIRA (if API supports it)."""
    delete_url = f"https://jira.marchex.com/rest/api/latest/user?username={user}"

    try:
        response = requests.delete(delete_url, headers=get_jira_headers())

        if response.status_code == 204:
            logging.info(f"Successfully removed {user} from JIRA.")
        elif response.status_code == 403:
            logging.warning(f"Insufficient permissions to remove {user} from JIRA.")
        else:
            logging.error(f"Failed to remove {user} from JIRA: {response.text}")

    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Error during JIRA user removal: {e}")

def main():
    """ Main function for JIRA access check/removal. """
    logging.info("Checking JIRA access...")

    users = input("Enter username(s) to check (comma-separated): ").strip().split(",")
    accessChoice = input("Would you like to check or remove access? (Check/Remove): ").strip().lower()

    while accessChoice not in ("remove", "check"):
        accessChoice = input("Invalid input. Please enter 'Remove' or 'Check': ").strip().lower()

    for user in users:
        user = user.strip()
        result = check_jira_access(user)

        if result:
            logging.info(f"{user} has JIRA access.")
            if accessChoice == "remove":
                remove_jira_access(user)
        else:
            logging.info(f"{user} does not have JIRA access.")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
next is microsites.py




import logging
import pymysql
import getpass
import secret

# Setup logging
logging.basicConfig(
    format="%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s",
    level=logging.INFO
)

# Database Configuration
DB_HOST = "bppdb-master.marchex.com"
DB_USER = secret.get_secret("_PROD_MYSQL_USER")
DB_PASS = secret.get_secret("_PROD_MYSQL_PASS")
DB_NAME = "microsite"

# SQL Queries
SQL_COMMANDS = {
    "check_for_user": "SELECT name, email, status FROM users WHERE status != 'inactive' AND (email LIKE %s OR name LIKE %s)",
    "deactivate": "UPDATE users SET status = 'inactive' WHERE email = %s",
}

def connect_db():
    """Connect to the MySQL database."""
    try:
        return pymysql.connect(host=DB_HOST, user=DB_USER, password=DB_PASS, database=DB_NAME)
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Database connection failed: {e}")
        return None

def check_user_access(username):
    """Check if a user has access to Microsite UI."""
    try:
        with connect_db() as db, db.cursor() as cursor:
            cursor.execute(SQL_COMMANDS["check_for_user"], (f"%{username}%", f"%{username}%"))
            return cursor.fetchall()
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Error executing query: {e}")
        return None

def deactivate_user(username):
    """Deactivate a user in Microsite UI."""
    try:
        with connect_db() as db, db.cursor() as cursor:
            cursor.execute(SQL_COMMANDS["deactivate"], (f"{username}@marchex.com",))
            db.commit()
            logging.info(f"Successfully deactivated {username} in Microsite UI.")
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Error deactivating {username}: {e}")

def process_user(username, access_choice):
    """Process a single user for access check or removal."""
    result = check_user_access(username)

    if result:
        logging.info(f"{username} has Microsite UI access.")
        if access_choice == "remove":
            deactivate_user(username)
    else:
        logging.info(f"{username} does not have Microsite UI access.")

def main():
    """Main function for Microsite access check/removal."""
    logging.info("Checking Microsite UI access...")

    users = input("Enter usernames to check (comma-separated): ").strip().split(",")
    access_choice = input("Would you like to check or remove access? (Check/Remove): ").strip().lower()

    while access_choice not in ("remove", "check"):
        access_choice = input("Invalid input. Please enter 'Remove' or 'Check': ").strip().lower()

    for user in users:
        process_user(user.strip(), access_choice)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
next is mysql_db.py




import logging
import pymysql
import sys
import secret
import dbaHostHelper

# Setup logging
logging.basicConfig(
    format="%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s",
    level=logging.INFO
)

# Get list of MySQL hosts
DB_HOSTS = dbaHostHelper.get_mysql_hosts()

# Database Credentials
DB_USER = secret.get_secret("_PROD_MYSQL_USER")
DB_PASS = secret.get_secret("_PROD_MYSQL_PASS")

# SQL Queries (using parameterized queries for security)
SQL_COMMANDS = {
    "findUser": "SELECT user FROM mysql.user WHERE user LIKE %s;",
    "dropUser": "DROP USER %s;",
    "flush": "FLUSH PRIVILEGES;",
}

def connect_db(host):
    """Establish a connection to a MySQL database."""
    try:
        return pymysql.connect(host=host, user=DB_USER, password=DB_PASS, database="mysql")
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Could not connect to MySQL on {host}: {e}")
        return None

def execute_mysql_command(db, query, params=None):
    """Execute a MySQL command with optional parameters."""
    try:
        with db.cursor() as cursor:
            cursor.execute(query, params)
            return cursor.fetchall()
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"MySQL query execution failed: {e}")
        return None

def check_user_access(username):
    """Check if a user has MySQL access on any host."""
    hostlist = []
    for host in DB_HOSTS:
        db = connect_db(host)
        if not db:
            continue
        try:
            result = execute_mysql_command(db, SQL_COMMANDS["findUser"], (f"%{username}%",))
            if result:
                hostlist.append(host)
        finally:
            db.close()
    return hostlist if hostlist else None

def deactivate_user(hostlist, username):
    """Remove a user from MySQL on all listed hosts."""
    for host in hostlist:
        db = connect_db(host)
        if not db:
            continue
        try:
            confirmation = input(f"{username} will be removed from {host}. Continue? (y/n): ").strip().lower()
            if confirmation != 'y':
                logging.info(f"{username} will NOT be removed from {host}.")
                continue

            if not execute_mysql_command(db, SQL_COMMANDS["findUser"], (username,)):
                logging.info(f"{username} was already removed from {host}.")
                continue

            execute_mysql_command(db, SQL_COMMANDS["dropUser"], (username,))
            execute_mysql_command(db, SQL_COMMANDS["flush"])
            db.commit()

            # Verify removal
            if not execute_mysql_command(db, SQL_COMMANDS["findUser"], (username,)):
                logging.info(f"✅ {username} successfully removed from {host}.")
            else:
                logging.warning(f"⚠️ {username} was NOT removed from {host}. Please check manually.")

        except Exception as e:
            db.rollback()
            logging.error(f"Error while removing {username} from {host}: {e}")
        finally:
            db.close()

def main():
    """Main function for MySQL user separation."""
    username = input("Enter the username to check: ").strip()
    access_choice = input("Would you like to check or remove access? (Check/Remove): ").strip().lower()

    while access_choice not in ("check", "remove"):
        access_choice = input("Invalid input. Please enter 'Check' or 'Remove': ").strip().lower()

    hostlist = check_user_access(username)
    
    if hostlist:
        logging.info(f"✅ {username} has MySQL access on: {', '.join(hostlist)}")
        if access_choice == "remove":
            deactivate_user(hostlist, username)
    else:
        logging.info(f"❌ {username} does not have MySQL access.")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
next is nimui.py




import logging
import os
import cx_Oracle
import secret

# Setup logging
logging.basicConfig(
    format="%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s",
    level=logging.INFO
)

# Oracle DB Instances to check
DB_INSTANCES = ["OPNEXT"]

# Database Credentials
DB_USER = secret.get_secret("_ORACLE_USER")
DB_PASS = secret.get_secret("_ORACLE_PASS")
DB_DSN = secret.get_secret("_ORACLE_DSN")  # Example: "hostname:port/service_name"

# Check if Oracle Client is installed
try:
    cx_Oracle.init_oracle_client(lib_dir="/path/to/oracle_client")
except Exception as e:
    logging.error(f"Could not initialize Oracle client: {e}")
    exit(1)

def check_nimui_access(username):
    """Check if the user has access to NimUI (Oracle DB)."""
    try:
        connection = cx_Oracle.connect(DB_USER, DB_PASS, DB_DSN)
        cursor = connection.cursor()

        query = """
        SELECT ID, USERNAME, EMAIL, STATUS
        FROM COMMON.USERS
        WHERE USERNAME = :username
        """

        cursor.execute(query, {"username": username})
        result = cursor.fetchall()

        cursor.close()
        connection.close()

        return result

    except cx_Oracle.DatabaseError as e:
        logging.error(f"Failed to query NimUI for {username}: {e}")
        return None

def foundAccess(result, username, accessChoice):
    """Report user access status."""
    if result:
        if accessChoice == "check":
            logging.info(f"✅ {username} has NimUI access.")
        elif accessChoice == "remove":
            logging.warning(f"⚠️ {username} has NimUI access, but automatic removal is NOT available. Please remove manually.")
    else:
        logging.info(f"❌ {username} does NOT have NimUI access.")

def main():
    """Main function to handle user separation for NimUI."""
    username = input("Enter LDAP username to check/remove: ").strip()
    accessChoice = input("Would you like to check or remove access? (Check/Remove): ").strip().lower()

    while accessChoice not in ("check", "remove"):
        accessChoice = input("Invalid input. Please enter 'Check' or 'Remove': ").strip().lower()

    result = check_nimui_access(username)
    foundAccess(result, username, accessChoice)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
next is oracle_db.py




import logging
import os
import cx_Oracle
import secret

# Setup logging
logging.basicConfig(
    format="%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s",
    level=logging.INFO
)

# Oracle Database Configuration
DB_INSTANCES = secret.get_secret("_ORACLE_INSTANCES")  # Example: ["OPNEXT", "DB2"]
DB_USER = secret.get_secret("_ORACLE_USER")
DB_PASS = secret.get_secret("_ORACLE_PASS")
DB_DSN = secret.get_secret("_ORACLE_DSN")  # Example: "hostname:port/service_name"

# Check if Oracle Client is installed
try:
    cx_Oracle.init_oracle_client(lib_dir="/path/to/oracle_client")
except Exception as e:
    logging.error(f"Could not initialize Oracle client: {e}")
    exit(1)

def check_oracle_access(username):
    """Check if the user has access to Oracle DB instances."""
    results = []

    for instance in DB_INSTANCES:
        try:
            connection = cx_Oracle.connect(DB_USER, DB_PASS, instance)
            cursor = connection.cursor()

            query = "SELECT username FROM dba_users WHERE username = :username"

            cursor.execute(query, {"username": username.upper()})
            result = cursor.fetchall()

            cursor.close()
            connection.close()

            if result:
                results.append(instance)
            else:
                logging.info(f"❌ {username} does NOT have Oracle access on {instance}.")

        except cx_Oracle.DatabaseError as e:
            logging.error(f"Failed to query Oracle instance {instance} for {username}: {e}")

    return results

def foundAccess(results, username, accessChoice):
    """Report user access status."""
    if results:
        if accessChoice == "check":
            logging.info(f"✅ {username} has Oracle access on: {', '.join(results)}.")
        elif accessChoice == "remove":
            logging.warning(f"⚠️ {username} has Oracle access, but automatic removal is NOT available. Please remove manually.")
    else:
        logging.info(f"❌ {username} does NOT have Oracle access.")

def main():
    """Main function to handle user separation for Oracle DB."""
    username = input("Enter LDAP username to check/remove: ").strip()
    accessChoice = input("Would you like to check or remove access? (Check/Remove): ").strip().lower()

    while accessChoice not in ("check", "remove"):
        accessChoice = input("Invalid input. Please enter 'Check' or 'Remove': ").strip().lower()

    results = check_oracle_access(username)
    foundAccess(results, username, accessChoice)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
next is pagerduty.py




import logging
import requests
import json
import secret

# Setup logging
logging.basicConfig(
    format="%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s",
    level=logging.INFO
)

# PagerDuty API Configuration
API_KEY = secret.get_secret("_PAGERDUTY_API_KEY")
URL = "https://api.pagerduty.com/users"

HEADERS = {
    "Authorization": f"Token token={API_KEY}",
    "Accept": "application/vnd.pagerduty+json;version=2",
    "Content-Type": "application/json"
}

def check_pagerduty_access(username):
    """Check if a user has access to PagerDuty."""
    params = {"query": username}
    
    try:
        response = requests.get(URL, headers=HEADERS, params=params)
        response.raise_for_status()
        data = response.json()

        users = data.get("users", [])
        if users:
            return users
        return None

    except requests.exceptions.RequestException as e:
        logging.error(f"Failed to fetch PagerDuty user data: {e}")
        return None

def remove_pagerduty_access(user_id):
    """Remove user from PagerDuty."""
    delete_url = f"{URL}/{user_id}"
    
    try:
        response = requests.delete(delete_url, headers=HEADERS)
        response.raise_for_status()

        if response.status_code == 204:
            logging.info(f"✅ Successfully removed user with ID {user_id} from PagerDuty.")
        else:
            logging.warning(f"⚠️ Unexpected response while removing user {user_id}: {response.status_code}")
    
    except requests.exceptions.RequestException as e:
        logging.error(f"Failed to remove PagerDuty user: {e}")

def foundAccess(user, accessChoice):
    """Handle found access logic."""
    user_data = check_pagerduty_access(user)
    
    if user_data:
        user_id = user_data[0]["id"]
        
        if accessChoice == "check":
            logging.info(f"✅ {user} has PagerDuty access.")
        elif accessChoice == "remove":
            logging.info(f"⚠️ {user} has PagerDuty access. Removing...")
            remove_pagerduty_access(user_id)
    else:
        logging.info(f"❌ {user} does NOT have PagerDuty access.")

def main():
    """Main function to handle user separation for PagerDuty."""
    username = input("Enter LDAP username to check/remove: ").strip()
    accessChoice = input("Would you like to check or remove access? (Check/Remove): ").strip().lower()

    while accessChoice not in ("check", "remove"):
        accessChoice = input("Invalid input. Please enter 'Check' or 'Remove': ").strip().lower()

    foundAccess(username, accessChoice)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
import logging
import psycopg2
import secret

# Setup logging
logging.basicConfig(
    format="%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s",
    level=logging.INFO
)

# Retrieve PostgreSQL Credentials
DB_USER = secret.get_secret('_PROD_POSTGRES_USER')
DB_PASS = secret.get_secret('_PROD_POSTGRES_PASS')

# Define PostgreSQL Hosts & Queries
DB_HOSTS = {
    "arcdb.sea1.marchex.com": {"dbname": "arc"},
    "audiencedb.som1.marchex.com": {"dbname": "audience"},
    "busmonitordb.sea1.marchex.com": {"dbname": "sqlmonitor"},
    "callanalyticsdb.som1.marchex.com": {"dbname": "call_analytics"},
    "cdrshepdb.sea1.marchex.com": {"dbname": "cdrshepherd"},
    "rtdb.sea1.marchex.com": {"dbname": "rt"},
    "jira.sea1.marchex.com": {"dbname": "jira"},
}

DB_QUERY = "SELECT usename FROM pg_catalog.pg_user WHERE usename ILIKE %s"

def connect_to_db(host, dbname):
    """Connect to a PostgreSQL database."""
    try:
        conn = psycopg2.connect(
            host=host,
            dbname=dbname,
            user=DB_USER,
            password=DB_PASS
        )
        return conn
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Failed to connect to {host}: {e}")
        return None

def check_user_access(user):
    """Check if a user has access to PostgreSQL databases."""
    found_databases = []

    for host, db_config in DB_HOSTS.items():
        conn = connect_to_db(host, db_config["dbname"])
        if not conn:
            continue
        
        try:
            cur = conn.cursor()
            cur.execute(DB_QUERY, (f"%{user}%",))
            if cur.fetchone():
                found_databases.append(host)
            
            cur.close()
            conn.close()
        except Exception as e:
            logging.error(f"⚠️ Query failed on {host}: {e}")
            continue

    return found_databases

def remove_user_access(user, databases):
    """Remove a user from the given PostgreSQL databases."""
    DROP_USER_QUERY = f"DROP USER IF EXISTS {user};"
    
    for host in databases:
        conn = connect_to_db(host, DB_HOSTS[host]["dbname"])
        if not conn:
            continue
        
        try:
            cur = conn.cursor()
            cur.execute(DROP_USER_QUERY)
            conn.commit()
            logging.info(f"✅ Successfully removed {user} from {host}")
            
            cur.close()
            conn.close()
        except Exception as e:
            logging.error(f"⚠️ Failed to remove {user} from {host}: {e}")

def main():
    """Main function to handle PostgreSQL user separation."""
    username = input("Enter LDAP username to check/remove: ").strip()
    accessChoice = input("Would you like to check or remove access? (Check/Remove): ").strip().lower()

    while accessChoice not in ("check", "remove"):
        accessChoice = input("Invalid input. Please enter 'Check' or 'Remove': ").strip().lower()

    databases = check_user_access(username)
    
    if databases:
        if accessChoice == "check":
            logging.info(f"✅ {username} has access to: {', '.join(databases)}")
        elif accessChoice == "remove":
            confirmation = input(f"⚠️ {username} has access to {len(databases)} databases. Proceed with removal? (y/n): ").strip().lower()
            if confirmation == "y":
                remove_user_access(username, databases)
            else:
                logging.info(f"❌ User {username} was NOT removed from PostgreSQL databases.")
    else:
        logging.info(f"❌ {username} does NOT have PostgreSQL access.")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
