import logging
import secret
import rt
from rt_marchex import rtbroker

# Setup logging
logging.basicConfig(
    format="%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s",
    level=logging.INFO
)

# Retrieve RT Credentials
RT_USER = secret.get_secret('_SOC_UI_USER')
RT_PASS = secret.get_secret('_SOC_UI_PASS')

# RT Server Info
RT_HOST = "https://rt.marchex.com"
RT_URL = "https://rt.marchex.com/REST/1.0"

RT_QUERY = (
    "Owner = '{user}' "
    "AND ( Status = 'new' OR Status = 'open')"
)

def loginToRT():
    """Log into the RT Ticketing system."""
    tracker = rt.Rt(RT_URL, RT_USER, RT_PASS)
    if not tracker.login():
        logging.error("❌ Failed to log in to RT.")
        return None
    return tracker

def main(user, creds):
    """Search for open tickets assigned to a given user in RT."""
    try:
        rtb = rtbroker(RT_HOST)
        rtb.loginUser(RT_USER, RT_PASS)

        tickets = rtb.ticket_search(RT_USER, RT_QUERY.format(user=user))
        
        if tickets:
            return (tickets, user, creds)
        else:
            return (None, user, creds)

    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Error querying RT for {user}: {e}")
        return (None, user, creds)

def foundAccess(result):
    """Determine if a user has RT tickets and handle removal if needed."""
    if result[0] is not None:
        accessChoice = result[2]["accessChoice"]
        
        if accessChoice == "check":
            logging.info(f"📌 RT Tickets found for {result[1]}:")
            for key, val in result[0].items():
                logging.info(f"🔹 {key}: {val}")

        elif accessChoice == "remove":
            logging.warning(f"⚠️ Attempting to reassign tickets for {result[1]}")
            stealTickets(result)

def stealTickets(result):
    """Reassign RT tickets from the user to another queue."""
    tracker = loginToRT()
    if not tracker:
        logging.error("❌ Unable to proceed with ticket reassignment due to login failure.")
        return

    for ticket_id in result[0].keys():
        try:
            tracker.edit_ticket(ticket_id, Queue="SOC")
            tracker.steal(ticket_id)
            tracker.edit_ticket(ticket_id, Owner=RT_USER, Queue="Production")
            logging.info(f"✅ Successfully reassigned ticket {ticket_id} from {result[1]}.")
        except Exception as e:
            logging.error(f"❌ Failed to reassign ticket {ticket_id} from {result[1]}: {e}")

def main_prompt():
    """Prompt user for input and initiate RT ticket separation process."""
    logging.info("🔍 Checking RT Tickets")
    
    sepList = input("Enter LDAP user(s) to be separated (comma-separated): ").split(",")
    accessChoice = input("Would you like to check or remove access? (Check/Remove): ").strip().lower()

    while accessChoice not in ("check", "remove"):
        accessChoice = input("Invalid input. Please enter 'Check' or 'Remove': ").strip().lower()

    creds = {"accessChoice": accessChoice}

    for user in sepList:
        result = main(user, creds)
        foundAccess(result)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main_prompt()

import pprint
import secret
from slackclient import SlackClient
import logging

slackToken = secret.get_secret('_SLACK_API_KEY')

# import logging above and these two statements squelch INFO and DEBUG printout during execution from separation.py
# this makes it so it will not print out anything below warning level (info and debug are below warning level)
logging.getLogger("requests").setLevel(logging.WARNING)
logging.getLogger("urllib3").setLevel(logging.WARNING)

def main(user,creds):
    sc = SlackClient(slackToken)
    users = sc.api_call("users.list")

    for i in users:
        for t in users['members']:
            if user in t['name']:
                if t['deleted'] == False:
                    member = user
                    break
            else:
                member = None

    return(member,user,creds)

def foundAccess(result):
    if result[0] is not None:
        accessChoice = result[2]['accessChoice']
        if accessChoice == 'check':
            print "{} has Slack access".format(result[1])
        if accessChoice == "remove":
            print "{} has Slack access, but automatic removal has not been implemented. Please remove manually".format(result[1])

if __name__ == '__main__':
    operatorUN = raw_input("Input your LDAP username: ")
    user = raw_input('Input user to check. If multiple, separate by commas: ').split(',')
    accessChoice = raw_input("Would you like to check or remove access? Check/Remove: ").lower()

    while True:
        if accessChoice not in ('remove','check'):
            accessChoice = raw_input("Sorry, looks like you misspelled 'remove' or 'check'. Please re-indicate if you'd like to remove all access or just check access.           Remove/Check: ").lower()
            continue
        else:
            accessChoice = accessChoice
            break

    inputDict = {}
    inputDict.update({'creds': {'accessChoice' : accessChoice}})
    creds = inputDict['creds']

    for u in user:
        result = main(u, creds)
        foundAccess(result)
import logging
import getpass
import ldap
import utils
import requests
import openpyxl
import os
import json
import rt
from concurrent.futures import ThreadPoolExecutor

# Setup logging
logging.basicConfig(
    format='%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s',
    level=logging.INFO
)

# 🟢 Enable Mock Mode for Safe Testing (Change to False for Live Runs)
MOCK_MODE = True  


# Systems that require separation processing
SYSTEMS_CATALOG = {
    "AdTrack": True,
    "AFR": True,
    "Auth0": True,
    "Avenger": True,
    "AWS": True,
    "ADO": True,
    "AzurePortal": True,
    "CallScoring": True,
    "Chef": True,
    "Cuttlefish": True,
    "EmailAccess": True,
    "Engage": True,
    "EquityEdge_GreatPlains": True,
    "GitHub": True,
    "Grafana": True,
    "Ipplan": True,
    "JIRA": True,
    "Marchex.io": True,
    "MI5": True,
    "Microsites": True,
    "NewRelic": True,
    "Nexus": True,
    "NimUI": True,
    "NISMaps": True,
    "OpenVPN": True,
    "PagerDuty": True,
    "Pulley": True,
    "Postman": True,
    "RT": True, # Checking RT for past access requests
    "Slack": True,
    "MarketingEdge": True,
    "Sendgrid": True,
    "Sentry": True,
    "Snowflake": True,
    "TACACS": True,  # Needs special handling (SEV5 ticket)
    "Wallace": True,
    "XMSHammer": True
}

ACCESS_LIST = [system for system, enabled in SYSTEMS_CATALOG.items() if enabled]
MISSING_SCRIPTS = []

# LDAP Configurations
LDAP_ADDR = 'ldaps://ldap.sea.marchex.com:636/'
LDAP_BASEDN = 'ou=users,dc=marchex,dc=com'
LDAP_BINDDN = 'uid={user},ou=users,dc=marchex,dc=com'
LDAP_SF = '(cn={user})'

# RT (Request Tracker) Configuration
RT_HOST = 'https://rt.marchex.com'
RT_URL = 'https://rt.marchex.com/REST/1.0'
RT_USER = "socbot"  # Replace with actual RT user
RT_PASS = "securepass"  # Replace with actual RT password

# High Priority Contact List Location
HIGH_PRI_FILE = r'\\marchex\files\soc\Emergency\High Priority Contact List\NOCHighPriorityContactList1.xlsx'

# Don't require signed cert for LDAP connection
ldap.set_option(ldap.OPT_X_TLS_REQUIRE_CERT, ldap.OPT_X_TLS_NEVER)


def get_user_input(prompt):
    """Wrapper for input to handle common input scenarios."""
    try:
        return input(prompt).strip()
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Error getting user input: {e}")
        return None


def get_directory_info(user):
    """Query Directory Manager for user alias & manager name."""
    directory_url = f"https://directorymanager.marchex.com/api/user/{user}"
    try:
        response = requests.get(directory_url)
        response.raise_for_status()
        user_data = response.json()
        return user_data.get('alias', 'Unknown'), user_data.get('manager', 'Unknown')
    except Exception as e:
        logging.warning(f"Failed to retrieve Directory Manager info for {user}: {e}")
        return 'Unknown', 'Unknown'


def check_rt_for_access_tickets(user):
    """Check RT (Request Tracker) for past access requests related to this user."""
    logging.info(f"Checking RT for past access requests related to {user}...")
    query = f"Owner = '{user}' AND (Status = 'new' OR Status = 'open')"
    tracker = rt.Rt(RT_URL, RT_USER, RT_PASS)
    if not tracker.login():
        logging.error("Failed to authenticate with RT.")
        return
    try:
        tickets = tracker.search(Queue="SOC", raw_query=query)
        if tickets:
            logging.info(f"User {user} has {len(tickets)} past access tickets in RT.")
            for ticket in tickets:
                logging.info(f"RT Ticket Found: {ticket['id']} - {ticket['Subject']}")
        else:
            logging.info(f"No previous access tickets found in RT for {user}.")
    except Exception as e:
        logging.warning(f"Error checking RT for {user}: {e}")


def check_high_priority_contact_list(user):
    """Check and remove user from High Priority Contact List."""
    if not os.path.exists(HIGH_PRI_FILE):
        logging.warning("High Priority Contact List file not found.")
        return
    try:
        wb = openpyxl.load_workbook(HIGH_PRI_FILE)
        sheet = wb.active
        for row in sheet.iter_rows():
            for cell in row:
                if str(user).lower() in str(cell.value).lower():
                    logging.info(f"Removing {user} from High Priority Contact List.")
                    cell.value = None
                    wb.save(HIGH_PRI_FILE)
                    return
        logging.info(f"{user} not found in High Priority Contact List.")
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Error modifying High Priority Contact List: {e}")


def submit_sev5_ticket_for_TACACS(user):
    """Submit a SEV5 ticket to NetEng for TACACS removal."""
    logging.info(f"Submitting SEV5 ticket for TACACS removal for {user}.")
    
    # Simulated API request
    ticket_payload = {
        "summary": f"SEV5 - Remove TACACS access for {user}",
        "description": f"User {user} requires TACACS access removal as part of separation.",
        "priority": "SEV5",
        "assigned_team": "NetEng"
    }
    try:
        response = requests.post("https://ticketing.marchex.com/api/tickets", json=ticket_payload)
        response.raise_for_status()
        logging.info(f"SEV5 ticket successfully created for TACACS removal: {response.json().get('ticket_id')}")
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Failed to create SEV5 ticket for TACACS: {e}")


def main():
    """ Main function for the separation script. """
    logging.info("########### SEPARATION SCRIPT #############")
    operatorUN = get_user_input("Enter your LDAP username: ")
    operatorPass = getpass.getpass("Enter your LDAP password: ")

    # Gather usernames to be separated
    sepList = get_user_input("Enter LDAP user(s) to be separated (comma-separated): ").split(',')

    # Check if user is a vendor
    while True:
        isVendor = get_user_input("Is this user a vendor? (yes/no): ").lower()
        if isVendor in ('yes', 'no'):
            break
        logging.warning("Invalid input. Please enter 'yes' or 'no'.")
    vendorEmail = None
    if isVendor == "yes":
        if any(sys in ACCESS_LIST for sys in ["PagerDuty", "Microsites"]):
            vendorEmail = get_user_input("Enter vendor email address: ")
        else:
            logging.info("Vendor email not needed for selected systems.")

    # Ask if we are checking or removing access
    while True:
        accessChoice = get_user_input("Would you like to remove all found access or just check access? (Remove/Check): ").lower()
        if accessChoice in ('remove', 'check'):
            break
        logging.warning("Invalid input. Please enter 'Remove' or 'Check'.")
    
    creds = {
        "operatorUN": operatorUN,
        "operatorPass": operatorPass,
        "sepList": sepList,
        "accessChoice": accessChoice,
        "vendorEmail": vendorEmail,
        "MOCK_MODE": MOCK_MODE  # 🟢 Global Mock Mode Toggle
    }

    try:
        ldp = ldap.initialize(LDAP_ADDR)
        ldp.simple_bind_s(LDAP_BINDDN.format(user=operatorUN), operatorPass)
    except ldap.INVALID_CREDENTIALS:
        logging.error("LDAP authentication failed. Exiting.")
        return
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Unexpected LDAP error: {e}")
        return
    
    with ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=5) as executor:
        executor.map(lambda user: process_user(ldp, user, creds), sepList)

    logging.info(f"####### No further access found for {user} #######")
    
    if MISSING_SCRIPTS:
        logging.warning(f"Missing separation scripts: {', '.join(set(MISSING_SCRIPTS))}")


def process_user(ldp, user, creds):
    """Process separation for an individual user."""
    try:
        alias, manager = get_directory_info(user)
        logging.info(f"User {user} Alias: {alias}, Manager: {manager}")
        check_rt_for_access_tickets(user)
        if ldapQuery(ldp, user):
            checkAccess(user, creds)
        check_high_priority_contact_list(user)
        if "TACACS" in ACCESS_LIST:
            submit_sev5_ticket_for_TACACS(user)
        logging.info(f"####### No further access found for {user} #######")
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Error processing user {user}: {e}")


def ldapQuery(ldp, user):
    """Check if user exists in LDAP."""
    logging.info(f"Checking LDAP access for {user}...")
    try:
        result_id = ldp.search(LDAP_BASEDN, ldap.SCOPE_SUBTREE, LDAP_SF.format(user=user))
        result_type, result_data = ldp.result(result_id, 0)
        if not result_data:
            logging.warning(f"User {user} not found in LDAP.")
            return False
        return True
    except ldap.LDAPError as e:
        logging.error(f"LDAP query failed for {user}: {e}")
        return False


def checkAccess(user, creds):
    """Run access removal scripts."""
    global MISSING_SCRIPTS 
    logging.info(f"Checking access for {user}...")
    for system in ACCESS_LIST:
        try:
            sep_module = __import__(f"separations.{system.lower()}", fromlist=[""])
            sep_module.main(user, creds)
        except ImportError:
            MISSING_SCRIPTS.append(system)
        except Exception as e:
            logging.error(f"Error running {system} separation: {e}")


if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

def main():
    """ Main function for the separation script. """
    logging.info("########### SEPARATION SCRIPT #############")
    operatorUN = get_user_input("Enter your LDAP username: ")
    operatorPass = getpass.getpass("Enter your LDAP password: ")

    # Gather usernames to be separated
    sepList = get_user_input("Enter LDAP user(s) to be separated (comma-separated): ").split(',')

    # Check if user is a vendor
    while True:
        isVendor = get_user_input("Is this user a vendor? (yes/no): ").lower()
        if isVendor in ('yes', 'no'):
            break
        logging.warning("Invalid input. Please enter 'yes' or 'no'.")

    vendorEmail = None
    if isVendor == "yes":
        if any(sys in ACCESS_LIST for sys in ["PagerDuty", "Microsites"]):
            vendorEmail = get_user_input("Enter vendor email address: ")
        else:
            logging.info("Vendor email not needed for selected systems.")

    # Ask if we are checking or removing access
    while True:
        accessChoice = get_user_input("Would you like to remove all found access or just check access? (Remove/Check): ").lower()
        if accessChoice in ('remove', 'check'):
            break
        logging.warning("Invalid input. Please enter 'Remove' or 'Check'.")
    
    creds = {
        "operatorUN": operatorUN,
        "operatorPass": operatorPass,
        "sepList": sepList,
        "accessChoice": accessChoice,
        "vendorEmail": vendorEmail,
        "MOCK_MODE": MOCK_MODE  # 🟢 Global Mock Mode Toggle CLI Controlled
    }

    try:
        ldp = ldap.initialize(LDAP_ADDR)
        ldp.simple_bind_s(LDAP_BINDDN.format(user=operatorUN), operatorPass)
    except ldap.INVALID_CREDENTIALS:
        logging.error("LDAP authentication failed. Exiting.")
        return
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Unexpected LDAP error: {e}")
        return
    
    with ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=5) as executor:
        executor.map(lambda user: process_user(ldp, user, creds), sepList)

    logging.info(f"####### No further access found for {user} #######")
    
    if MISSING_SCRIPTS:
        logging.warning(f"Missing separation scripts: {', '.join(set(MISSING_SCRIPTS))}")


def process_user(ldp, user, creds):
    """Process separation for an individual user."""
    try:
        logging.info(f"Processing user: {user}")
        if "MOCK_MODE" in creds and creds["MOCK_MODE"]:
            logging.info(f"[MOCK] Simulating access removal for {user}.")
            return
        
        check_rt_for_access_tickets(user)
        if ldapQuery(ldp, user):
            checkAccess(user, creds)
        check_high_priority_contact_list(user)
        if "TACACS" in ACCESS_LIST:
            submit_sev5_ticket_for_TACACS(user)
        logging.info(f"####### No further access found for {user} #######")
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Error processing user {user}: {e}")


def ldapQuery(ldp, user):
    """Check if user exists in LDAP."""
    logging.info(f"Checking LDAP access for {user}...")
    try:
        result_id = ldp.search(LDAP_BASEDN, ldap.SCOPE_SUBTREE, LDAP_SF.format(user=user))
        result_type, result_data = ldp.result(result_id, 0)
        if not result_data:
            logging.warning(f"User {user} not found in LDAP.")
            return False
        return True
    except ldap.LDAPError as e:
        logging.error(f"LDAP query failed for {user}: {e}")
        return False


def checkAccess(user, creds):
    """Run access removal scripts."""
    global MISSING_SCRIPTS 
    logging.info(f"Checking access for {user}...")
    for system in ACCESS_LIST:
        try:
            sep_module = __import__(f"separations.{system.lower()}", fromlist=[""])
            sep_module.main(user, creds)
        except ImportError:
            MISSING_SCRIPTS.append(system)
        except Exception as e:
            logging.error(f"Error running {system} separation: {e}")


if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

import logging
import getpass
import ldap3 as ldap
import utils
import requests
import openpyxl
import os
import json
import rt
from concurrent.futures import ThreadPoolExecutor

# Setup logging
logging.basicConfig(
    format='%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s',
    level=logging.INFO
)

# 🟢 Mock Mode (Secret Backdoor Enabled)
MOCK_MODE = False  # Default is OFF

# 🔐 Secret Backdoor Command (Toggle Mock Mode)
secret_command = getpass.getpass("Enter command or press Enter to continue: ").strip().lower()
if secret_command == "testmode":
    MOCK_MODE = True
    logging.warning("🚀 Test Mode Activated: Mock Mode is ENABLED.")
else:
    logging.info("Running in LIVE Mode.")

# Systems that require separation processing
SYSTEMS_CATALOG = {
    "AdTrack": True,
    "AFR": True,
    "Auth0": True,
    "Avenger": True,
    "AWS": True,
    "ADO": True,
    "AzurePortal": True,
    "CallScoring": True,
    "Chef": True,
    "Cuttlefish": True,
    "EmailAccess": True,
    "Engage": True,
    "EquityEdge_GreatPlains": True,
    "GitHub": True,
    "Grafana": True,
    "Ipplan": True,
    "JIRA": True,
    "Marchex.io": True,
    "MI5": True,
    "Microsites": True,
    "NewRelic": True,
    "Nexus": True,
    "NimUI": True,
    "NISMaps": True,
    "OpenVPN": True,
    "PagerDuty": True,
    "Pulley": True,
    "Postman": True,
    "RT": True, # Checking RT for past access requests
    "Slack": True,
    "MarketingEdge": True,
    "Sendgrid": True,
    "Sentry": True,
    "Snowflake": True,
    "TACACS": True,  # Needs special handling (SEV5 ticket)
    "Wallace": True,
    "XMSHammer": True
}

ACCESS_LIST = [system for system, enabled in SYSTEMS_CATALOG.items() if enabled]
MISSING_SCRIPTS = []

# LDAP Configurations
LDAP_ADDR = 'ldaps://ldap.sea.marchex.com:636/'
LDAP_BASEDN = 'ou=users,dc=marchex,dc=com'
LDAP_BINDDN = 'uid={user},ou=users,dc=marchex,dc=com'
LDAP_SF = '(cn={user})'

# RT (Request Tracker) Configuration
RT_HOST = 'https://rt.marchex.com'
RT_URL = 'https://rt.marchex.com/REST/1.0'
RT_USER = "socbot"  # Replace with actual RT user
RT_PASS = "securepass"  # Replace with actual RT password

# High Priority Contact List Location
HIGH_PRI_FILE = r'\\marchex\files\soc\Emergency\High Priority Contact List\NOCHighPriorityContactList1.xlsx'

# Don't require signed cert for LDAP connection
ldap.set_option(ldap.OPT_X_TLS_REQUIRE_CERT, ldap.OPT_X_TLS_NEVER)


def get_user_input(prompt):
    """Wrapper for input to handle common input scenarios."""
    try:
        return input(prompt).strip()
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Error getting user input: {e}")
        return None


def get_directory_info(user):
    """Query Directory Manager for user alias & manager name."""
    directory_url = f"https://directorymanager.marchex.com/api/user/{user}"
    try:
        response = requests.get(directory_url)
        response.raise_for_status()
        user_data = response.json()
        return user_data.get('alias', 'Unknown'), user_data.get('manager', 'Unknown')
    except Exception as e:
        logging.warning(f"Failed to retrieve Directory Manager info for {user}: {e}")
        return 'Unknown', 'Unknown'


def check_rt_for_access_tickets(user):
    """Check RT (Request Tracker) for past access requests related to this user."""
    logging.info(f"Checking RT for past access requests related to {user}...")
    query = f"Owner = '{user}' AND (Status = 'new' OR Status = 'open')"
    tracker = rt.Rt(RT_URL, RT_USER, RT_PASS)
    if not tracker.login():
        logging.error("Failed to authenticate with RT.")
        return
    try:
        tickets = tracker.search(Queue="SOC", raw_query=query)
        if tickets:
            logging.info(f"User {user} has {len(tickets)} past access tickets in RT.")
            for ticket in tickets:
                logging.info(f"RT Ticket Found: {ticket['id']} - {ticket['Subject']}")
        else:
            logging.info(f"No previous access tickets found in RT for {user}.")
    except Exception as e:
        logging.warning(f"Error checking RT for {user}: {e}")


def check_high_priority_contact_list(user):
    """Check and remove user from High Priority Contact List."""
    if not os.path.exists(HIGH_PRI_FILE):
        logging.warning("High Priority Contact List file not found.")
        return
    try:
        wb = openpyxl.load_workbook(HIGH_PRI_FILE)
        sheet = wb.active
        for row in sheet.iter_rows():
            for cell in row:
                if str(user).lower() in str(cell.value).lower():
                    logging.info(f"Removing {user} from High Priority Contact List.")
                    cell.value = None
                    wb.save(HIGH_PRI_FILE)
                    return
        logging.info(f"{user} not found in High Priority Contact List.")
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Error modifying High Priority Contact List: {e}")


def submit_sev5_ticket_for_TACACS(user):
    """Submit a SEV5 ticket to NetEng for TACACS removal."""
    logging.info(f"Submitting SEV5 ticket for TACACS removal for {user}.")
    
    # Simulated API request
    ticket_payload = {
        "summary": f"SEV5 - Remove TACACS access for {user}",
        "description": f"User {user} requires TACACS access removal as part of separation.",
        "priority": "SEV5",
        "assigned_team": "NetEng"
    }
    try:
        response = requests.post("https://ticketing.marchex.com/api/tickets", json=ticket_payload)
        response.raise_for_status()
        logging.info(f"SEV5 ticket successfully created for TACACS removal: {response.json().get('ticket_id')}")
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Failed to create SEV5 ticket for TACACS: {e}")


def main():
    """ Main function for the separation script. """
    logging.info("########### SEPARATION SCRIPT #############")
    operatorUN = get_user_input("Enter your LDAP username: ")
    operatorPass = getpass.getpass("Enter your LDAP password: ")

    # Gather usernames to be separated
    sepList = get_user_input("Enter LDAP user(s) to be separated (comma-separated): ").split(',')

    # Check if user is a vendor
    while True:
        isVendor = get_user_input("Is this user a vendor? (yes/no): ").lower()
        if isVendor in ('yes', 'no'):
            break
        logging.warning("Invalid input. Please enter 'yes' or 'no'.")

    vendorEmail = None
    if isVendor == "yes":
        if any(sys in ACCESS_LIST for sys in ["PagerDuty", "Microsites"]):
            vendorEmail = get_user_input("Enter vendor email address: ")
        else:
            logging.info("Vendor email not needed for selected systems.")

    # Ask if we are checking or removing access
    while True:
        accessChoice = get_user_input("Would you like to remove all found access or just check access? (Remove/Check): ").lower()
        if accessChoice in ('remove', 'check'):
            break
        logging.warning("Invalid input. Please enter 'Remove' or 'Check'.")
    
    creds = {
        "operatorUN": operatorUN,
        "operatorPass": operatorPass,
        "sepList": sepList,
        "accessChoice": accessChoice,
        "vendorEmail": vendorEmail,
        "MOCK_MODE": MOCK_MODE  # 🟢 Global Mock Mode Toggle CLI Controlled
    }

    try:
        ldp = ldap.initialize(LDAP_ADDR)
        ldp.simple_bind_s(LDAP_BINDDN.format(user=operatorUN), operatorPass)
    except ldap.INVALID_CREDENTIALS:
        logging.error("LDAP authentication failed. Exiting.")
        return
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Unexpected LDAP error: {e}")
        return
    
    with ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=5) as executor:
        executor.map(lambda user: process_user(ldp, user, creds), sepList)

    logging.info(f"####### No further access found for {user} #######")
    
    if MISSING_SCRIPTS:
        logging.warning(f"Missing separation scripts: {', '.join(set(MISSING_SCRIPTS))}")


def process_user(ldp, user, creds):
    """Process separation for an individual user."""
    try:
        logging.info(f"Processing user: {user}")
        if "MOCK_MODE" in creds and creds["MOCK_MODE"]:
            logging.info(f"[MOCK] Simulating access removal for {user}.")
            return
        
        check_rt_for_access_tickets(user)
        if ldapQuery(ldp, user):
            checkAccess(user, creds)
        check_high_priority_contact_list(user)
        if "TACACS" in ACCESS_LIST:
            submit_sev5_ticket_for_TACACS(user)
        logging.info(f"####### No further access found for {user} #######")
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Error processing user {user}: {e}")


def ldapQuery(ldp, user):
    """Check if user exists in LDAP."""
    logging.info(f"Checking LDAP access for {user}...")

    try:
        ldp.search(LDAP_BASEDN, f"(cn={user})", ldap3.SUBTREE)
        if not ldp.entries:
            logging.warning(f"User {user} not found in LDAP.")
            return False
        return True
    except ldap3.LDAPException as e:
        logging.error(f"LDAP query failed for {user}: {e}")
        return False


def checkAccess(user, creds):
    """Run access removal scripts."""
    global MISSING_SCRIPTS 
    logging.info(f"Checking access for {user}...")
    for system in ACCESS_LIST:
        try:
            sep_module = __import__(f"separations.{system.lower()}", fromlist=[""])
            sep_module.main(user, creds)
        except ImportError:
            MISSING_SCRIPTS.append(system)
        except Exception as e:
            logging.error(f"Error running {system} separation: {e}")


if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

    "MarketingEdge": True,
    "Sendgrid": True,
    "Sentry": True,
    "Snowflake": True,
    "TACACS": True,  # Needs special handling (SEV5 ticket)
    "Wallace": True,
    "XMSHammer": True
}

ACCESS_LIST = [system for system, enabled in SYSTEMS_CATALOG.items() if enabled]
MISSING_SCRIPTS = []

# LDAP Configurations
LDAP_ADDR = 'ldaps://ldap.sea.marchex.com:636/'
LDAP_BASEDN = 'ou=users,dc=marchex,dc=com'
LDAP_BINDDN = 'uid={user},ou=users,dc=marchex,dc=com'
LDAP_SF = '(cn={user})'

# RT (Request Tracker) Configuration
RT_HOST = 'https://rt.marchex.com'
RT_URL = 'https://rt.marchex.com/REST/1.0'
RT_USER = "socbot"  # Replace with actual RT user
RT_PASS = "securepass"  # Replace with actual RT password

# High Priority Contact List Location
HIGH_PRI_FILE = r'\\marchex\files\soc\Emergency\High Priority Contact List\NOCHighPriorityContactList1.xlsx'

# Don't require signed cert for LDAP connection
ldap.set_option(ldap.OPT_X_TLS_REQUIRE_CERT, ldap.OPT_X_TLS_NEVER)


def get_user_input(prompt):
    """Wrapper for input to handle common input scenarios."""
    try:
        return input(prompt).strip()
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Error getting user input: {e}")
        return None


def get_directory_info(user):
    """Query Directory Manager for user alias & manager name."""
    directory_url = f"https://directorymanager.marchex.com/api/user/{user}"
    try:
        response = requests.get(directory_url)
        response.raise_for_status()
        user_data = response.json()
        return user_data.get('alias', 'Unknown'), user_data.get('manager', 'Unknown')
    except Exception as e:
        logging.warning(f"Failed to retrieve Directory Manager info for {user}: {e}")
        return 'Unknown', 'Unknown'


def check_rt_for_access_tickets(user):
    """Check RT (Request Tracker) for past access requests related to this user."""
    logging.info(f"Checking RT for past access requests related to {user}...")
    query = f"Owner = '{user}' AND (Status = 'new' OR Status = 'open')"
    tracker = rt.Rt(RT_URL, RT_USER, RT_PASS)
    if not tracker.login():
        logging.error("Failed to authenticate with RT.")
        return
    try:
        tickets = tracker.search(Queue="SOC", raw_query=query)
        if tickets:
            logging.info(f"User {user} has {len(tickets)} past access tickets in RT.")
            for ticket in tickets:
                logging.info(f"RT Ticket Found: {ticket['id']} - {ticket['Subject']}")
        else:
            logging.info(f"No previous access tickets found in RT for {user}.")
    except Exception as e:
        logging.warning(f"Error checking RT for {user}: {e}")


def check_high_priority_contact_list(user):
    """Check and remove user from High Priority Contact List."""
    if not os.path.exists(HIGH_PRI_FILE):
        logging.warning("High Priority Contact List file not found.")
        return
    try:
        wb = openpyxl.load_workbook(HIGH_PRI_FILE)
        sheet = wb.active
        for row in sheet.iter_rows():
            for cell in row:
                if str(user).lower() in str(cell.value).lower():
                    logging.info(f"Removing {user} from High Priority Contact List.")
                    cell.value = None
                    wb.save(HIGH_PRI_FILE)
                    return
        logging.info(f"{user} not found in High Priority Contact List.")
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Error modifying High Priority Contact List: {e}")


def submit_sev5_ticket_for_TACACS(user):
    """Submit a SEV5 ticket to NetEng for TACACS removal."""
    logging.info(f"Submitting SEV5 ticket for TACACS removal for {user}.")
    
    # Simulated API request
    ticket_payload = {
        "summary": f"SEV5 - Remove TACACS access for {user}",
        "description": f"User {user} requires TACACS access removal as part of separation.",
        "priority": "SEV5",
        "assigned_team": "NetEng"
    }
    try:
        response = requests.post("https://ticketing.marchex.com/api/tickets", json=ticket_payload)
        response.raise_for_status()
        logging.info(f"SEV5 ticket successfully created for TACACS removal: {response.json().get('ticket_id')}")
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Failed to create SEV5 ticket for TACACS: {e}")


def main():
    """ Main function for the separation script. """
    logging.info("########### SEPARATION SCRIPT #############")
    operatorUN = get_user_input("Enter your LDAP username: ")
    operatorPass = getpass.getpass("Enter your LDAP password: ")

    # Gather usernames to be separated
    sepList = get_user_input("Enter LDAP user(s) to be separated (comma-separated): ").split(',')

    # Check if user is a vendor
    while True:
        isVendor = get_user_input("Is this user a vendor? (yes/no): ").lower()
        if isVendor in ('yes', 'no'):
            break
        logging.warning("Invalid input. Please enter 'yes' or 'no'.")

    vendorEmail = None
    if isVendor == "yes":
        if any(sys in ACCESS_LIST for sys in ["PagerDuty", "Microsites"]):
            vendorEmail = get_user_input("Enter vendor email address: ")
        else:
            logging.info("Vendor email not needed for selected systems.")

    # Ask if we are checking or removing access
    while True:
        accessChoice = get_user_input("Would you like to remove all found access or just check access? (Remove/Check): ").lower()
        if accessChoice in ('remove', 'check'):
            break
        logging.warning("Invalid input. Please enter 'Remove' or 'Check'.")
    
    creds = {
        "operatorUN": operatorUN,
        "operatorPass": operatorPass,
        "sepList": sepList,
        "accessChoice": accessChoice,
        "vendorEmail": vendorEmail,
        "MOCK_MODE": MOCK_MODE  # 🟢 Global Mock Mode Toggle CLI Controlled
    }

    try:
        ldp = ldap.initialize(LDAP_ADDR)
        ldp.simple_bind_s(LDAP_BINDDN.format(user=operatorUN), operatorPass)
    except ldap.INVALID_CREDENTIALS:
        logging.error("LDAP authentication failed. Exiting.")
        return
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Unexpected LDAP error: {e}")
        return
    
    with ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=5) as executor:
        executor.map(lambda user: process_user(ldp, user, creds), sepList)

    logging.info(f"####### No further access found for {user} #######")
    
    if MISSING_SCRIPTS:
        logging.warning(f"Missing separation scripts: {', '.join(set(MISSING_SCRIPTS))}")


def process_user(ldp, user, creds):
    """Process separation for an individual user."""
    try:
        logging.info(f"Processing user: {user}")
        if "MOCK_MODE" in creds and creds["MOCK_MODE"]:
            logging.info(f"[MOCK] Simulating access removal for {user}.")
            return
        
        check_rt_for_access_tickets(user)
        if ldapQuery(ldp, user):
            checkAccess(user, creds)
        check_high_priority_contact_list(user)
        if "TACACS" in ACCESS_LIST:
            submit_sev5_ticket_for_TACACS(user)
        logging.info(f"####### No further access found for {user} #######")
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Error processing user {user}: {e}")


def ldapQuery(ldp, user):
    """Check if user exists in LDAP."""
    logging.info(f"Checking LDAP access for {user}...")

    try:
        ldp.search(LDAP_BASEDN, f"(cn={user})", ldap3.SUBTREE)
        if not ldp.entries:
            logging.warning(f"User {user} not found in LDAP.")
            return False
        return True
    except ldap3.LDAPException as e:
        logging.error(f"LDAP query failed for {user}: {e}")
        return False


def checkAccess(user, creds):
    """Run access removal scripts."""
    global MISSING_SCRIPTS 
    logging.info(f"Checking access for {user}...")
    for system in ACCESS_LIST:
        try:
            sep_module = __import__(f"separations.{system.lower()}", fromlist=[""])
            sep_module.main(user, creds)
        except ImportError:
            MISSING_SCRIPTS.append(system)
        except Exception as e:
            logging.error(f"Error running {system} separation: {e}")


if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

import urllib
import urllib2
import re
import dateutil.parser
import logging
# http://requesttracker.wikia.com/wiki/REST

#dict = {'Queue':'Production','Requestor':'mmason','Subject':'Zenbot Test','Owner':'mmason','Status':'open','CF':{'Severity':'5'},'Text':"I don't usually test my code.\n\nBut when I do so, I do it in production.\n(Test for custom RT module)"}

class Error(Exception):
    pass

class AuthorizationError(Error):
    """ Authorization Error

    Raised whenever the REST API responds with a 401 (Unauthorized)
    response code. Also raised when supplied credentials are incorrect
    on loginUser().
    """
    pass

class UnexpectedResponse(Error):
    """ Unexpected Response from RT

    Raised when the response from the REST API could not be parsed by
    this package, or when the response contains information which is
    never expected.
    """
    pass

class ConnectionError(Error):
    """ Connection Error

    Currently, only raised on init. This is raised when the url specified
    for RT could not be reached, or when the response from that URL does not
    look like RT.
    """
    pass

class InvalidQueryError(Error):
    """ Invalid Query Error

    Raised if required parameters for a function (RT query) are not given.

    Honestly, this should be removed and replaced by built-in functionality
    of python. Think **kwargs.
    """
    pass

# RT Client
class rtbroker:

    _rt_format = re.compile(r'^(RT/.*?) (.*?) (.*?)')
    @staticmethod
    def rt_format(header):
        out = rtbroker._rt_format.match(header)
        if out:
            return out.groups()
        return None


    def __init__(self, url):
        try:
            response = urllib2.urlopen(url + '/REST/1.0/')
            header = rtbroker.rt_format(response.readline())
            if not header:
                raise ConnectionError("Could not connect to RT: bad header")
            self.url = url + '/REST/1.0/'
            self.cookies = {}
        except Exception as err:
            raise ConnectionError("Could not connect to RT: " + str(err))
        logging.getLogger(__name__)
        logging.basicConfig(level=logging.DEBUG)

    def loginUser(self, username, password):
        auth = "?user={0}&pass={1}".format(username, password)
        result = urllib2.urlopen(self.url + auth)
        if result.code != 200:
            raise UnexpectedResponse(result.code)

        response = result.read()
        header = rtbroker.rt_format(response)

        if not header:
            raise UnexpectedResponse(response)

        if header[1] == '200':
            self.cookies[username] = result.headers['Set-Cookie']
        elif header[1] == '401':
            raise AuthorizationError("Could not log in to RT with provided credentials")
        else:
            raise Error(data)
        self.connected = True

    # Move to meta subclass?
    def listUsers(self):
        return self.cookies.keys()

    def logoutUser(self, user):
        self.cookies

    def _request(self, user, path, data=None, params=None):
        if not user in self.cookies:
            raise AuthorizationError("User '%s' is not logged in", user)

        params = urllib.urlencode(params or {})
        #logging.debug("Fetching request: %s", self.url + path + '?' + params)

        if data:
            request = urllib2.Request(self.url + path + '?' + params, data,
                    headers={'Cookie': self.cookies[user]})
        else:
            request = urllib2.Request(self.url + path + '?' + params,
                    headers={'Cookie': self.cookies[user]})
        response = urllib2.urlopen(request)

        if response.code != 200:
            raise UnexpectedResponse(response.code)

        header = rtbroker.rt_format(response.readline())
        data = response.read()
        comments = re.findall(r'#.*',data)
        if header[1] == '200':
            return self._parse(data)
        elif header[1] == '401':
            raise AuthorizationError(' '.join(comments))
        else:
            raise Error(' '.join(header)+' '.join(comments))

    def _parse(self, text):
        result = {}
        rows = text.split("\n")
        count = len(rows)
        i = 1 # Skip header
        key = ''
        while i < count:
            if rows[i] == '' or rows[i] == 'No matching results.' or rows[i].startswith(('#','>')):
                pass
            elif rows[i].startswith(' ' * 9):
                result[key] += "\n" + rows[i][9:]
            else:
                try:
                    key, value = rows[i].split(':',1)
                    if key.startswith("CF."):
                        # Remove wrapping ex: "CF.{Severity}"
                        result[key[4:-1]] = value.strip()
                    else:
                        result[key] = value.strip()
                except ValueError:
                    logging.warn('RT could not parse string "%s" from \'%s\'',
                                    rows[i], rows[2])
                    pass
            i += 1
        if 'Created' in result:
            result['Created'] = dateutil.parser.parse(result['Created'])
        if 'LastUpdated' in result:
            result['LastUpdated'] = dateutil.parser.parse(result['LastUpdated'])
        if 'Started' in result:
            result['Started'] = dateutil.parser.parse(result['Started'])
        return result

    def ticket_search(self, user, query):
        return self._request(user, 'search/ticket', params={'query': query})

    def ticket(self, user, id):
        return self._request(user, 'ticket/' + str(id))

    def ticket_links(self, user, id):
        links = self._request(user, 'ticket/' + str(id) + '/links')
        for key in links:
            m = re.search(r'\d+$', links[key])
            links[key] = int(m.group(0))
        return links

    def ticket_new(self, user, dict):
        dict['id'] = "ticket/new"
        if any(k not in dict for k in ('Queue','Requestor','Subject','Owner','Status','Text')):
            raise InvalidQueryError("Required fields missing")

        dict['Text'].replace("\n", "\n ")
        if 'CF' in dict:
            for key, val in dict['CF'].iteritems():
                dict['CF-' + key] = val
            del dict['CF']

        raw = ''
        for key, val in dict.iteritems():
            raw += key + ': ' + val + "\n"
        data = urllib.urlencode({'content': raw})
        self._request(user, 'ticket/new', data)

    def ticket_edit(self, user, id, dict):
        if 'CF' in dict:
            for key, val in dict['CF'].iteritems():
                dict['CF-' + key] = val
            del dict['CF']

        if 'Text' in dict:
            dict['Comment'].replace("\n", "\n ")

        raw = ''
        for key, val in dict.iteritems():
            raw += key + ': ' + val + "\n"
        data = urllib.urlencode({'content': raw})
        self._request(user, 'ticket/' + id + '/edit', data)

    def ticket_resolve(self, user, id):
        data = urllib.urlencode({'content': 'Status: resolved'})
        self._request(user, 'ticket/' + id + '/edit', data)

    def ticket_comment(self, user, id, comment, dict={}):
        dict['id'] = id
        dict['Action'] = 'comment'
        dict['Text'] = comment.replace("\n", "\n ")
        # TODO: Add cc/bcc from dict
        raw = ''
        for key, val in dict.iteritems():
            raw += key + ': ' + val + "\n"
        data = urllib.urlencode({'content': raw})
        self._request(user, 'ticket/' + id + '/comment', data)

    def ticket_reply(self, user, id, reply, dict={}):
        dict['id'] = str(id)
        dict['Action'] = 'correspond'
        dict['Text'] = reply.replace("\n", "\n ")
        # TODO: Add cc/bcc from dict
        raw = ''
        for key, val in dict.iteritems():
            raw += key + ': ' + val + "\n"
        data = urllib.urlencode({'content': raw})
        self._request(user, 'ticket/' + id + '/comment', data)

from __future__ import print_function
import logging
import sys

class bcolors:
	HEADER = '\033[95m'
	OKBLUE = '\033[94m'
	OKGREEN = '\033[92m'
	WARNING = '\033[93m' # yellow
	FAIL = '\033[91m'    # red
	ENDC = '\033[0m'
	BOLD = '\033[1m'
	UNDERLINE = '\033[4m'

def header(text):
	return bcolors.HEADER + str(text) + bcolors.ENDC

def blue(text):
	return bcolors.OKBLUE + str(text) + bcolors.ENDC

def green(text):
	return bcolors.OKGREEN + str(text) + bcolors.ENDC

def warn(text):
	return bcolors.WARNING + str(text) + bcolors.ENDC
def yellow(text):
	return bcolors.WARNING + str(text) + bcolors.ENDC

def fail(text):
	return bcolors.FAIL + str(text) + bcolors.ENDC
def red(text):
	return bcolors.FAIL + str(text) + bcolors.ENDC

def bold(text):
	return bcolors.BOLD + str(text) + bcolors.ENDC

def underline(text):
	return bcolors.UNDERLINE + str(text) + bcolors.ENDC


def colorize_logging():
	# DEBUG: Normal Green
	logging.addLevelName( logging.DEBUG, "\033[92m%s\033[0m" % logging.getLevelName(logging.DEBUG))
	# INFO: Normal Blue
	logging.addLevelName( logging.INFO, "\033[94m%s\033[0m" % logging.getLevelName(logging.INFO))
	# WARNING: Bold Red
	logging.addLevelName( logging.WARNING, "\033[1;31m%s\033[1;0m" % logging.getLevelName(logging.WARNING))
	# ERROR: Bold Red background
	logging.addLevelName( logging.ERROR, "\033[1;41m%s\033[1;0m" % logging.getLevelName(logging.ERROR))
	# CRITICAL: BOLD Red on White background
	logging.addLevelName( logging.CRITICAL, "\033[1;31;47m%s\033[1;0m" % logging.getLevelName(logging.CRITICAL))

def stderr(*message):
	print(*message, file=sys.stderr)

def default_input(message, default):
	result = raw_input(' > {} [{}]: '.format(message, default))
	if not result:
		result = default
	return result

def required_input(message):
	result = None
	while not result:
		result = raw_input(message)
		if result:
			return result
		print(fail(' ! VALUE REQUIRED\n'))

def yes_no_input(message, default='n'):
	valid = {'yes': True, 'y': True, 'ye': True,
			 'no': False, 'n': False}
	while True:
		response = raw_input('{} (y/n): [{}] '.format(message, default))
		if not response:
			return valid[default]
		if response in valid:
			return valid[response]
		else:
			print(fail(" ! Please respond with 'yes' or 'no' (or 'y' or 'n')\n"))

# Systems that require separation processing

# LDAP Configurations
LDAP_ADDR = 'ldaps://ldap.sea.marchex.com:636/'
LDAP_BASEDN = 'ou=users,dc=marchex,dc=com'
LDAP_BINDDN = 'uid={user},ou=users,dc=marchex,dc=com'
LDAP_SF = '(cn={user})'

# RT (Request Tracker) Configuration

RT_URL = 'https://rt.marchex.com/REST/1.0'

# Create an LDAP server object with TLS options
tls_configuration = Tls(validate=ldap3.VALIDATE_NEVER)
server = Server(LDAP_ADDR, use_ssl=True, tls=tls_configuration)


def get_user_input(prompt):
    """Wrapper for input to handle common input scenarios."""
    try:
        return input(prompt).strip()
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Error getting user input: {e}")
        return None


def get_directory_info(user):
    """Query Directory Manager for user alias & manager name."""
    directory_url = f"https://directorymanager.marchex.com/api/user/{user}"
    try:
        response = requests.get(directory_url)
        response.raise_for_status()
        user_data = response.json()
        return user_data.get('alias', 'Unknown'), user_data.get('manager', 'Unknown')
    except Exception as e:
        logging.warning(f"Failed to retrieve Directory Manager info for {user}: {e}")
        return 'Unknown', 'Unknown'


def check_rt_for_access_tickets(user):
    """Check RT (Request Tracker) for past access requests related to this user."""
    logging.info(f"Checking RT for past access requests related to {user}...")
    query = f"Owner = '{user}' AND (Status = 'new' OR Status = 'open')"
    tracker = rt.Rt(RT_URL, RT_USER, RT_PASS)
    if not tracker.login():
        logging.error("Failed to authenticate with RT.")
        return
    try:
        tickets = tracker.search(Queue="SOC", raw_query=query)
        if tickets:
            logging.info(f"User {user} has {len(tickets)} past access tickets in RT.")
            for ticket in tickets:
                logging.info(f"RT Ticket Found: {ticket['id']} - {ticket['Subject']}")
        else:
            logging.info(f"No previous access tickets found in RT for {user}.")
    except Exception as e:
        logging.warning(f"Error checking RT for {user}: {e}")


def check_high_priority_contact_list(user):
    """Check and remove user from High Priority Contact List."""
    if not os.path.exists(HIGH_PRI_FILE):
        logging.warning("High Priority Contact List file not found.")
        return
    try:
        wb = openpyxl.load_workbook(HIGH_PRI_FILE)
        sheet = wb.active
        for row in sheet.iter_rows():
            for cell in row:
                if str(user).lower() in str(cell.value).lower():
                    logging.info(f"Removing {user} from High Priority Contact List.")
                    cell.value = None
                    wb.save(HIGH_PRI_FILE)
                    return
        logging.info(f"{user} not found in High Priority Contact List.")
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Error modifying High Priority Contact List: {e}")


def submit_sev5_ticket_for_TACACS(user):
    """Submit a SEV5 ticket to NetEng for TACACS removal."""
    logging.info(f"Submitting SEV5 ticket for TACACS removal for {user}.")
    
    # Simulated API request
    ticket_payload = {
        "summary": f"SEV5 - Remove TACACS access for {user}",
        "description": f"User {user} requires TACACS access removal as part of separation.",
        "priority": "SEV5",
        "assigned_team": "NetEng"
    }
    try:
        response = requests.post("https://ticketing.marchex.com/api/tickets", json=ticket_payload)
        response.raise_for_status()
        logging.info(f"SEV5 ticket successfully created for TACACS removal: {response.json().get('ticket_id')}")
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Failed to create SEV5 ticket for TACACS: {e}")


def main():
    """ Main function for the separation script. """
    logging.info("########### SEPARATION SCRIPT #############")
    operatorUN = get_user_input("Enter your LDAP username: ")
    operatorPass = getpass.getpass("Enter your LDAP password: ")

    # Gather usernames to be separated
    sepList = get_user_input("Enter LDAP user(s) to be separated (comma-separated): ").split(',')

    # Check if user is a vendor
    while True:
        isVendor = get_user_input("Is this user a vendor? (yes/no): ").lower()
        if isVendor in ('yes', 'no'):
            break
        logging.warning("Invalid input. Please enter 'yes' or 'no'.")

    vendorEmail = None
    if isVendor == "yes":
        if any(sys in ACCESS_LIST for sys in ["PagerDuty", "Microsites"]):
            vendorEmail = get_user_input("Enter vendor email address: ")
        else:
            logging.info("Vendor email not needed for selected systems.")

    # Ask if we are checking or removing access
    while True:
        accessChoice = get_user_input("Would you like to remove all found access or just check access? (Remove/Check): ").lower()
        if accessChoice in ('remove', 'check'):
            break
        logging.warning("Invalid input. Please enter 'Remove' or 'Check'.")
    
    creds = {
        "operatorUN": operatorUN,
        "operatorPass": operatorPass,
        "sepList": sepList,
        "accessChoice": accessChoice,
        "vendorEmail": vendorEmail,
        "MOCK_MODE": MOCK_MODE  # 🟢 Global Mock Mode Toggle CLI Controlled
    }

    try:
        ldp = Connection(server, user=LDAP_BINDDN.format(user=operatorUN), password=operatorPass, auto_bind=True)
    except ldap.INVALID_CREDENTIALS:
        logging.error("LDAP authentication failed. Exiting.")
        return
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Unexpected LDAP error: {e}")
        return
    
    with ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=5) as executor:
        executor.map(lambda user: process_user(ldp, user, creds), sepList)

    logging.info(f"####### No further access found for {user} #######")
    
    if MISSING_SCRIPTS:
        logging.warning(f"Missing separation scripts: {', '.join(set(MISSING_SCRIPTS))}")


def process_user(ldp, user, creds):
    """Process separation for an individual user."""
    try:
        logging.info(f"Processing user: {user}")
        if "MOCK_MODE" in creds and creds["MOCK_MODE"]:
            logging.info(f"[MOCK] Simulating access removal for {user}.")
            return
        
        check_rt_for_access_tickets(user)
        if ldapQuery(ldp, user):
            checkAccess(user, creds)
        check_high_priority_contact_list(user)
        if "TACACS" in ACCESS_LIST:
            submit_sev5_ticket_for_TACACS(user)
        logging.info(f"####### No further access found for {user} #######")
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Error processing user {user}: {e}")


def ldapQuery(ldp, user):
    """Check if user exists in LDAP."""
    logging.info(f"Checking LDAP access for {user}...")

    try:
        ldp.search(LDAP_BASEDN, f"(cn={user})", ldap3.SUBTREE)
        if not ldp.entries:
            logging.warning(f"User {user} not found in LDAP.")
            return False
        return True
    except ldap3.LDAPException as e:
        logging.error(f"LDAP query failed for {user}: {e}")
        return False


def checkAccess(user, creds):
    """Run access removal scripts."""
    global MISSING_SCRIPTS 
    logging.info(f"Checking access for {user}...")
    for system in ACCESS_LIST:
        try:
            sep_module = __import__(f"separations.{system.lower()}", fromlist=[""])
            sep_module.main(user, creds)
        except ImportError:
            MISSING_SCRIPTS.append(system)
        except Exception as e:
            logging.error(f"Error running {system} separation: {e}")


if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

import logging
import getpass
import ldap3 as ldap
import sys
import os
import ssl
import requests
import openpyxl
import json

sys.path.append(os.path.abspath("C:/Users/kboller/Desktop/socbot/socbot-dev/lib/python"))

import utils 
import rt_marchex as rt
from concurrent.futures import ThreadPoolExecutor
from ldap3 import Server, Connection, Tls, ALL


# Setup logging     
logging.basicConfig(
    format='%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s',
    level=logging.INFO
)

# 🟢 Mock Mode (Secret Backdoor Enabled)
MOCK_MODE = False  # Default is OFF

# 🔐 Secret Backdoor Command (Toggle Mock Mode)
secret_command = getpass.getpass("Enter command or press Enter to continue: ").strip().lower()
if secret_command == "testmode":
    MOCK_MODE = True
    logging.warning("🚀 Test Mode Activated: Mock Mode is ENABLED.")
else:
    logging.info("Running in LIVE Mode.")

# Systems that require separation processing
SYSTEMS_CATALOG = {
    "AdTrack": True,
    "AFR": True,
    "Auth0": True,
    "Avenger": True,
    "AWS": True,
    "ADO": True,
    "AzurePortal": True,
    "CallScoring": True,
    "Chef": True,
    "Cuttlefish": True,
    "EmailAccess": True,
    "Engage": True,
    "EquityEdge_GreatPlains": True,
    "GitHub": True,
    "Grafana": True,
    "Ipplan": True,
    "JIRA": True,
    "Marchex.io": True,
    "MI5": True,
    "Microsites": True,
    "NewRelic": True,
    "Nexus": True,
    "NimUI": True,
    "NISMaps": True,
    "OpenVPN": True,
    "PagerDuty": True,
    "Pulley": True,
    "Postman": True,
    "RT": True, # Checking RT for past access requests
    "Slack": True,
    "MarketingEdge": True,
    "Sendgrid": True,
    "Sentry": True,
    "Snowflake": True,
    "TACACS": True,  # Needs special handling (SEV5 ticket)
    "Wallace": True,
    "XMSHammer": True
}

ACCESS_LIST = [system for system, enabled in SYSTEMS_CATALOG.items() if enabled]
MISSING_SCRIPTS = []

# LDAP Configurations
LDAP_ADDR = 'ldaps://ldap.sea.marchex.com:636/'
LDAP_BASEDN = 'ou=users,dc=marchex,dc=com'
LDAP_BINDDN = 'uid={user},ou=users,dc=marchex,dc=com'
LDAP_SF = '(cn={user})'

# RT (Request Tracker) Configuration
RT_HOST = 'https://rt.marchex.com'
RT_URL = 'https://rt.marchex.com/REST/1.0'
RT_USER = "socbot"  # Replace with actual RT user
RT_PASS = "securepass"  # Replace with actual RT password

# High Priority Contact List Location
HIGH_PRI_FILE = r'\\marchex\files\soc\Emergency\High Priority Contact List\NOCHighPriorityContactList1.xlsx'


# Create an LDAP server object with TLS options
tls_configuration = Tls(validate=ssl.CERT_NONE)
server = Server(LDAP_ADDR, use_ssl=True, tls=tls_configuration)


def get_user_input(prompt):
    """Wrapper for input to handle common input scenarios."""
    try:
        return input(prompt).strip()
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Error getting user input: {e}")
        return None


def get_directory_info(user):
    """Query Directory Manager for user alias & manager name."""
    directory_url = f"https://directorymanager.marchex.com/api/user/{user}"
    try:
        response = requests.get(directory_url)
        response.raise_for_status()
        user_data = response.json()
        return user_data.get('alias', 'Unknown'), user_data.get('manager', 'Unknown')
    except Exception as e:
        logging.warning(f"Failed to retrieve Directory Manager info for {user}: {e}")
        return 'Unknown', 'Unknown'


def check_rt_for_access_tickets(user):
    """Check RT (Request Tracker) for past access requests related to this user."""
    logging.info(f"Checking RT for past access requests related to {user}...")
    query = f"Owner = '{user}' AND (Status = 'new' OR Status = 'open')"
    tracker = rt.Rt(RT_URL, RT_USER, RT_PASS)
    if not tracker.login():
        logging.error("Failed to authenticate with RT.")
        return
    try:
        tickets = tracker.search(Queue="SOC", raw_query=query)
        if tickets:
            logging.info(f"User {user} has {len(tickets)} past access tickets in RT.")
            for ticket in tickets:
                logging.info(f"RT Ticket Found: {ticket['id']} - {ticket['Subject']}")
        else:
            logging.info(f"No previous access tickets found in RT for {user}.")
    except Exception as e:
        logging.warning(f"Error checking RT for {user}: {e}")


def check_high_priority_contact_list(user):
    """Check and remove user from High Priority Contact List."""
    if not os.path.exists(HIGH_PRI_FILE):
        logging.warning("High Priority Contact List file not found.")
        return
    try:
        wb = openpyxl.load_workbook(HIGH_PRI_FILE)
        sheet = wb.active
        for row in sheet.iter_rows():
            for cell in row:
                if str(user).lower() in str(cell.value).lower():
                    logging.info(f"Removing {user} from High Priority Contact List.")
                    cell.value = None
                    wb.save(HIGH_PRI_FILE)
                    return
        logging.info(f"{user} not found in High Priority Contact List.")
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Error modifying High Priority Contact List: {e}")


def submit_sev5_ticket_for_TACACS(user):
    """Submit a SEV5 ticket to NetEng for TACACS removal."""
    logging.info(f"Submitting SEV5 ticket for TACACS removal for {user}.")
    
    # Simulated API request
    ticket_payload = {
        "summary": f"SEV5 - Remove TACACS access for {user}",
        "description": f"User {user} requires TACACS access removal as part of separation.",
        "priority": "SEV5",
        "assigned_team": "NetEng"
    }
    try:
        response = requests.post("https://ticketing.marchex.com/api/tickets", json=ticket_payload)
        response.raise_for_status()
        logging.info(f"SEV5 ticket successfully created for TACACS removal: {response.json().get('ticket_id')}")
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Failed to create SEV5 ticket for TACACS: {e}")


def main():
    """ Main function for the separation script. """
    logging.info("########### SEPARATION SCRIPT #############")
    operatorUN = get_user_input("Enter your LDAP username: ")
    operatorPass = getpass.getpass("Enter your LDAP password: ")

    # Gather usernames to be separated
    sepList = get_user_input("Enter LDAP user(s) to be separated (comma-separated): ").split(',')

    # Check if user is a vendor
    while True:
        isVendor = get_user_input("Is this user a vendor? (yes/no): ").lower()
        if isVendor in ('yes', 'no'):
            break
        logging.warning("Invalid input. Please enter 'yes' or 'no'.")

    vendorEmail = None
    if isVendor == "yes":
        if any(sys in ACCESS_LIST for sys in ["PagerDuty", "Microsites"]):
            vendorEmail = get_user_input("Enter vendor email address: ")
        else:
            logging.info("Vendor email not needed for selected systems.")

    # Ask if we are checking or removing access
    while True:
        accessChoice = get_user_input("Would you like to remove all found access or just check access? (Remove/Check): ").lower()
        if accessChoice in ('remove', 'check'):
            break
        logging.warning("Invalid input. Please enter 'Remove' or 'Check'.")
    
    creds = {
        "operatorUN": operatorUN,
        "operatorPass": operatorPass,
        "sepList": sepList,
        "accessChoice": accessChoice,
        "vendorEmail": vendorEmail,
        "MOCK_MODE": MOCK_MODE  # 🟢 Global Mock Mode Toggle CLI Controlled
    }

    try:
        ldp = Connection(server, user=LDAP_BINDDN.format(user=operatorUN), password=operatorPass, auto_bind=True)
    except ldap.INVALID_CREDENTIALS:
        logging.error("LDAP authentication failed. Exiting.")
        return
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Unexpected LDAP error: {e}")
        return
    
    with ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=5) as executor:
        executor.map(lambda user: process_user(ldp, user, creds), sepList)

    logging.info(f"####### No further access found for {user} #######")
    
    if MISSING_SCRIPTS:
        logging.warning(f"Missing separation scripts: {', '.join(set(MISSING_SCRIPTS))}")


def process_user(ldp, user, creds):
    """Process separation for an individual user."""
    try:
        logging.info(f"Processing user: {user}")
        if "MOCK_MODE" in creds and creds["MOCK_MODE"]:
            logging.info(f"[MOCK] Simulating access removal for {user}.")
            return
        
        check_rt_for_access_tickets(user)
        if ldapQuery(ldp, user):
            checkAccess(user, creds)
        check_high_priority_contact_list(user)
        if "TACACS" in ACCESS_LIST:
            submit_sev5_ticket_for_TACACS(user)
        logging.info(f"####### No further access found for {user} #######")
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Error processing user {user}: {e}")


def ldapQuery(ldp, user):
    """Check if user exists in LDAP."""
    logging.info(f"Checking LDAP access for {user}...")

    try:
        ldp.search(LDAP_BASEDN, f"(cn={user})", ldap.SUBTREE)
        if not ldp.entries:
            logging.warning(f"User {user} not found in LDAP.")
            return False
        return True
    except ldap.LDAPException as e:
        logging.error(f"LDAP query failed for {user}: {e}")
        return False


def checkAccess(user, creds):
    """Run access removal scripts."""
    global MISSING_SCRIPTS 
    logging.info(f"Checking access for {user}...")
    for system in ACCESS_LIST:
        try:
            sep_module = __import__(f"separations.{system.lower()}", fromlist=[""])
            sep_module.main(user, creds)
        except ImportError:
            MISSING_SCRIPTS.append(system)
        except Exception as e:
            logging.error(f"Error running {system} separation: {e}")


if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

        "MOCK_MODE": MOCK_MODE  # 🟢 Global Mock Mode Toggle CLI Controlled
    }

    try:
        ldp = Connection(server, user=LDAP_BINDDN.format(user=operatorUN), password=operatorPass, auto_bind=True)
    except LDAPBindError:
        logging.error("❌ LDAP authentication failed. Invalid username or password.")
        return
    except Exception as e:

    with ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=5) as executor:
        executor.map(lambda user: process_user(ldp, user, creds), sepList)

def process_user(ldp, user, creds):
    """Process separation for an individual user."""
    try:
        logging.info(f"Processing user: {user}")
        if "MOCK_MODE" in creds and creds["MOCK_MODE"]:
            logging.info(f"[MOCK] Simulating access removal for {user}.")
            return

        logging.info(f"####### No further access found for {user} #######")
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Error processing user {user}: {e}")

    """Check if user exists in LDAP."""
    logging.info(f"Checking LDAP access for {user}...")

    try:
        ldp.search(LDAP_BASEDN, f"(cn={user})", ldap.SUBTREE)
        if not ldp.entries:
            logging.warning(f"User {user} not found in LDAP.")
            return False
        return True
    except ldap.LDAPException as e:
        logging.error(f"LDAP query failed for {user}: {e}")
        return False

    main()

import logging
import getpass
import ldap3 as ldap
import sys
import os
import ssl
import requests

import json

sys.path.append(os.path.abspath("C:/Users/kboller/Desktop/socbot/socbot-dev/lib/python"))

import utils 
import rt_marchex as rt
from concurrent.futures import ThreadPoolExecutor
from ldap3 import Server, Connection, Tls, ALL
from ldap3.core.exceptions import LDAPBindError


# Setup logging     
logging.basicConfig(
    format='%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s',
    level=logging.INFO
)

# 🟢 Mock Mode (Secret Backdoor Enabled)
MOCK_MODE = False  # Default is OFF

# 🔐 Secret Backdoor Command (Toggle Mock Mode)
secret_command = getpass.getpass("Enter command or press Enter to continue: ").strip().lower()
if secret_command == "testmode":
    MOCK_MODE = True
    logging.warning("🚀 Test Mode Activated: Mock Mode is ENABLED.")
else:
    logging.info("Running in LIVE Mode.")

# Systems that require separation processing
SYSTEMS_CATALOG = {
    "AdTrack": True,
    "AFR": True,
    "Auth0": True,
    "Avenger": True,
    "AWS": True,

    "Wallace": True,

ACCESS_LIST = [system for system, enabled in SYSTEMS_CATALOG.items() if enabled]
MISSING_SCRIPTS = []

# LDAP Configurations
LDAP_HOST = 'ldap.sea.marchex.com'
LDAP_PORT = 636
LDAP_BASEDN = 'ou=users,dc=marchex,dc=com'
LDAP_BINDDN = 'uid={user},ou=users,dc=marchex,dc=com'
LDAP_SF = '(cn={user})'

# RT (Request Tracker) Configuration
RT_HOST = 'https://rt.marchex.com'
RT_URL = 'https://rt.marchex.com/REST/1.0'
RT_USER = "socbot"  # Replace with actual RT user
RT_PASS = "securepass"  # Replace with actual RT password

# High Priority Contact List Location
HIGH_PRI_FILE = r'\\marchex\files\soc\Emergency\High Priority Contact List\NOCHighPriorityContactList1.xlsx'


try:
    server = Server(LDAP_HOST, port=LDAP_PORT, use_ssl=True)
    logging.info(f"✅ Successfully connected to LDAP server: {LDAP_HOST}:{LDAP_PORT}")
except Exception as e:
    logging.error(f"❌ Failed to connect to LDAP server: {e}")
    sys.exit(1)


def get_user_input(prompt):
    """Wrapper for input to handle common input scenarios."""
    try:
        return input(prompt).strip()
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Error getting user input: {e}")
        return None


def get_directory_info(user):
    """Query Directory Manager for user alias & manager name."""
    directory_url = f"https://directorymanager.marchex.com/api/user/{user}"
    try:
        response = requests.get(directory_url)
        response.raise_for_status()
        user_data = response.json()
        return user_data.get('alias', 'Unknown'), user_data.get('manager', 'Unknown')
    except Exception as e:
        logging.warning(f"Failed to retrieve Directory Manager info for {user}: {e}")
        return 'Unknown', 'Unknown'


def check_rt_for_access_tickets(user):
    """Check RT (Request Tracker) for past access requests related to this user."""
    logging.info(f"Checking RT for past access requests related to {user}...")
    query = f"Owner = '{user}' AND (Status = 'new' OR Status = 'open')"
    tracker = rt.Rt(RT_URL, RT_USER, RT_PASS)
    if not tracker.login():
        logging.error("Failed to authenticate with RT.")
        return
    try:
        tickets = tracker.search(Queue="SOC", raw_query=query)
        if tickets:
            logging.info(f"User {user} has {len(tickets)} past access tickets in RT.")
            for ticket in tickets:
                logging.info(f"RT Ticket Found: {ticket['id']} - {ticket['Subject']}")
        else:
            logging.info(f"No previous access tickets found in RT for {user}.")
    except Exception as e:
        logging.warning(f"Error checking RT for {user}: {e}")


def check_high_priority_contact_list(user):
    """Check and remove user from High Priority Contact List."""
    if not os.path.exists(HIGH_PRI_FILE):
        logging.warning("High Priority Contact List file not found.")
        return
    try:
        wb = openpyxl.load_workbook(HIGH_PRI_FILE)
        sheet = wb.active
        for row in sheet.iter_rows():
            for cell in row:
                if str(user).lower() in str(cell.value).lower():
                    logging.info(f"Removing {user} from High Priority Contact List.")
                    cell.value = None
                    wb.save(HIGH_PRI_FILE)
                    return
        logging.info(f"{user} not found in High Priority Contact List.")
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Error modifying High Priority Contact List: {e}")


def submit_sev5_ticket_for_TACACS(user):
    """Submit a SEV5 ticket to NetEng for TACACS removal."""
    logging.info(f"Submitting SEV5 ticket for TACACS removal for {user}.")
    
    # Simulated API request
    ticket_payload = {
        "summary": f"SEV5 - Remove TACACS access for {user}",
        "description": f"User {user} requires TACACS access removal as part of separation.",
        "priority": "SEV5",
        "assigned_team": "NetEng"
    }
    try:
        response = requests.post("https://ticketing.marchex.com/api/tickets", json=ticket_payload)
        response.raise_for_status()
        logging.info(f"SEV5 ticket successfully created for TACACS removal: {response.json().get('ticket_id')}")
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Failed to create SEV5 ticket for TACACS: {e}")


def main():
    """ Main function for the separation script. """
    logging.info("########### SEPARATION SCRIPT #############")
    operatorUN = get_user_input("Enter your LDAP username: ")
    operatorPass = getpass.getpass("Enter your LDAP password: ")

    # Gather usernames to be separated
    sepList = get_user_input("Enter LDAP user(s) to be separated (comma-separated): ").split(',')

    # Check if user is a vendor
    while True:
        isVendor = get_user_input("Is this user a vendor? (yes/no): ").lower()
        if isVendor in ('yes', 'no'):
            break
        logging.warning("Invalid input. Please enter 'yes' or 'no'.")

    vendorEmail = None
    if isVendor == "yes":
        if any(sys in ACCESS_LIST for sys in ["PagerDuty", "Microsites"]):
            vendorEmail = get_user_input("Enter vendor email address: ")
        else:
            logging.info("Vendor email not needed for selected systems.")

    # Ask if we are checking or removing access
    while True:
        accessChoice = get_user_input("Would you like to remove all found access or just check access? (Remove/Check): ").lower()
        if accessChoice in ('remove', 'check'):
            break
        logging.warning("Invalid input. Please enter 'Remove' or 'Check'.")
    
    creds = {
        "operatorUN": operatorUN,
        "operatorPass": operatorPass,
        "sepList": sepList,
        "accessChoice": accessChoice,
        "vendorEmail": vendorEmail,
        "MOCK_MODE": MOCK_MODE  # 🟢 Global Mock Mode Toggle CLI Controlled
    }

    try:
        ldp = Connection(server, user=LDAP_BINDDN.format(user=operatorUN), password=operatorPass, auto_bind=True)
    except LDAPBindError:
        logging.error("❌ LDAP authentication failed. Invalid username or password.")
        return
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"⚠️ Unexpected LDAP error: {e}")
        return
    
    with ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=5) as executor:
        executor.map(lambda user: process_user(ldp, user, creds), sepList)

    logging.info(f"####### No further access found for {user} #######")
    
    if MISSING_SCRIPTS:
        logging.warning(f"Missing separation scripts: {', '.join(set(MISSING_SCRIPTS))}")


def process_user(ldp, user, creds):
    """Process separation for an individual user."""
    try:
        logging.info(f"Processing user: {user}")
        if "MOCK_MODE" in creds and creds["MOCK_MODE"]:
            logging.info(f"[MOCK] Simulating access removal for {user}.")
            return
        
        check_rt_for_access_tickets(user)
        if ldapQuery(ldp, user):
            checkAccess(user, creds)
        check_high_priority_contact_list(user)
        if "TACACS" in ACCESS_LIST:
            submit_sev5_ticket_for_TACACS(user)
        logging.info(f"####### No further access found for {user} #######")
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Error processing user {user}: {e}")


def ldapQuery(ldp, user):
    """Check if user exists in LDAP."""
    logging.info(f"Checking LDAP access for {user}...")

    try:
        ldp.search(LDAP_BASEDN, f"(cn={user})", ldap.SUBTREE)
        if not ldp.entries:
            logging.warning(f"User {user} not found in LDAP.")
            return False
        return True
    except ldap.LDAPException as e:
        logging.error(f"LDAP query failed for {user}: {e}")
        return False


def checkAccess(user, creds):
    """Run access removal scripts."""
    global MISSING_SCRIPTS 
    logging.info(f"Checking access for {user}...")
    for system in ACCESS_LIST:
        try:
            sep_module = __import__(f"separations.{system.lower()}", fromlist=[""])
            sep_module.main(user, creds)
        except ImportError:
            MISSING_SCRIPTS.append(system)
        except Exception as e:
            logging.error(f"Error running {system} separation: {e}")


if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
